介休 (出生地)

-----title
阆中
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='64757800b7e2408ba6021caeccffbe02_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("64757800b7e2408ba6021caeccffbe02");'><span id='64757800b7e2408ba6021caeccffbe02_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1019')">1017-1019年</a>，12-14岁</div><div id='64757800b7e2408ba6021caeccffbe02' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　送龙昌期归陵阳。作品：《送龙昌期先生归蜀序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_1160303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送龙昌期先生归蜀序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1018年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160303")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160303'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160303'>井络之区，炳岷嶓之秀，是以异人间出，俊乂凤集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160303_comment'></div>长卿导清源于前，子云扇芳尘于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160303_comment'></div>历此而降，鸿硕颇繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160303_comment'></div>然或以浮诞相高，流荡忘返者，十室而九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160303_comment'></div>其励志坟典，游心圣奥，盖亦鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160303_comment'></div>达斯道者，其惟武陵先生龙君乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160303_comment'></div>先生，陵阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160303_comment'></div>藏器于身，不交世务，闭关却扫，开卷自得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160303_comment'></div>著书数万言，穷经二十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160303_comment'></div>浮英华而沈道德，先周孔而后黄老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160303_comment'></div>杨墨塞路，辞而辟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160303_comment'></div>名动士林，高视两蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160303_comment'></div>遂不远万里，上书公车，累叫天阍，久而不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160303_comment'></div>乃喟然叹曰：「道未亨矣，吾其归欤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160303_comment'></div>因假道阆川，获挹眉宇，是故经籍奥义，得以咨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160303_comment'></div>或撞钟待问，则多多而益办；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160303_comment'></div>或盱衡高论，则亹亹而来逼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160303_comment'></div>缙绅之流，靡不推服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160303_comment'></div>且以堂有慈亲，贫乏甘旨，遽轸《南陔》之思，遂谋西辕之役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160303_comment'></div>掺执之际，乌得默然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160303_comment'></div>因举酒而言曰：夫古之人患于不明经也，茍明一经，取朱紫若拾地芥尔，何况于先生之经明行修乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160303_comment'></div>但老氏所谓大器晚成也尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160303_comment'></div>行矣自爱，先生其志于斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160303_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1160303'>藏器于身，不涉世务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160303_comment'></div>闭关著书，开卷独得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160303_comment'></div>杨墨塞路，辞而辟之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160303_comment'></div>名动士林，高视两蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160303_comment'></div>不远万里，累诣公车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160303_comment'></div>上书自荐，寄食上都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160303_comment'></div>久而不报，遂复喟然叹曰：「命未泰矣，吾其归欤」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160303_comment'></div>因假道阆川，获挹眉宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160303_comment'></div>仰碧鸡之雄辩，鄙吝顿祛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160303_comment'></div>听黄马之剧谈，座客皆靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160303_comment'></div>方以陟岵在念，戒涂有期，送君河梁，聊复赠言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160303_comment'></div>勉哉是行，以保远大。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1160303'></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1160303_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　求学备考。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c644d37dae6d4d24b1631964ee70018a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c644d37dae6d4d24b1631964ee70018a");'><span id='c644d37dae6d4d24b1631964ee70018a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1026')">1023-1026年</a>，18-21岁</div><div id='c644d37dae6d4d24b1631964ee70018a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　送张观赴阙。作品：《送张大丞赴阙序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_1160302' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160302' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160302?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送张太丞赴阙序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1023年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160302")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160302_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160302'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160302'>袁宏曰：帝王之道，莫大于选贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160302_comment'></div>选贤之义，各有其方也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160302_comment'></div>故周有俊造之科，汉有贤良之举，莫不取经国宏材，济民远略，然后授之以职，而使不失其任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160302_comment'></div>膺是选者，寔难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160302_comment'></div>太丞状元禀山岳之灵，蕴经纶之业，才识敏茂，声华籍甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160302_comment'></div>始以大司徒论秀而升于太学，俄以春官氏辨材而扬于王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160302_comment'></div>狗监诵《子虚》之赋，恨不同时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160302_comment'></div>天子览平津之策，迁为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160302_comment'></div>卿士大夫，莫不嘉叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160302_comment'></div>而自策名桂籍，解褐仕路，凡载佐郡，皆有治声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160302_comment'></div>天子嘉其能，而自麟台郎改丞奉常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160302_comment'></div>虽行路之人，悉以庆慰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160302_comment'></div>然缙绅之士咸称其位不充量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160302_comment'></div>方属芝检召贤之日，葵丘代戍之秋，严助已别会稽，贾谊重归宣室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160302_comment'></div>则公之是行也，排金门，升玉堂，固其宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160302_comment'></div>然鸿鹄之志，一举万里，非燕雀之所能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160302_comment'></div>某以忝窥隩隅，获丐馀重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160302_comment'></div>片言之誉，东陵殆侔西山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160302_comment'></div>半面之荣，郑璞仅逾周宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160302_comment'></div>逮兹于迈，岂其无言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160302_comment'></div>踯躅燥吻，聊为之序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1160302_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　德号继明颂。作品：《德号继明颂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1160325' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160325' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160325?labeling=true' target='_blank'>德号继明颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（1023年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160325")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160325_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160325'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160325'>臣闻圆象高明，运四时而不言所利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160325_comment'></div>方祇博厚，载万物而罔矜厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160325_comment'></div>然则藏用显仁，其来尚矣，仰观俯察，无能名焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160325_comment'></div>及乎太古造书，先王画卦，钩赜崇卑之理，范围清浊之原，必也正名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160325_comment'></div>况以乾坤之象，所以昭德配于易简之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160325_comment'></div>圜璧方琮，钦崇之礼遂广；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160325_comment'></div>往图先谍，拟议之文益多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160325_comment'></div>叹凤著隤摧之言，犹龙有清宁之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160325_comment'></div>斯岂陋神明以永称谓，发施贶以伫推崇者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160325_comment'></div>诚以资始之道隆，则非常之名自显；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160325_comment'></div>成物之功博，则溢美之号攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160325_comment'></div>至若厥初生人，树以司牧，虽越绳契之上，固有筌宰之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160325_comment'></div>必立之名，用纪于德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160325_comment'></div>则大庭、柏皇之氏，栗陆、骊连之君，赫胥、昊英联车而继起，尊卢、浑沌接武而互兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160325_comment'></div>申史阙之寡闻，尚概举而疏略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160325_comment'></div>春皇启运，帝魁在辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160325_comment'></div>云师、土德之精，凤纪、金天之历，参于天地，炳若丹青，莫不本嘉瑞以建官，因盛德以著号，弥上世而夐出，亘来籍而罕俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160325_comment'></div>颛顼、高辛，陶尧、虞舜，揖让而治，具存传圣之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160325_comment'></div>损益可知，兼袭建邦之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160325_comment'></div>三王而下，两汉已还，虽积德以成王，率因土而命氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160325_comment'></div>祖功宗德，观七庙以廑存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160325_comment'></div>茂实英声，去二《典》而愈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160325_comment'></div>是知德号地号，皇哉唐哉，非炎宋之嗣兴，信兼之者鲜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160325_comment'></div>洪惟太祖皇帝，禀天皇之精气，基唐侯之创封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160325_comment'></div>静渊有谋，爰膺五胜之箓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160325_comment'></div>神武不杀，讵烦三战之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160325_comment'></div>狱讼攸归，民灵允属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160325_comment'></div>五让难推于天历，六飞肇正于宸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160325_comment'></div>丹鱼之祥，罄鳞宗而渊跃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160325_comment'></div>朱草之瑞，旅荚物以海渟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160325_comment'></div>皆所以协火德之景光，表炎灵之丕运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160325_comment'></div>太宗皇帝嗣显离照，绍熙宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160325_comment'></div>徂征不庭，削诸侯之髋髀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160325_comment'></div>高拱无事，坐合宫之蟺蜎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160325_comment'></div>虎包不试于五兵，鱼梦荐登于四釜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160325_comment'></div>广详延之路，焕乎有文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160325_comment'></div>辟箴诵之涂，变而至道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160325_comment'></div>真宗皇帝握元枢而观妙，执大象以司民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160325_comment'></div>文物葳蕤，逾武宣制作之盛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160325_comment'></div>轨迹夷易，轶成康勤俭之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160325_comment'></div>象译遝臻，边鄙不耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160325_comment'></div>于是博采处士之议，曲询樵夫之谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160325_comment'></div>刻石纪功，辗无怀之远迹；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1160325_comment'></div>奉符行事，迈元封之上仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1160325_comment'></div>是故得万国之欢心，尽百王之能事者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1160325_comment'></div>皇上天资敦敏，日慎温恭，灵承三后之基，绍绎九功之叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1160325_comment'></div>顺稽古道，惠绥庶氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1160325_comment'></div>孝爱尽于尧门，节俭刑于禹室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1160325_comment'></div>始谋于庙，宫邻咸庆于乃欢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1160325_comment'></div>其智如神，荒憬具瞻于惟睿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1160325_comment'></div>风行桂海，化渐冰天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1160325_comment'></div>鲸津底贡以率宾，月竁奉琛而来享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1160325_comment'></div>书文车轨，遐迩以混同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1160325_comment'></div>乾符坤珍，升降而沕潏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1160325_comment'></div>于时股肱三事，岳牧庶邦，越雍泮之诸生，迄胶庠之群老，绀宇丹房之士，文身辨发之酋，累伏当涂，愿上徽号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1160325_comment'></div>上犹懔然驭朽，惕若乘奔，坚持德柄之谦，俾断公车之奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1160325_comment'></div>群心益固，得请为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1160325_comment'></div>日簉南端之前，罔虞北垒之系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1160325_comment'></div>皇上以重烦台弼，俯徇黔黎，尚依违而积时，方僶俛而从欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1160325_comment'></div>先是，礼官错事，将陈报本之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1160325_comment'></div>委粟增坛，肇举因高之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1160325_comment'></div>会兹勤请，颇迩严禋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1160325_comment'></div>俾竣事于圜丘，甫受册于路寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1160325_comment'></div>仲冬初吉，太宰前诹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1160325_comment'></div>祲仪象物而陈，旧礼不戒而具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1160325_comment'></div>天子乃凝虑蠖濩，逆釐神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1160325_comment'></div>一之日祗见于琳宫，二之日昭告于祖庙，三之日，乃备法驾，将臻夫泰坛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1160325_comment'></div>摄提运衡，风后参乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1160325_comment'></div>招摇炜烨，上纪于旌常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1160325_comment'></div>堪舆奋撝，中静于关轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1160325_comment'></div>及夫郊之夕也，歌大吕，舞云门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1160325_comment'></div>百神受职以降康，四圭有邸而登荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1160325_comment'></div>惟圣飨帝，稽戴《礼》而有光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1160325_comment'></div>惟辟奉天，鉴周《书》而无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1160325_comment'></div>瘗祀云毕，乘舆乃旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1160325_comment'></div>御员阙之嶕峣，发大号以涣汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1160325_comment'></div>纆校悉原于滞系，粲薪咸释于弛刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1160325_comment'></div>曾未踰时，协气充于上下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1160325_comment'></div>固不旋踵，欢声动于华夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1160325_comment'></div>既而回六尺之斗车，正九筵之斧座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1160325_comment'></div>百僚师师以就列，多士济济以盈庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1160325_comment'></div>胪传甫终，宝册遂上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1160325_comment'></div>未央前殿，方蒇于鸿仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1160325_comment'></div>兴庆内朝，先崇于大号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1160325_comment'></div>大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1160325_comment'></div>事地之礼著矣，承乾之道光矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1160325_comment'></div>恢三雍之上仪，监二代以增郁，圣文也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1160325_comment'></div>兼七德以禁暴，罄八荒而畏威，睿武也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1160325_comment'></div>御众以宽，临下有赫，仁明也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1160325_comment'></div>继志于外，承颜于中，孝德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1160325_comment'></div>宜乎绍列圣之丕休，举邃古之坠典，钟八九之遐武，兼三五之懿称者尔！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1160325_comment'></div>臣跂仰德辉，亲逢圣旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1160325_comment'></div>濡化偶从于学版，载涂窃效于髫歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1160325_comment'></div>穆如清风，敢冀先臣之式；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1160325_comment'></div>叹之不足，愿续游童之谣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1160325_comment'></div>谨上颂曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_95_1160325'>厥初生民，树以司牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1160325_comment'></div>三皇继轸，五帝联毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1160325_comment'></div>民淳世质，仁洽道丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1160325_comment'></div>罄地作主，与天比崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1160325_comment'></div>德号地号，大道常道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1160325_comment'></div>腾茂飞英，绵穹浃昊，三王而后，两汉已还，继之者鲜，行之惟艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1160325_comment'></div>皇矣帝宋，绍天阐绎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1160325_comment'></div>德焕往图，道光前辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1160325_comment'></div>赫赫太祖，巍巍圣功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1160325_comment'></div>龙兴雷泽，凤起丰宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1160325_comment'></div>拓世贻统，图大宅中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1160325_comment'></div>万邦作乂，四海会同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1160325_comment'></div>于穆太宗，嗣兴舜麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1160325_comment'></div>绍尧之绪，纂禹之服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1160325_comment'></div>大明继照，时文载郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1160325_comment'></div>俗阜刑清，远迩安肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1160325_comment'></div>真皇抚运，大叶重熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1160325_comment'></div>礼乐备具，文物葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1160325_comment'></div>东封岱岳，西祀汾脽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1160325_comment'></div>鸿勋显号，纪石铭彝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1160325_comment'></div>皇上握枢，体元立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1160325_comment'></div>四叶重光，三后贻翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1160325_comment'></div>居域中大，为天下式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1160325_comment'></div>圣文睿武，仁明孝德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1160325_comment'></div>轩崇附宝，唐奉庆都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1160325_comment'></div>内熙坤则，外赞宝图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1160325_comment'></div>慈教广被，仁风诞敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1160325_comment'></div>化亿兆兮归厚，与三五兮同涂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_122_1160325_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1024')">1024年</a>　从孙复学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1025&endYear=1025')">1025年</a>　乡试备考。作品：《圣驾幸太学赋并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_1159913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣驾幸太学赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1025年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159913")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159913'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159913'>国家以寰宇昭泰，仍岁登平，务恢儒风，以章示黎献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159913_comment'></div>皇帝乃备法驾，幸于太学，诏诸儒博士，讲论前典，亲临听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159913_comment'></div>臣获逢休吉之期，恭闻伟盛之事，舞蹈不足，形于赋盳，诚不能述宣上德，褒硈形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159913_comment'></div>姑第樵夫之谈，以协击辕之砋尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159913_comment'></div>词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1159913'>炎宋受命之四叶，皇上御极之三年，九有咸若，六合晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159913_comment'></div>黎庶跻于寿域，文教烛乎冰天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159913_comment'></div>朝无阙政，野无遗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159913_comment'></div>九叙可歌而不紊，百官承式以惟虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159913_comment'></div>刑罚几措，宿澍不愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159913_comment'></div>荒憬清夷而偃革，狙犷訰骝而慕砄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159913_comment'></div>轶漠踰沙，趣藁街者有万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159913_comment'></div>受缨请吏，伏魏观者且千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159913_comment'></div>碧缬文鈛之珍，充仞乎储邸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159913_comment'></div>黑章肉角之兽，驯扰乎郊阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159913_comment'></div>嘉祥麇集，异瑞蝉联；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159913_comment'></div>天降甘露，地出醴泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159913_comment'></div>语鸿烈则超图而益牒，较盛时则绝后而光前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159913_comment'></div>宜乎优游当宁，拱默承乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159913_comment'></div>尚乃惕严衷而驭朽，思嘉谟而涉渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159913_comment'></div>以为治国之道，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1159913", 1159913, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>校学</span>为先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159913_comment'></div>故周氏东胶，往诰之所显；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159913_comment'></div>商人右学，来叶之以传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159913_comment'></div>上既行则民胥效也，君所令则臣必从焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159913_comment'></div>虽平昔之已务，在于今之益宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159913_comment'></div>于是命有司，涓良日，薐仪盛蒇，法驾乃出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159913_comment'></div>天威穆穆，国容皇皇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159913_comment'></div>采章焕烂，和銮铿锵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159913_comment'></div>太史协乐以前导，大丙弭节而徐翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159913_comment'></div>严羽卫，历康庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159913_comment'></div>在浚之都，于国之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159913_comment'></div>神移斗运，乃至于上庠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159913_comment'></div>宸心虔巩，天步高骧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159913_comment'></div>历阶逾阃，睹奥窥堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159913_comment'></div>晞将圣兮有穆，如悉数兮相当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159913_comment'></div>然后趣讲室，明典章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159913_comment'></div>缨谎匝序，巾卷充廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159913_comment'></div>钜儒硕生，奉帙而在列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159913_comment'></div>礼官博士，掌姻而诏王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159913_comment'></div>展东面之殊礼，法西周之旧章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159913_comment'></div>禹听弥审，尧聪益详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159913_comment'></div>夫子善言，由兹而不昧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159913_comment'></div>虞舜好问，于是乎有光<span class='inlineComment2'>（时宣诸直讲，臣讲《鲁论》。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159913_comment'></div>于时闾荶直欢，民灵胥喜，扶老携弱，自遐及迩，莫不连踵而憬集，驾肩而戾止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159913_comment'></div>悉云委于桥门，尽堵观于璧水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159913_comment'></div>粤有华颠胡老，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1159913", 1159913, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>童牙</span>胄子，含经味道之流，方领高冠之士，咸相与而言曰：赫胥远而大庭尚矣，无得称焉，不可详已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159913_comment'></div>自夫五帝而降，三王之始，书契可以传闻，宪章可以追拟，悉皆恢雍泮之基，盛胶庠之阯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159913_comment'></div>四术四教，因是而兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159913_comment'></div>三行三德，所由而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159913_comment'></div>是故醇化丕隆，至德逾美，为万世之所宗，弥亿载而罕比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159913_comment'></div>卯金之后，盖不足纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159913_comment'></div>当涂窘蹙，典午沦弛，南取岛夷之讥，北贻索虏之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159913_comment'></div>干戈于是日寻，俎豆以之中圮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159913_comment'></div>咸不永于卜世，但胥循于覆轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159913_comment'></div>逮乎有唐，皇维诞张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159913_comment'></div>五室之仪兮绝而复嗣，四郊之制兮抑而复扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159913_comment'></div>置序于术，建塾于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159913_comment'></div>家知礼让，民用和康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159913_comment'></div>所以卜年久而享国长，号治古而振懿纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159913_comment'></div>朱石之际，蛙声闰位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159913_comment'></div>覆亡则曾不暇给，学校则诚非拟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159913_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159913_comment'></div>大道不可以终否，斯文不可以久坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159913_comment'></div>故昊天命我太祖，扫除僭伪，俾万方无坠炭之劳，百姓有息肩之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159913_comment'></div>三后继明，百祥还至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159913_comment'></div>展云岱之鸿仪，绍元封之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159913_comment'></div>盛德大业，固无与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159913_comment'></div>今我皇上克奉先烈，夤绍庆基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159913_comment'></div>体元则大，累洽重熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159913_comment'></div>将使儒风寝盛，文教日滋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159913_comment'></div>故乘舆亲视于学，俾亿丑预觇其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159913_comment'></div>足鄙元鼎之间，屡有甘泉之幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159913_comment'></div>堪讥延熹之际，惟尚濯龙之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159913_comment'></div>夫然，则三代之风必能缓步而越矣，两汉之盛岂可并日而论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159913_comment'></div>伟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159913_comment'></div>轨迹夷易，文物葳蕤，信千载而一时<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159913_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1159913'>第：《国朝二百家名贤文粹》作「采」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1159913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159913'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_74_1159913_0'>⑴ 《文潞公文集》卷一，明嘉靖五年王溱刻本。又见《国朝二百家名贤文粹》卷一七六，《历代赋汇》卷五七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159913_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　乡试中举。<br /></div>
-----end

<div class='label1' id='f63877125ba44f9c87040dfb72c9f56e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f63877125ba44f9c87040dfb72c9f56e");'><span id='f63877125ba44f9c87040dfb72c9f56e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1027')">1026-1027年</a>，21-22岁</div><div id='f63877125ba44f9c87040dfb72c9f56e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　作诗赠包拯。作品：《寄友人包兼济拯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_494767' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494767' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494767?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄友人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>包兼济拯<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作极，据四库本改）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1026年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494767")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494767_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494767_0'>① 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494767'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494767'>缔交何止号如龙，发箧畴年绛帐同。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494767'>方领聚游多雅致，幅巾嘉论有清风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494767'>名高阙里二三子，学继台城百六公<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：每策事，则生之条疏常多。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494767'>别后愈知琨气大，可能持久在江东<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：生惠诗有枕戈待旦之句。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494767_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494767'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494767_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　从史炤学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　为诗呈友人。作品：《诏开礼闱偶作呈诸友》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_494776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494776?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诏开礼闱偶作呈诸友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494776")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494776'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494776'>星弧首辟群英彀，天毕初张众目罗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494776'>汉傅<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作传）</span>仍闻求泛驾，周明何止育菁莪。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494776'>碧纱已有蓬山籍，绿李将分桂殿科。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494776'>全伏阿香推毂力，九门三月化陶梭。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494776_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494776'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494776_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　参加省试。作品：《省试诸侯春入贡赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一。）</span>《省试青圭礼东方赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一。）</span>《省试蒲车诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span>《天圣五年春省试献羔开冰》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_1159915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省试诸侯春入贡赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（天下侯国，春入方物。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159915")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159915'>圣启洪绪，君临溥天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159915_comment'></div>侯国之辨方有要，王春之入贡昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159915_comment'></div>列爵正仪，谨奉藩而立制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159915_comment'></div>建宣协序，致任土以居先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159915_comment'></div>稽芳载于礼经，仰徽名于帝者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159915_comment'></div>诸侯述职以无旷，太史奉时而可假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159915_comment'></div>以谓惟王建国，我则叙五等于域中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159915_comment'></div>与物为春，我则任九贡于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159915_comment'></div>徒观夫爵分显父，位列元侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159915_comment'></div>当是时，缇管顺煦和之美，皇祗布发生之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159915_comment'></div>震方之善气睶道，长乐之洪仪聿脩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159915_comment'></div>帝容执瑁以端拱，臣节奉璋而告猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159915_comment'></div>旅弊群方，咸奉舜班之瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159915_comment'></div>充庭万品，皆分禹别之州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159915_comment'></div>但见云布封疆，绮分邦域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159915_comment'></div>故我当岁首以入用，致坤珍而罔忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159915_comment'></div>巽风和令，导传胪之九宾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159915_comment'></div>迟日当阳，丽执玉之万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159915_comment'></div>岂不以辨九土者当贡，首四序者上春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159915_comment'></div>盖将备物宜于时育，助邦光之日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159915_comment'></div>龟纳江沱之锡，磬浮泗水之滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159915_comment'></div>齿革羽毛以偕至，球琳琅籼而毕陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159915_comment'></div>三品良金，于以向履端而执贽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159915_comment'></div>五都奇货，于以当献岁而效珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159915_comment'></div>莫不名物森罗，衣缨杂袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159915_comment'></div>虽厚篚以斯备，在庶邦而允集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159915_comment'></div>此春也霈于皇泽，当邹律之均温；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159915_comment'></div>彼贡也错于地财，异楚茅之不入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159915_comment'></div>彼来宗者夏之礼制，献功者秋之典章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159915_comment'></div>曷若谨岁贡以备物，庆春祺之载阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159915_comment'></div>谅脩时而贡职，乃辨物以居方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159915_comment'></div>备于蕃于宣之仪，皇皇辑瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159915_comment'></div>当载生载育之候，济济来王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159915_comment'></div>故圣人灼叙声明，光昭文物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159915_comment'></div>懿公侯之隆盛，充贡赋之繁蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159915_comment'></div>属后王布和之辰，献国珍而罔咈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1159915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159915'><span class='label'>按：</span>《文潞公文集》卷一。又见《古今图书集成》食货典卷一九四、礼仪典卷二七三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1159915_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1159916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省试青圭礼东方赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（修举春祀，崇尚圭荐。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159916")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159916'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159916'>青惟五色之首，圭乃六器之俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159916_comment'></div>朝日之郊是荐，迎春之礼聿脩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159916_comment'></div>结绿鸿辉，既肃陈于震位；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159916_comment'></div>出蓝美质，将仰奉于神休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159916_comment'></div>原夫谷旦前诹，薐威具举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159916_comment'></div>太史先春而必告，宗伯庀职而攸叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159916_comment'></div>青圭之秘宝爰资，苍帝之明灵可伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159916_comment'></div>谓物生有象，我则锐其质以协宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159916_comment'></div>谓岁起于东，我则莍其方而得所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159916_comment'></div>无瑕可贵，有美惟珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159916_comment'></div>配其色，表盛德之在木；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159916_comment'></div>正其位，彰与物以为春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159916_comment'></div>异彫楮之奇文，琢工奚取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159916_comment'></div>侔剪桐之秀彩，寅位斯陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159916_comment'></div>讵止温其，宁专瑟彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159916_comment'></div>成形自表于瑰器，致用必先于毖祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159916_comment'></div>色斯举矣，俯玉按以相鲜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159916_comment'></div>礼以行之，背金方而致美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159916_comment'></div>岂不以标十德者圭为贵，列四序者春是崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159916_comment'></div>将顺时而展礼，故辨方而在东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159916_comment'></div>葱茜呈恣，禀粹自辉山之石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159916_comment'></div>虔恭致荐，逆矨从解冻之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159916_comment'></div>然则为器之用不同，礼神之功可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159916_comment'></div>名参有邸之义，色异因方之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159916_comment'></div>缥华中秘，生成之气候斯迎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159916_comment'></div>绀䌽外融，温厚之方隅相向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159916_comment'></div>懿哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159916_comment'></div>享兹生物之主，异彼迎秋于西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159916_comment'></div>神感而登礼必答，时和而迓衡不迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159916_comment'></div>用可重焉，且异舜班之瑞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159916_comment'></div>文为贵也，还殊禹锡之圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159916_comment'></div>故得鸿覆降康，太庭锡羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159916_comment'></div>祈民福以昭格，授人时而于变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159916_comment'></div>盖由以方圭总翠之美，欸青郊而可荐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1159916_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_494777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省试蒲车诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494777")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_494777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494777'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494777'>汉祀精禋洁，云亭禅礼殊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494777'>金泥伸秘检，车毂尚编蒲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494777'>越席侔前制，文茵愧后涂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494777'>软轮同致美，规地用难符。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494777'>翠幰芳蕤集，华芝秀彩敷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_494777'>升中仪矩盛，备物壮皇图。<div id='poem_sentence_5_494777_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_494777'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_494777_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_494778' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494778' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494778?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天圣五年春省试献羔开冰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494778")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_494778_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494778'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494778'>国重司<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>寒祭，羔羊献礼陈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494778'>开冰遵旧典，荐庙属昌辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494778'>肥羜方登俎，清壶冀飨神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494778'>虫疑非蚤夏，狐听异先春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494778'>凿凿凝光莹，峨峨发彩新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_494778'>何当比鱼上，从此出迷津。<div id='poem_sentence_5_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_494778'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_494778_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_494778'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_494778_0'>⑴ 原作思，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494778_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　中王尧臣榜进士甲等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　投贽行卷。作品：《温卷启 一》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一○。）</span>《温卷启 二》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一○。）</span>《上知南京晏侍郎启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一○。）</span><div id='poem_1160281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上知南京晏侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1027年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160281")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160281'>伏念逖阻藩房，迅更时籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160281_comment'></div>青纶猥隶，方类于窘拘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160281_comment'></div>绛幰前驺，寖疏于望拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160281_comment'></div>仰瞻荧座，俯郁丹衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160281_comment'></div>恭惟某官雅望冠时，清淡镇俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160281_comment'></div>丕赞景炎之运，懋宣夤亮之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160281_comment'></div>越在夙龄，亲逢圣旦，照蜺光于近署，腾袅足于夷涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160281_comment'></div>代邸方开，早协咨谋之选；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160281_comment'></div>周储肇建，复膺调护之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160281_comment'></div>六飞嗣止于宸居，一德弼成于睿化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160281_comment'></div>民瞻允属，帝简滋隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160281_comment'></div>亟迁内相之荣，旋领中枢之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160281_comment'></div>导扬基命，罄敷将顺之规；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160281_comment'></div>献纳嘉猷，显著弥纶之绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160281_comment'></div>矧平台之近辅，寔兴王之创封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160281_comment'></div>妙简皇僚，谨司留籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160281_comment'></div>契《君陈》之分正，尹兹东郊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160281_comment'></div>绍申伯之于宣，式是南国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160281_comment'></div>行闻圭觐，拱俟节趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160281_comment'></div>入调伊鼎之和，克协傅梅之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160281_comment'></div>举斯舍植，咸切倾祈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160281_comment'></div>某向侍庭闱，幸窥幕府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160281_comment'></div>仰钤斋之秘邃，猥预阶升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160281_comment'></div>晞文席之峻严，曲容隅坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160281_comment'></div>被尊光之委照，宽蒙渎之深尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160281_comment'></div>元冲术参，无补狄笼之阙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160281_comment'></div>曾晰父子，并依丘仞之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160281_comment'></div>铭琢厚恩，铺完充革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160281_comment'></div>未路亟婴于随牒，俶城遽邈于图居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160281_comment'></div>属罕遘于飞邮，仍久乖于奏记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160281_comment'></div>惟增蕊茹，若在薄深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160281_comment'></div>仲吕戒辰，长嬴首序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160281_comment'></div>伏冀仰缘宗社，善保寝兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160281_comment'></div>尹氏秉均，克永维毗之寄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160281_comment'></div>樊侯赋政，益崇明哲之资<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文潞公文集》卷一○。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1160281'></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1160281_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cd6c2a1c504f4d33ba46fafe426f0685_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cd6c2a1c504f4d33ba46fafe426f0685");'><span id='cd6c2a1c504f4d33ba46fafe426f0685_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>，32岁</div><div id='cd6c2a1c504f4d33ba46fafe426f0685' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>张观荐，迁监察御史。作品：《谢陈龙图谏议惠渚宫集启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一○。）</span><div id='poem_1160282' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160282' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160282?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢陈龙图谏议惠渚宫集启<span class='inlineComment2'>（代人作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160282")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160282_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160282'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160282'>伏蒙龙图谏议特赐手书，兼辱贶所著《渚宫新编》二策者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160282_comment'></div>发青泥之封，捧缃袟之卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160282_comment'></div>得璠玙之秘宝，识愧郢人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160282_comment'></div>奏《韶》《武》之大音，听惭俚耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160282_comment'></div>仰蒙恩顾，伏积怔营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160282_comment'></div>窃以楚谣汉风，宗淡雅而尚质；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160282_comment'></div>魏制晋造，惭辩丽以弥文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160282_comment'></div>代祀寖更，情忘逾广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160282_comment'></div>自匪纷披盛藻，管综众流，达三变形似之言，轶七子殊轩之迹，则何以陪金闺之士，宣美于当年，俪平台之踪，贻范于来叶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160282_comment'></div>恭惟某官帝宫甍栋，清庙光辉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160282_comment'></div>怀器望以斡时，厉风猷而轨俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160282_comment'></div>学臻灵匮，该冢璧以采珍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160282_comment'></div>文掞神庭，浃龟沙而流誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160282_comment'></div>亲逢清运，登践紫阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160282_comment'></div>蕴辑宁干翼之才，未施于柄用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160282_comment'></div>□禁密图书之职，式迩于帝晖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160282_comment'></div>所以出观陕服之风，坐镇汉阳之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160282_comment'></div>赖恢崇于远略，永羁制于诸戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160282_comment'></div>顷以掌命西垣，建麾南郡，肃政治以多暇，因纪咏以立言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160282_comment'></div>俄及岁时，积成篇卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160282_comment'></div>垂诸不朽，比岘山而名高；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160282_comment'></div>竞以相传，致洛都之纸贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160282_comment'></div>乃缨绅之圭臬，述作之龟枚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160282_comment'></div>岂谓猥见暗投，俾之穷览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160282_comment'></div>与尺题而狎至，并觉恩荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160282_comment'></div>会群俊以讨论，少明宗致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160282_comment'></div>奏议纳忠而款至，赞颂美德以雍容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160282_comment'></div>序引纪事以精详，风什缘情而妍丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160282_comment'></div>贻之千载，勒成一家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160282_comment'></div>诮陆氏之蓬山，终多芜累；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160282_comment'></div>探张融之玉海，徒美名称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160282_comment'></div>永秘缇缃，用资禀学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160282_comment'></div>某庸虚有素，鉴局无闻，适沐圣风，偶尘官牒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160282_comment'></div>隶曲台而引籍，守微国以于宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160282_comment'></div>虽务勉修，尚多于秕政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160282_comment'></div>唯虞刺举，莫遏于谣言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160282_comment'></div>岂谓龙图忘礼秩之殊，垂提奖之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160282_comment'></div>惠之珍牍，贶以高文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160282_comment'></div>而复列上天朝，敷闻宸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160282_comment'></div>丹雘致饰，期修蟠木之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160282_comment'></div>刻画为功，欲掩倭傀之丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160282_comment'></div>镂肌肤而不灭，摩顶踵以难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160282_comment'></div>伏限城守，不果躬诣门地，卑情伏增悚感依咏、真切知归之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1160282_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>吕夷简荐，转殿中侍御史。作品：《赠清河先生序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_1160304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠清河先生序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160304")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160304_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160304'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160304'>秘校清河君器识淹雅，文行渊懿，学有师法，名高士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160304_comment'></div>游五经之郛，超然深诣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160304_comment'></div>驰六艺之驾，邈矣远至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160304_comment'></div>载丁家艰，未充英彀，濡滞之叹，有识所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160304_comment'></div>天圣初，某始到都下，接诸公游，首得清河君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160304_comment'></div>以文相会，以道相合，行藏游息，相得甚欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160304_comment'></div>未几，予忝荣名，则雾露之润，朋友之益，从可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160304_comment'></div>予仲弟彦若尝师于清河君，授以经义，教之艺文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160304_comment'></div>虽未能传其家法，亦庶几得其一技。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160304_comment'></div>前年春，彦若复忝科级，旋为外诸侯奏□总郡学讲授之职，则清河君之善诲又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160304_comment'></div>今予之季弟彦伯又得师事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160304_comment'></div>一日，彦伯谓予曰：「某依张先生之门垂三年矣，愚冥之识，颇有开悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160304_comment'></div>尝于群弟子之末预闻先生之言：『夫业文者必始于通经，通经者必在乎讲贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160304_comment'></div>故先师曰：学而不讲，是吾忧也』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160304_comment'></div>以是群弟子尝请于先生，愿闻讲习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160304_comment'></div>始则讲《大戴礼》，终则讲《左氏春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160304_comment'></div>论叙精敏，晓譬详明，学者所疑，涣然开释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160304_comment'></div>先生之于五经无不通者，将与群弟子请于先生，愿讲《尚书》一经，以重烦而未白也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160304_comment'></div>予应之曰：「昔与清河君游，亟闻其谈经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160304_comment'></div>于《典》、《谟》、《训》《、诰》、《誓》、《命》之文，《禹贡》、《洪范》之说，尤所精达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160304_comment'></div>余遇有所疑，就而质问，若叩洪钟，大小必应，未尝不虚往而实归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160304_comment'></div>一行为吏，十岁于兹，不闻益友之高论久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160304_comment'></div>今将与尔皆就学焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160304_comment'></div>翌日，躬请于清河君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160304_comment'></div>君亦重违予之勤请，巽辞以从曰：「虞夏商周之书，历代宝以为训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160304_comment'></div>昔尝学于斯文，勉与诸君评之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160304_comment'></div>莫逆于心，喜可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160304_comment'></div>将布席以发论，当闻善而相告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160304_comment'></div>好古博雅、与我同志者，愿闻来学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160304_comment'></div>二月日，太常博士文某白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1160304_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2d31fd3191ad422489675c80dd911726_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2d31fd3191ad422489675c80dd911726");'><span id='2d31fd3191ad422489675c80dd911726_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>，35岁</div><div id='2d31fd3191ad422489675c80dd911726' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　服除，还任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年3月</a>　请战时专将权，严军法。作品：《奏乞主帅便行军令后奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞主帅便行军令后奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159936")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159936'>臣闻穰苴出师，首诛庄贾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159936_comment'></div>孙武教战，先斩爱姬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159936_comment'></div>当事而行，未尝禀命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159936_comment'></div>盖将权不可以不专，军法不可以不峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159936_comment'></div>兹所以攻必克而战必胜者，用法严也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159936_comment'></div>自古有将权不专、军法不峻而行师必胜者，未之闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159936_comment'></div>臣切闻去岁以来，用兵西鄙，或有禁军小尉临阵而先退，边垒偏师望敌而不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159936_comment'></div>而统帅之臣，即时不行军令，悉以事状上闻，皆令邻郡置狱取勘，下法寺详案定刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159936_comment'></div>臣以谓失阃外之制，隳军中之令，临事不断，禀命不威，岂曰军容，同夫儿戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159936_comment'></div>复恐推劾之际，据引枝蔓，萌其茍免之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159936_comment'></div>奏报之间，淹延时日，启其幸生之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159936_comment'></div>纵不至此，亦慢令稽诛，无以励众，乃老师骄兵之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159936_comment'></div>臣不知朝廷所用将臣，必欲不令专制，悉上禀于宸算乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159936_comment'></div>复不知将臣不能用军法，皆取则于朝廷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159936_comment'></div>傥朝廷用将而不令专制，则臣所谓失阃外之制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159936_comment'></div>古之遣将也，君推毂而命之曰：「阃以内者，寡人制之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159936_comment'></div>阃以外者，将军制之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159936_comment'></div>此非徒然也，盖委任责成之道不得不重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159936_comment'></div>今而多轻之，故臣所谓失阃外之制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159936_comment'></div>茍将臣不能自用军法，则臣所谓隳军中之令矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159936_comment'></div>人之常情，孰不畏死，赊亿万之众，冒矢石之冲，刑之不严，何以督战？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159936_comment'></div>《兵法》曰：「畏我者不畏敌，畏敌者不畏我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159936_comment'></div>岂非严刑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159936_comment'></div>故对敌而伍中有不进者，伍长杀之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159936_comment'></div>伍长不进，什长杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159936_comment'></div>夫以什伍之长，尚得专杀，而统帅之重，不能诛一小校，以厉士卒，故臣以谓隳军中之令矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159936_comment'></div>议者或曰：今所遇之寇，未为大敌，所兴之师，未至深入，军中之法，未可专用，将校有犯，所宜奏裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159936_comment'></div>茍如议者之言，臣以为过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159936_comment'></div>寇非大敌，兵未深入，尚且狼狈先退，逗挠不进，傥遇大敌深入，而将校有犯，必须上闻，则穰苴之戮庄贾，非大敌也，止于会军而后期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159936_comment'></div>孙武之斩美人，非深入也，惟以习战而众笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159936_comment'></div>戮其君之宠臣、爱姬，亦未尝素禀而先启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159936_comment'></div>终于齐师胜晋，吴人入郢，孙武、穰苴皆为名将者，委任专而法素行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159936_comment'></div>以区区霸国，犹知任将之道，岂巍巍圣朝，不及于是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159936_comment'></div>且国朝著令：凡禁军将校，有过奏裁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159936_comment'></div>此则施于平居无事之日，边州守戍、近郡屯聚，则用之可矣，今昊贼乱常，蜂趸有毒，防边之兵逾数十万，将权不专，军法不峻，则何以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159936_comment'></div>臣伏望陛下出自宸断，稍假将权，凡有偏裨小校临阵先退，望敌不进，如此之类，罪犯灼然，但合该军法者，不须置狱，并许本部统帅对众便行军令讫，然后奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159936_comment'></div>如此，则师旅畏威，进退从令，或守或战，必有殊功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159936_comment'></div>兵者，国之大事，陛下于庙堂之上，与宰辅大臣计之审矣，岂容疏贱，辄有轻议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159936_comment'></div>然臣承乏宪署，职在司聪，茍有见闻，安可缄默？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159936_comment'></div>陛下勿以臣之此言徒习先生之常谈耳，遂忽而不省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159936_comment'></div>臣熟思之，任将治兵之术，何莫由斯道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159936_comment'></div>愚者之虑，幸赐采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159936_comment'></div>干冒旒冕，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1159936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　于河中府（今山西永济蒲州镇）置狱，审黄德和诬刘平、石元孙投敌事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年4月</a>　结河中府狱，诛黄德和，赏恤刘平、石元孙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　请不官修太祖神御殿，且务俭朴。作品：《奏为修开先殿乞循制度事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159934' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159934' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159934?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏为修开先殿乞循制度事<span class='inlineComment2'>（康定元年殿中侍御史）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159934")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159934_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159934'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159934'>臣某昧死谨疏上皇帝陛下：臣某诚惶诚惧、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159934_comment'></div>臣闻狂夫之言，圣人择焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159934_comment'></div>臣遭逢圣神，敢献狂瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159934_comment'></div>伏惟天地之大德，特贷盺钺之严诛，则微臣幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159934_comment'></div>臣伏睹今月十四日诏书，太平兴国寺僧绍宗缘化修盖外，所有太祖神御殿令三司差系官工匠重修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159934_comment'></div>又云：「庶重修于宏丽，获时荐于芬馨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159934_comment'></div>有以见陛下奉先思孝之道，高出百王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159934_comment'></div>复又尽给国财，不烦民力，此乃陛下敦崇俭德、勤恤民隐之意也，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159934_comment'></div>臣切以载营宝殿，严奉圣容，仰伫灵游，是为别庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159934_comment'></div>臣闻清庙之制，理在去华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159934_comment'></div>茅屋采椽，本贵乎克俭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159934_comment'></div>丹楹刻桷，乃讥其崇侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159934_comment'></div>《汉书·艺文志》曰：「墨家者流，出于清庙之官，是以贵俭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159934_comment'></div>由此观之，则清庙之尚俭明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159934_comment'></div>臣伏恐监工之官，未详诏旨，惟务宏丽，不稽典故，乖清庙尚俭之文，累烈祖恭德之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159934_comment'></div>臣伏望申敕有司，凡所营修，循以典制，经始勿亟，必顺天时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159934_comment'></div>臣按《月令》云：「孟春，无聚大众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159934_comment'></div>孟夏，无起事工」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159934_comment'></div>又曰：「孟冬可以造宫室」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159934_comment'></div>皆不欲妨农事而违天时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159934_comment'></div>臣窃计今之力役，固应不减千夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159934_comment'></div>虽用官工，不妨民事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159934_comment'></div>然而聚大众，起大功，作事不时，恐乖令典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159934_comment'></div>伏望预计徒庸，渐储材用，俟良月而兴作，亦不日而考成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159934_comment'></div>神之格思，宜锡纯嘏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159934_comment'></div>臣又风闻群僧籍籍，道路云云，皆谓既建太祖神御殿庭，则本寺佛殿钟楼，即应次第官修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159934_comment'></div>事之然否，虽未审知，臣忝陛下风宪之任，为陛下耳目之官，茍有所闻，理当先事言之，庶几上达宸听，盖欲杜其萌渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159934_comment'></div>臣伏睹景皊三年八月十三日所降圣旨云：「太平兴国寺佛殿钟楼并戒坛院舍宇等，官中更不修盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159934_comment'></div>令开封府及僧录司告示僧俗诸色人，并许缘化钱取便兴修」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159934_comment'></div>明命既行，远迩胥悦，皆以谓陛下省不急无益之务，轸爱民节用之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159934_comment'></div>自后已有僧绍宗化钱兴修，渐成轮奂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159934_comment'></div>臣伏虑群僧党扇，希望官中兼修佛殿钟楼，不复化缘营造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159934_comment'></div>伏乞申举景皊三年先降圣旨，其兴国寺佛殿钟楼，任令僧俗缘化兴修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159934_comment'></div>所冀绝其希望之心，固其缘化之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159934_comment'></div>况佛寺者非急之务，何须速成，国帑者有限之财，不可虚费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159934_comment'></div>景皊中，昊贼未萌逆节，朝廷未议兵事，尚且爱惜用度，不修佛舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159934_comment'></div>今则戍重兵于西鄙，一日之费，何啻千金？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159934_comment'></div>苟旬时之间，昊贼之首未即枭于藁街，臣恐事边之费，未免重困于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159934_comment'></div>臣愚以谓宜节营寺之浮费，以济备边之急用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159934_comment'></div>边既实，则狂寇何忧乎不歼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159934_comment'></div>皌荛之言，愿赐详择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159934_comment'></div>干冒天听，臣无任进退屏营之至<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文潞公文集》卷一四。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1159934'></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1159934_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　奏州县官吏须得其人，乞陕西、河东等近边县由审官院选差得力京朝官知县。作品：《乞令审官院选差沿边州郡知县》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159935' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159935' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159935?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令审官院选差沿边州郡知县事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159935")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159935_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159935'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159935'>臣伏见西边用兵缓急，有民间科率，应副军期，全藉州县，官吏必得其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159935_comment'></div>臣欲乞应是陜西河东近边及当路县分，自来只差县令处，乞令审官院并选差有心力干事京朝官知县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159935_comment'></div>如本院阙官差注，即乞外移合入西川官充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159935_comment'></div>兼有流外官见任本县簿尉处，亦乞令流内铨选差有出身干事选人充逐县簿尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159935_comment'></div>所贵缓急之间，易为集事，凡有科率，必得均平，则人户安居，不至劳苦。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1159935_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='25d1a8df46c14fbf9163d719b08183ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("25d1a8df46c14fbf9163d719b08183ad");'><span id='25d1a8df46c14fbf9163d719b08183ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1048')">1047-1048年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='25d1a8df46c14fbf9163d719b08183ad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　至京，张贵妃亲视供帐以待彦博夫人入谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　淯井监夷人作乱，彦博认为不必从秦凤路发兵，以其路途太远。作品：《乞差嘉眉益利屯兵救应淯井监更不差秦州兵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1159944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159944?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞差嘉眉益利屯兵救应淯井监更不差秦州兵奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159944")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159944_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159944'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159944'>臣今观梓州路奏称：缩井监夷人作过，事体不小，乞依庆历四年例，于秦凤路差发兵马赴本路救应事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159944_comment'></div>臣勘会庆历四年夏泸州界夷人作过，是时臣任秦凤路都部署、经略等使，准朝旨，令臣发禁军两指挥赴泸州救应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159944_comment'></div>臣以秦州去戎泸四十馀程，地远，必赴救不及，枉有拖曳兵甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159944_comment'></div>臣虽知不便，当时以朝旨丁宁，不敢稽留异议，遂发禁军两指挥赴泸州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159944_comment'></div>未及中路，夷人果已退去，其上件两指挥兵士只到遂州驻泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159944_comment'></div>是时川界州军见此兵士经过，人情颇亦惊恐，兼为遂州官吏不晓军政，不能平心抚驭，动有猜疑，几至生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159944_comment'></div>臣知益州日，炮此举动之失，曾具利害擘画闻奏，以谓戎、泸些少夷人作过，只是本处白艻子弟及宁远兵，亦自可御遏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159944_comment'></div>若贼势稍大，则计会梓、夔、益、利两路就近差那兵甲，可以讨击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159944_comment'></div>盖蠢尔小蛮，来则御之，不可穷其窟穴，岂烦远自秦凤兴师，空自劳弊，兼恐别有惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159944_comment'></div>况嘉、眉州皆是益、利钤辖司屯兵之处，若发兵救应，乘舟下水，不三四日便至泸州，赴救之势，最为神速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159944_comment'></div>臣之奏章，必枢府可以覆视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159944_comment'></div>伏乞更不自秦凤发兵，只令速计会益、利钤辖司相度量差兵甲，由水路赴泸州策应，甚为允当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159944_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159944_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1159944'>臣比欲候假开日面奏，又恐枢密院以梓州路所奏急切，已入文字乞依所奏，须至先具此奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1159944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　荐举梓州路转运使傅永。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　请速令田况选择官兵、使臣、总兵赴泸州。作品：《乞下田况选择官兵使臣总兵赴泸州仍令禀梓州路官指踪事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1159945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞下田况选择兵官使臣总兵赴泸州仍令禀梓州路官指纵事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159945")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159945'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159945'>臣伏见自去秋以来，日官所奏星文变异，皆云蜀中稍须防备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159945_comment'></div>近睹梓州路所奏缩井夷人作过，若只是十州五团夷人，即计其事体，必不致大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159945_comment'></div>本路便奏乞自秦凤发兵救应，臣却恐因此张皇，别致生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159945_comment'></div>兼庆历四年自秦凤发兵往彼，不惟无益于救援，而几乎别生他事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159945_comment'></div>臣炮此失，遂于前日奏乞不自秦凤发兵，只委益、利钤辖司相度，就便发兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159945_comment'></div>伏闻已依臣所奏，欲乞更速下田况，令选择兵官使臣总领赴泸州，每事令禀梓州路官指纵，不得辄分彼我，致有不和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159945_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159945_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1159945'>庆历四年秦凤所发兵到遂州，只为本处兵官不能平心抚驭，事分彼我，以致军情怨愤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159945_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年3月</a>　乞早罢兵招安夷人。作品：《乞早罢兵招安夷人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1159946' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159946' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159946?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞蚤罢兵招安夷人奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159946")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159946_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159946'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159946'>泸州风土瘴毒，至春夏尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159946_comment'></div>祥符二年秋，夷人作过，官军讨伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159946_comment'></div>至次年五月，诏曰：「泸州三月即苦瘴毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159946_comment'></div>如戎人尚敢旅拒，量留兵扼其险路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159946_comment'></div>令孙正辞等自二月领兵分屯近郡」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159946_comment'></div>臣以谓今来已是三月，本土气候方恶，乞密谕本路兵官、转运使，蚤令依常例招安打誓了，免致迁延瘴疠之地，人心不宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159946_comment'></div>兼祥符中，孙正辞等以蛮事未了，奏请添兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159946_comment'></div>真宗以边徼穷僻，供亿非易，不许其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159946_comment'></div>仍诏正辞等，如蛮人不受招安，已经诛剪畏服，勿穷追之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159946_comment'></div>又以丁谓招抚夔州，令歃血为盟，刻石柱为记事付之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159946_comment'></div>及令责招安小校，云：若夷人安集则赏，否则部送阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159946_comment'></div>未几，夷人果就招安，悉皆平定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159946_comment'></div>臣昨在益州，尝询采戎泸事体，多云本处招安将甚有狡猾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159946_comment'></div>平居无事，则间谍夷人，兴起事绪，意在差使招诱，率皆迁延玩寇，即所利甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159946_comment'></div>官吏乍到，或上下蒙蔽，不知其癚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159946_comment'></div>臣欲乞令本处兵官一面用兵威追胁诛剪，更须督责招安将用心招诱，早令安集，免致宿兵生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159946_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159946_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1159946'>臣以夷人作过虽不大，其如西蜀久安，若用兵多日，恐别生事。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1159946'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1159946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　乞封示两制等议泛使事文字，密示两府，免致漏泄。作品：《乞封示两制等议泛使事文字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159943' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞封示两制等议汎使事文字奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159943")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159943_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159943'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159943'>今月十七日，崇政殿蒙赐圣问，以北边汎使忽来，恐有邀求之事，深可预防，作何回报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159943_comment'></div>切以镇抚四夷，宰相之职，以臣之愚短，待罪宰司，不能有所建明，以致上烦宸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159943_comment'></div>然臣自闻北虏聚兵云朔，及闻有汎使来告西行，夙夕深思，多方迎料，但不欲先自张皇，预有漏泄，恐非示以闲暇镇静之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159943_comment'></div>须虏使之至，万一妄有邀求，或即别怀狡诈，则臣之思虑有素，可以随宜裁制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159943_comment'></div>臣今虽与陈执中等同署奏状，上答圣问示，不敢周悉开陈，以俟节假开日，细具面奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159943_comment'></div>兼臣两日以来，密采外议，皆云朝廷百僚只为议汎使事，传闻外方，深似不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159943_comment'></div>或恐学士以下，进日议状论汎使事，乞令左右封收，密示两府，免致漏泄，传布中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159943_comment'></div>谨具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159943_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1159943_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年9月</a>　欧阳修有贺拜参知政事启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年12月</a>　两次乞亲平贝州王则之叛。作品：《乞亲平贝州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年1月8日</a>　除参知政事兼河北宣抚使，以平贝州之乱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年1月</a>　请军事专行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年1月</a>　请用将作监主簿鞠真卿等三人掌机宜文字。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='42d4151a34804b419ad52b5f8f2f74fd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("42d4151a34804b419ad52b5f8f2f74fd");'><span id='42d4151a34804b419ad52b5f8f2f74fd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1051')">1048-1051年</a>，43-46岁</div><div id='42d4151a34804b419ad52b5f8f2f74fd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月9日</a>　告贝州平。槛车送王则至京师。诛知贝州张得一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月戊申</a>　同中书门下平章事、集贤殿大学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年闰1月</a>　欧阳修有贺拜相启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　杜衍贺拜相。彦博有诗谢之。作品：《宫保相公杜以某于贝之役与有劳焉及闻非才忝爰立之命……辄成拙恶一章以达谢意》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年2月</a>　以彦博荐，皇甫泌改知泽州，田京通判兖州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年4月</a>　以彦博数推明镐之功，权三司使明镐为参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年7月7日</a>　以彦博荐恩州城下勤劳，学士院试殿中丞王起、将作监主簿鞠真卿，诏充馆阁校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　乞知县、县令不得闲慢公事差出。作品：《乞知县县令不得闲慢公事差出》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1159951' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159951' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159951?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞知县县令不得闲慢公事差出奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159951")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159951_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159951'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159951'>县令为亲民重任，旧制不许差出，盖虑妨阙政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159951_comment'></div>近岁以来，诸路职司官多是将闲慢公事皏以为名，差遣出入，颇妨本县民政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159951_comment'></div>大抵皆是自便私故，或即避见本任繁难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159951_comment'></div>朝廷累有约束，未绝其弊痈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159951_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后知县、县令除许差推勘重难刑狱及应副军期差使，或权知繁剧郡县外，更不得以闲慢公事差出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159951_comment'></div>仍令今后凡差出知县、县令，并须依旧例具事由奏知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159951_comment'></div>如差讫不奏，或依前以闲慢公事差出知县、县令，其所差职司官吏，并从违制分数定罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159951_comment'></div>被差之官，亦行断罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159951_comment'></div>所贵县务别无妨阙，民政得以修举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159951_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159951_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1159951'>此事最关民政，承前虽有约束，终未绝其弊，今乞严行指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1159951_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　乞继上奏封细陈事理，以防面陈口奏时，蹇讷有所未尽，事理有所未周。作品：《乞继上奏封细陈事理》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一五。）</span><div id='poem_1159950' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159950' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159950?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞继上奏封细陈事理奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159950")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159950_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159950'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159950'>臣读唐史，见白居易为翰林学士，因事进谏，语甚切直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159950_comment'></div>宪宗不悦，谓宰相李绛曰：「白居易小子是朕拔擢，致名位而无礼于朕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159950_comment'></div>朕极难奈」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159950_comment'></div>绛对曰：「居易所以不避死亡之诛，事无大小而必言者，盖酬陛下拔擢耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159950_comment'></div>陛下欲开谏诤之路，不宜阻居易之言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159950_comment'></div>宪宗曰：「卿言是也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159950_comment'></div>由是言多听纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159950_comment'></div>臣以居易被宪宗拔擢，才为学士，能尽忠极谏，以报恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159950_comment'></div>而况臣非才寒进，孤立无党，独蒙陛下误听，特力拔擢，位至宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159950_comment'></div>犬马之诚，坚于报主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159950_comment'></div>然自待罪两府，已逾二年，略无谋猷，上裨神圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159950_comment'></div>虽则日奉天颜，常亲黼座，所奏覆者率多冗细事务，常程文书，徒烦睿听，无益治体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159950_comment'></div>以此为宰相职业，真所谓素餐尸禄，龊龊小谨而已，岂陈平所谓「宰相者，上佐天子，理阴阳，顺四时，外镇抚四夷，使卿大夫各得任其职」之义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159950_comment'></div>房乔、杜如晦，唐之贤相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159950_comment'></div>太宗犹常责之曰：「公为宰相，当须开耳目，求访贤哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159950_comment'></div>有武艺谋略、才堪抚众者，任以边事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159950_comment'></div>有经明德修、立性明悟者，任以侍臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159950_comment'></div>有明干清悫、处事公平者，任以剧务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159950_comment'></div>有学通古今、识达政术者，任以治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159950_comment'></div>此乃宰相之裨益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159950_comment'></div>比闻听受词讼，日不暇给，安能助朕求贤哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159950_comment'></div>斯言之责，诚为至当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159950_comment'></div>臣每侍丹扆，累闻德音，常以求贤致治为切务，推诚纳谏为至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159950_comment'></div>臣愚不能上副圣意，而陛下至仁，未忍以大义责臣，而臣独不内愧于心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159950_comment'></div>臣复自念性本朴忠，言多蹇拙，幸得进对咫尺天威，凡所敷陈，或未详尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159950_comment'></div>臣尝观唐宰相赵憬奏章，欲上书论事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159950_comment'></div>其略曰：「稽颡丹陛，仰对宸严，蹇纳易穷，遽数难辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159950_comment'></div>理详则尘渎颇甚，言略则利害不分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159950_comment'></div>切闻贞观、开元之际，宰辅论事，或多上书，所冀获尽情理」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159950_comment'></div>时德宗嘉纳之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159950_comment'></div>今臣之愚，犹憬之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159950_comment'></div>此后有面陈口奏，顷刻之间，或蹇纳有所未尽，事理有所未周，即欲继上奏封，细陈理道，上裨睿圣访纳之勤，下尽微臣区区之蕴，固不敢妄陈偏见，亦不乞留中不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159950_comment'></div>惟冀圣慈，特赐详择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1159950_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　为父母自山西介休县迁葬洛阳伊阙县事，乞罢重任。作品：《乞罢重任》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　将迁葬事托付给了司马光。司马光代为作迁葬相关文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　司马光为彦博父文洎作挽词三首。诏王尧臣为彦博父文洎作神道碑文，司马光代彦博作谢表。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　承仁宗亲飞白赐奉坟寺额，父“教忠积庆”，母“永福”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　答御札手诏，以仁宗赐彦博手诏。较全面地展现出彦博之为政思想。作品：《答御札手诏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一六。）</span><div id='poem_1159952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答御札手诏奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159952")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159952'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159952'>臣等各以非才，忝居大任，不能裨补圣政，燮和阴阳，以致星文屡有变异，下饬人事，上贻圣忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159952_comment'></div>陛下曲示包容，未赐罢免，责以来效，使之极言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159952_comment'></div>诏旨丁宁，睿思宽大，跪受伏读，兢鷏失图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159952_comment'></div>恭以陛下尧舜用心，禹汤罪己，钦若天戒，增修圣政，弥灾召和，宜集休应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「德政阙修，刑赏差滥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓刑不为贵近而屈，赏不可侥痈而求，则无差滥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159952_comment'></div>刑赏不滥，则德政自修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「人有冤滞而无控雪之路，民已匮困而无宽恤之实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓人有冤滞，必由郡县及按察之司节级陈诉，若犹未伸，又许检、鼓檛诉，固无壅遏之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159952_comment'></div>然更须州郡官吏常得其人，为之伸理，则民绝冤滞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159952_comment'></div>今冗费无艺，国用窘乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159952_comment'></div>故岁一不登，下民艰食，虽欲恤之而力不足也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159952_comment'></div>若减不急之务，罢无功之赏，及兵籍官吏之浮冗者稍澄汰之，则庶几国用不乏，则可以有恤民之实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「官局具设而职务或弛，典章备存而纲纪不振」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓为官择人，不使侥痈者求而得之，久于其任，考其殿最而升黜之，无使屡迁速易，不为茍简之政，则职务焉敢废弛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159952_comment'></div>祖宗之法备在典册，举而行之，似若甚易，但不为权痈所挠，则为至难。<div
