class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159952_comment'></div>茍上下一意，守兹典章，坚如金石，行此号令，信如四时，则纲纪振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「科役烦重，肆成暴刻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159952_comment'></div>军政简堕，而莫为经制」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓前之所陈减不急之务，罢无功之赏，澄汰兵吏之冗，则国用不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159952_comment'></div>国用不乏，则可以省科役之烦重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159952_comment'></div>州郡官吏常得其人，虽有科役，亦不至于暴刻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159952_comment'></div>慎择将帅，稍假威权，抚驭士卒，不务姑息，勿使贵臣骁将挠于其间，则军政自肃而有经制矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「教令轻出，有所未安，贤智在下，遗而弗举」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓令出惟行，慎乎始出，出而不慎，故行之未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159952_comment'></div>近岁以来，兹弊颇甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159952_comment'></div>由议臣轻建言而须必行，行之无效而终无责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159952_comment'></div>或虽有嘉谋，而事无近效，人之多言，横为沮议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159952_comment'></div>朝廷不能持之，故多中变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159952_comment'></div>条其事状，此类尤繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159952_comment'></div>举贤任官，宰相之职，宰相不能悉知其人，但当慎择台省长官及州县大吏，使如近制，各举所知，庶几无遗才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「癚痈妄求而不抑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159952_comment'></div>此正今之所患，臣等继日议之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「惠泽旋壅而不流」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159952_comment'></div>臣以谓朝廷推恩，靡不下究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159952_comment'></div>然恐郡县之吏，不称朝廷之意，或逋负之物，合除而未除，流窜之人，可释而不释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159952_comment'></div>如此类者，更宜申明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「将此十二条于军国庶务中推求实事，有合更张振举者，密切条上，朕当悉心详究，即议施行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159952_comment'></div>有以见陛下求治之心，勤切之至，所恨臣等空疏，不能上副好问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159952_comment'></div>虽然，敢不罄竭愚短，粗有所裨？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159952_comment'></div>然今所陈，乃其大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159952_comment'></div>盖虑繁词，终成虚语，徒烦睿览，无补大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159952_comment'></div>臣等欲将十二条事，举一两条细述，合更张振举事件，逐时面奏，委曲敷陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159952_comment'></div>所冀言之必行，行之必当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159952_comment'></div>斯亦舜、禹、皋陶吁谟都俞之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159952_comment'></div>臣等不胜区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「德政阙修，刑赏差滥」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159952_comment'></div>臣等近奏以谓刑不为贵近所屈，赏不为侥痈所求，则无滥矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159952_comment'></div>臣等请略举一端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159952_comment'></div>如往年苏舜钦、刘巽以进奏院赛神，辄用官钱，即皆坐除名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159952_comment'></div>去年曾睪、宋永宗赛神，亦用官钱，其罚当与舜钦辈均，而曾睪等止停见任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159952_comment'></div>近日史昭文等以不觉察手下人吏取受稍场钱物冲替，未得与差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159952_comment'></div>寻有监稍场官阎继隆等，却为昭文所发，亦是不觉察专典取受，一例冲替，而昭文即时却与差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159952_comment'></div>其同事冯经亦连茹牵复，而继隆等冲替如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159952_comment'></div>此盖昭文、曾睪辈以亲近而从轻罚，舜钦、继隆等以疏远而受重责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159952_comment'></div>又去年亲事官作过，皇城司官吏当坐重责，然皆是近臣贵戚，止于降秩补外，才逾年即皆复职，或更迁官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159952_comment'></div>往年张沔以保州及李鰎事降黜，数经大赦，至今未复旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159952_comment'></div>言体则皇城司事为重，议罪则张沔等辈为轻，升擢废弃，理似未均，不惟刑罚失平，实恐贵痈坏法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159952_comment'></div>臣等以谓今后用法，理当振举，更务均平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159952_comment'></div>赏典之滥，则如近日司天监周琮、李用晦，止以选课日辰，便乞转官任子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159952_comment'></div>医官别无劳绩，妄乞额外转迁，如冯琦、潘象、苏惟和、沈遇明之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1159952_comment'></div>赖陛下圣断，皆与裁抑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1159952_comment'></div>然未悉如先朝之制及前后条贯，更欲申明遵守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「人有冤滞，而无控雪之路」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1159952_comment'></div>臣等谓人有冤滞，必由郡县按察之官节级陈诉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1159952_comment'></div>若未申雪，又许检、鼓院鉲诉，计无壅遏之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1159952_comment'></div>今欲更敕约转运司、提刑司，凡有理诉，并令子细究详，如事理稍涉冤枉，即选官就近覆勘，勿令烦扰淹延，免致贫穷无资不能诣阙者抑而无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「民已困匮而无宽恤之实」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1159952_comment'></div>又曰：「科役烦重，肆成暴刻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1159952_comment'></div>臣等以谓国用窘则科役烦，科役烦则民困匮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1159952_comment'></div>民力既困，国用自乏，虽欲恤民，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1159952_comment'></div>臣等请言其国用窘乏之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1159952_comment'></div>恭惟祖宗以来置兵与吏，及赏赉赐予，皆有定制，量入以出，故财不屈乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1159952_comment'></div>自康定用兵之后，添募新兵几四十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1159952_comment'></div>数年以来，虽逃亡减废之外，犹不减三十馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1159952_comment'></div>每岁所费衣粮钱物等，共约三千万贯、匹、两、石、束，赏赉之数不在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1159952_comment'></div>兼自庆历二年后来添给二虏金帛，每岁共四十馀万匹两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1159952_comment'></div>加以频遭水旱，复除租赋，则国用不得不窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1159952_comment'></div>故国用窘则科役烦，科役烦则民力困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1159952_comment'></div>今将恤民之困穷，宽民之科役，正在省冗费而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1159952_comment'></div>省冗费之大者，在减冗兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1159952_comment'></div>臣等已尝奏述，欲于今冬别立拣兵之格，密降付逐路转运使，俟至春首，依常年例计会帅臣，同共依新格择选老弱，以减冗费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1159952_comment'></div>其次则罢不急之土木，停无功之赐予，抑侥痈之求请，省员外之冗官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1159952_comment'></div>衣服用度，务从敦质，多方节约，诸事简俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1159952_comment'></div>年岁之间，渐期足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1159952_comment'></div>国用既足，则科役不烦，则是恤民之实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「官局具设而职务或弛，典章备存而纲纪不振」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1159952_comment'></div>臣等以谓官得其人，职务自举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1159952_comment'></div>选才任官，正是臣等之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1159952_comment'></div>若官须择人，不甚拘以资地，事须责实当时校其殿最，三载考绩，必行黜陟，百官修饬，孰敢懈弛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1159952_comment'></div>臣等请略举其弊：只如省府之官及外计之任，近岁以来，迁改颇速，有如假道，岂暇举职？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1159952_comment'></div>所以务为一切茍简之政，而职务不得不弛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1159952_comment'></div>臣等欲乞更颁诏敕，约束中外之官，必须二年之外，方许迁替，考其殿最而升降之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1159952_comment'></div>若特敕擢才，则不在兹限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1159952_comment'></div>所谓典章者，朝廷之大法，祖宗之旧制，举而行之，执而用之，岂有纲纪不振哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1159952_comment'></div>盖近岁以来，缘贵痈之臣堕大法、坏旧制者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1159952_comment'></div>臣等略举其尤者：祖宗之制，官有定员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1159952_comment'></div>今员外而置官者多矣，如勾当皇城军头司及医官使副之比是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1159952_comment'></div>又俸禄之法，各有定制，等级赋与，固不可差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1159952_comment'></div>今则有任观察使而请留后俸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1159952_comment'></div>如此之类，其徒萛繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1159952_comment'></div>臣等欲乞今后更不溢旧额而置官，逾本官而受俸，一守祖宗旧制，不为贵痈所侵，则纲纪振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1159952_comment'></div>乞特颁一诏敕处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「军政简堕，而莫为经制」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1159952_comment'></div>臣等尝谓慎择将帅，不务姑息，勿使贵臣骄将害之，军政自肃矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「教令轻出，有所未安」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1159952_comment'></div>臣等尝谓慎乃出令，令出惟行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1159952_comment'></div>若轻出之，必有未允，则数易屡改，此为政之大弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1159952_comment'></div>若近日钱令、盐法，为弊不细，而建言者谋之不臧，未尝有责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1159952_comment'></div>此所以致轻改作而易受弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1159952_comment'></div>往年建言诸州招刺义军，去岁却拣配诸军，人心骚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1159952_comment'></div>其始不能详慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1159952_comment'></div>致不数年，便有改易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1159952_comment'></div>臣略举此数条，盖事之稍大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「贤智在下，遗而弗举」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1159952_comment'></div>臣等尝谓举贤择才，辅臣之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1159952_comment'></div>辅臣之不能悉知众才，惟当慎择台省长官、州郡大吏，使如近制，各举所知，庶几无遗才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1159952_comment'></div>然臣等敢不益励蠢愚，博求才智，将期得士之美，上副任贤之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「癚痈妄求而不抑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1159952_comment'></div>臣等以谓近臣贵戚、医工卜祝及诸司人吏，因缘请皏，妄述微劳，希求内降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1159952_comment'></div>如此之类，尽守旧制，一切裁抑，则官邪之蹊可以渐塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1159952_comment'></div>圣诏曰：「惠泽旋壅而不流」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1159952_comment'></div>臣等尝谓凡有推恩，靡不下究，犹恐州郡之吏，不称朝廷之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1159952_comment'></div>或逋负之物，当除而未除；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1159952_comment'></div>流窜之人，可释而不释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1159952_comment'></div>臣等欲乞应经前年大赦合放负欠物色，如省司以未见保明文字，州郡以未受朝省指挥，至今尚行催理者，速令勘会，依赦蠲除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1159952_comment'></div>编配之人，除属拣选路分外，有已经量移情理轻者，令具元犯奏闻看详，依赦释放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1159952_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_127_1159952'></div><div id='poem_sentence_127_1159952_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　进无为而治论，请仁宗谨守祖宗之成法，使爵赏刑罚不失其当。作品：《进无为而治论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_1160315' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160315' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160315?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进无为而治论</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160315")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160315_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160315'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160315'>臣顷因奏事，亲闻德音，谓古称无为而治者，必当先有为而致无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160315_comment'></div>臣虽即时仰对曰：「虞舜垂衣而治者，亦皆先有为而后无为，诚如圣意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160315_comment'></div>臣退而伏思曰：陛下有尧舜求治之心，而臣愚无皋、夔致君之术，夙夕惭惧，启处不遑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160315_comment'></div>又以奉对之际，蹇讷未周，谨寻前典所述虞舜之德著于简牍，仰尘鉴观，庶几愚忠，上裨圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160315_comment'></div>仲尼曰：「无为而治者，其舜也欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160315_comment'></div>夫何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160315_comment'></div>恭己正南面而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160315_comment'></div>先儒之解，以谓：任官得其人，故无为而治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160315_comment'></div>考于《虞书》，则舜之治也，流共工于幽州，以其心狠貌恭，足以惑世也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160315_comment'></div>放驩兜于崇山，以其掩义隐贼，党于共工也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160315_comment'></div>窜三苗于三危，以其贪冒食货，崇侈不才也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160315_comment'></div>殛鲧于羽山，以其顽嚚傲狠，治水无功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160315_comment'></div>四罪而天下咸服，兹所谓去邪不疑而罚当其罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160315_comment'></div>于是询四岳以谋政治，辟四门以求众贤，明四目，达四聪，以广视听于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160315_comment'></div>命禹作司空，以平水土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160315_comment'></div>弃为后稷，以播百谷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160315_comment'></div>契作司徒，以敷五教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160315_comment'></div>皋陶作士师，以典五刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160315_comment'></div>垂作共工，益作朕虞，伯夷作秩宗，以典三礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160315_comment'></div>夔典乐，以教胄子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160315_comment'></div>龙作纳言，出纳朕命惟允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160315_comment'></div>既命以官，因戒敕之曰：各恭其职，乃能立天下之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160315_comment'></div>然后三载考绩，三考，黜陟幽明，庶绩咸熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160315_comment'></div>兹所谓任贤勿贰，而官得其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160315_comment'></div>夫明四目，达四聪，去四凶，命庶官，其勤至矣，得不谓之先有为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160315_comment'></div>及夫庶绩咸熙，天下服，垂衣裳，正南面而己，得不谓之后无为乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160315_comment'></div>臣究观经史之载，舜之至德也，有大功二十，举十六相，去四凶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160315_comment'></div>十六相谓八元、八凯，稷、契、皋、夔之伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160315_comment'></div>去四凶则朝廷无奸邪之党，举十六相则左右皆贤哲之辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160315_comment'></div>如是而天下不治者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160315_comment'></div>故后世圣帝明王，莫不劳于求贤，而逸于致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160315_comment'></div>劳于求贤，则先有为也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160315_comment'></div>逸于致治，则后无为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160315_comment'></div>恭以陛下绍祖宗之丕基，行尧舜之至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160315_comment'></div>黜邪远佞，去四凶之志也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160315_comment'></div>求贤审官，举十六相之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160315_comment'></div>然而一日万务，尚劳宵旰，兹乃臣愚不称职之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160315_comment'></div>臣以为方今之务，正在谨守祖宗之成法，使爵赏刑罚不失其当耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160315_comment'></div>爵赏当，则奸邪无功者不敢侥倖而希进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160315_comment'></div>刑罚当，则贵近有罪者不敢请求而茍免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160315_comment'></div>纪纲正而朝廷尊，号令行而天下服，如此，则陛下高拱穆清之中，无为而与虞舜比隆，而下视三代之盛矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1160315_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年7月</a>　赞以推恩，晏殊、张观、杜衍等十四人皆迁官加职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　和致政相公杜衍频有唱和。作品：《寄致政太师相公杜四首》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年8月</a>　言恩礼薄，陈执中优除兵部尚书、知陈州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年8月2日</a>　迁昭文馆大学士、同中书门下平章事、监修国史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　优迁王尧臣，以彦博与之同年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　胡宿封还杨怀敏复除内侍副都知词头不草，彦博为其开脱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　与枢密使庞籍主省冗兵之议，并担保“万一果聚为盗贼，二臣请死之”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　请牙盘上食务尽精洁，一依旧仪，不擅增改。作品：《牙盘食奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>牙盘食奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160255")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160255'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160255'>近臣睹臣僚上言以太庙时享，牙盘食品，宜尽精美，一如常膳器皿之物，亦取常所进御，于理为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160255_comment'></div>臣切以清庙昭德，著于前训，牙盘上食，本非旧仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160255_comment'></div>始因唐天宝五载，实明皇之季年，缘秦汉陵寝之制，有朔望上食之仪，遂诏太庙时享，兼供牙盘常食，于牲牢笾俎之閒，杂燕私膳羞之品，率情变礼，亵味渎神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160255_comment'></div>而当时礼官，不能执守典法，遂即因循行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160255_comment'></div>贞元以来，达礼之士，频议寝罢，然亦惮于改革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160255_comment'></div>伏自国朝以来，奉宗庙之重，修祭祀之礼，率遵典故，备极精虔，牙盘上食，亦循唐制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160255_comment'></div>行之已久，罢之固难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160255_comment'></div>臣近以差摄祠官，祭享太庙，于点膳之日，亲阅牙盘食器，并皆精洁，涂金银镶，朱里漆器，列于簠簋之次，实得奢俭之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160255_comment'></div>至于食味品数，皆有旧规，谓宜谨守故常，不可增改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160255_comment'></div>但申敕所司，每遇上食，务尽精洁，其食器稍有损故，随即申请饰换，一切如故仪，更不擅议增改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160255_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160255_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年2月19日</a>　议明堂制度。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年4月10日</a>　奏亲献之礼。作品：《亲献之礼奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160257?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲献之礼奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐二年四月十日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160257")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160257_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160257'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160257'>以诏书所定亲献之礼，若周于五天帝、神州地祇，比圜丘之位，恐陟降为劳也，请命官分献之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1160257_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年5月1日</a>　奏礼神祭玉及燔玉用珉制度。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年5月24日</a>　撰明堂乐章。作品：降神《诚安》；送神《诚安》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《文彦博集校注》佚诗。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年9月27日</a>　任大礼使，大飨明堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月</a>　加礼部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年10月</a>　诏彦博等编修《大飨明堂记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　举李綎。作品：《举李綎》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年12月</a>　乞立家庙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月</a>　上《明堂大飨记》二十卷、《纪要》二卷。作品：《进大飨明堂记表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160258?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进大飨明堂记表</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160258")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160258'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160258'>禁中论述，方伉曲台之编；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160258_comment'></div>圣世典容，宁后江都之集？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160258_comment'></div>《玉海》卷九六。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160258_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年5月</a>　荐张瑰、王安石、韩维，皆以恬退。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月丁酉</a>　被唐介弹劾。言其显用张尧佐，阴结张贵妃，自为谋身之计。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月</a>　请退。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　梅尧臣作《书窜诗》，以彦博为巨奸。或以此诗出自魏泰《碧云騢》，伪以梅尧臣之名，乃诋毁时贤也。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='cc5d528cc99d4686a58142de6eb06c38_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc5d528cc99d4686a58142de6eb06c38");'><span id='cc5d528cc99d4686a58142de6eb06c38_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，50岁</div><div id='cc5d528cc99d4686a58142de6eb06c38' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>仁宗问二相于欧阳修，修答以“朝士相贺”<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>仁宗问二相于庞籍。庞籍称彦博“实无所私，但恶之者毁之尔”<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>文同书贺彦博拜昭文相。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>请陕西乡狭户少处，三两乡合差一里正。作品：《奏里正衙前事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159959?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏里正衙前事</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159959")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159959'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159959'>臣昨在陜西，访问民间甚苦者，里正、衙前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159959_comment'></div>里正法用第一等户，乡狭户少者，至差第三等充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159959_comment'></div>是致差定之时，更相纠决，禁系追呼，动逾岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159959_comment'></div>校计家资，纤细不漏，至于食器甚贱之物，估直为业，及充衙前，籍为抵当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159959_comment'></div>主持场务，稍有欠折，则竭产偿官，犹不能足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159959_comment'></div>欲令陜西都转运使相度辖下州县，有乡狭户少处，将比近三两乡合差一里正，即可选力及人户充役，且不致差遣频并，庶宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159959_comment'></div>况自前累有上言，乞尽罢里正者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159959_comment'></div>今以三两乡合差一里正，事亦酌中。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1159959'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159959_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>奏陕西衙前押木筏纲事。作品：《奏陕西衙前押木筏纲事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏陕西衙前押木筏纲</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159960")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159960_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159960'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159960'>陜西衙前最苦者押木筏纲，无不被刑破产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159960_comment'></div>臣在永兴，令通判职官周询其弊，皆言每岁春初，方自朝省分配到合要木植，比至收买系筏，须及夏末以来，仅得办集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159960_comment'></div>正值黄河水泛涨之时，常有飘失，其劳苦费用，动逾数倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159960_comment'></div>遂擘画于年前冬初，沿河出木处县邑，官置买木场，先勘会省转向前分配文字，约度常年须合应用木植，预前收买，如法安置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159960_comment'></div>比至春初，省司配木植文字到来，量事添备，便可系筏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159960_comment'></div>趁四月间水势平缓之时，驾放赴下纳州军，极甚省功减费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159960_comment'></div>此只是永兴军一处，通判职官等已如此擘画，其馀沿河出木州军未曾行遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159960_comment'></div>欲乞下陜西转运司更相度经久施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159960_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a8edcd546a2f471eb85f82dc6ee8af58_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a8edcd546a2f471eb85f82dc6ee8af58");'><span id='a8edcd546a2f471eb85f82dc6ee8af58_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1058')">1055-1058年</a>，50-53岁</div><div id='a8edcd546a2f471eb85f82dc6ee8af58' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　奏王安论亲事官张贵事。作品：《奏王安论亲事官张贵事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159962?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏王安论亲事官张贵事</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159962")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159962'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159962'>臣今日酉时准内降劄子，为王安所论事，实有𨧱刀，称在角楼下埋藏，为日晚，欲就来早监取，又恐隔夜，人惧罪藏隐，如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159962_comment'></div>臣蚤来读王安首状，内言张贵称有刀埋在东北角楼下，切恐有干连人惧罪隐藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159962_comment'></div>欲乞差稳审内臣一名，今夜且于所指通埋刀去处侧近，别作行勾当名目觉察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159962_comment'></div>或令密使人巡觑照望至晓，必不至别有人擅去发掘，亦不至张皇惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159962_comment'></div>乞令勘官陈旭仔细审问张贵所埋刀去处，疾速闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159962_comment'></div>兼臣早来详王安状内，张贵称已结连得三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159962_comment'></div>寻有劄子令军头司官员，如获张贵，先且取问，除见今指名收捉共七人外，更有徒党，即就便逐急收捉，免致走漏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159962_comment'></div>更乞下陈旭紧切推问张贵，如实更有徒伴，即密具姓名疾速闻奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159962_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　智沮武继隆、贾昌朝之谋，主修六塔河。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　与参知政事程戡以亲家故乞回避。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　擢通判青州黄庶知康州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年1月</a>　仁宗暴得疾，威坐安宫禁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　果断斩告反禁卒以靖众。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　任大礼使，恭谢天地。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　乞立宗实（英宗之名）为嗣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　苏洵上书彦博。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　请迁唐介。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　建言重定《本草图经》作品：节要〈本草图〉序。<div id='poem_1160306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>节要本草图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160306")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160306'>余尝以近世医工，虽处方有据，而用药不精，以至疗疾寡效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160306_comment'></div>盖古医用药，率多自采，故桐君著《采药录》，备其花叶形色，别其是非真假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160306_comment'></div>用之决无乖误，服之咸得痊愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160306_comment'></div>而又择郡国地产之良，及春秋秀实之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160306_comment'></div>今则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160306_comment'></div>药肆不能尽识，但凭采送之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160306_comment'></div>医工鲜通本草，莫辨良苦之杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160306_comment'></div>加之膺伪，遂以合和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160306_comment'></div>以兹疗治，宜其寡效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160306_comment'></div>唐室之盛，置《药园生本草图》，欲悉知其形色、气味，用药之精且慎如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160306_comment'></div>嘉祐初，余在政府，建言重定《本草图经》，凡数年而成，例蒙赐本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160306_comment'></div>然药品繁夥，尽形绘事，卷帙颇多，披阅匪易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160306_comment'></div>因录其常用要切者若干种，别为图策，以便披检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160306_comment'></div>简则易辨，人得有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160306_comment'></div>按图而验，辨误识真，用之于医，所益多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160306_comment'></div>潞国公宽夫记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1160306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160225'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160225'>臣切见大理寺丞姚复学政精勤，临事干敏，士检端悫，为众所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160225_comment'></div>臣两奏充掌机宜文字，备见其能，伏望圣慈特赐召试出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160225_comment'></div>如经擢用后所举不如状，甘谬妄之坐。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1160225'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160225_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　举魏沂。作品：《举魏沂》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160229?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举魏沂劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160229")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160229_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160229'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160229'>臣去年夏奉制判永兴军，奏辟河南府伊阙县主簿魏沂就若充京兆府学教授，未到任间，臣被召赴阙，沂已经流内铨投状，情愿更不赴任，在铨祗候注官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160229_comment'></div>勘会沂自嘉皊八年登进士第，初任河南府伊阙县主簿方十个月，以臣奏举罢官，不成考第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160229_comment'></div>近知改注真定府户曹参军，犹待远阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160229_comment'></div>伏缘本人久预太学生员，众所推其学业，臣今保举，伏乞朝廷改注沂西京或南京国子教授差遣，免致久罢官守，妨废资考，足以推广学业，训励生员。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160229_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a
