class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495118'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495118'>厥初丕命集，咸庆长君贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495118'>恭俭敦尧德，忧勤损舜年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495118'>象耕苍野地，龙御鼎湖天。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495118'>帝锡宣英号，鸿休耀信编。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495118_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495118'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495118_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495119?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年1月8日）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495119'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495119'>在隐推龙德，重明协帝华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495119'>蓼萧均泽及，四海詟威加。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495119'>就日心方切，腾天驭已赊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495119'>攀髯不可跂<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作跋，据四库本改）</span>，泪目送云霞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495119_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　以为横山族长不可招纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　条奏薛向奏疏《西陲利害》作品：《条奏薛向利害》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159964' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159964?labeling=true' target='_blank'>条奏薛向利害</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159964")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159964'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159964'>臣被旨令看薛向所上疏并边陲利害，具可否条例录进入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159964_comment'></div>臣详观向之所陈，大要有五：其一，任将帅以制其冲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159964_comment'></div>其二，亟攻伐以罢其敌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159964_comment'></div>其三，省戍兵以实其力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159964_comment'></div>其四，绝利原以弊其国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159964_comment'></div>其五，慎经费以固其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159964_comment'></div>所谓任将帅者，朝廷何尝不慎择而重之，但所择或得或否耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159964_comment'></div>既得其人，固当如向所论，使久其任，必各成效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159964_comment'></div>犹如前时屡迁数易，虽得贤才，使将帅亦难责其成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159964_comment'></div>所谓亟攻伐以罢其敌者，一曰先举之策，以谓先发制人攻胜，后发制于人攻负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159964_comment'></div>故欲亟肆以罢之，多方以误之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159964_comment'></div>二曰浅攻之策，其大旨欲招诱横山部族，团结熟户之兵及义勇弓箭手之众，侵扰贼境，使不宁居，将自困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159964_comment'></div>此皆朝廷素留意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159964_comment'></div>兼韩琦上言，庆历初，曾与范仲俺尝建此议，会西人输款而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159964_comment'></div>去岁枢密院遂与中书同议，悉有成算，寻已降付逐路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159964_comment'></div>今录奏议进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159964_comment'></div>兼逐路之兵，自来未尝精较实数，去岁枢密院令编例官类聚得确实人数降下诸路，严切训练，至于部分，亦有成法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159964_comment'></div>并检康定中诸路出师牵制之术，并密封，逐帅遵守<span class='inlineComment2'>（今并别录本进呈。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159964_comment'></div>朝廷处置之详，殆无遗策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159964_comment'></div>然此举动，必当其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159964_comment'></div>去岁十月臣尝上奏于先帝，若谅祚果遂倔强，自绝于朝廷，以讨伐凶渠，招纳降附，无所不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159964_comment'></div>若犹恭顺服过，即当含容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159964_comment'></div>所谓羁縻不绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159964_comment'></div>况王者之师，非不得已，岂宜轻用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159964_comment'></div>今向亦云若谅祚改图自新，复守誓诏，伏望廓天地之量，霁雷霆之怒，省费罢兵，安边息民，天下之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159964_comment'></div>斯言是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159964_comment'></div>然于平时不可不讲议精熟，一旦有隙，用之无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159964_comment'></div>所谓省戍兵以实其力者，其要欲省东兵之疲软，拣土兵之精勤，取实用，损虚为，持久必胜之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159964_comment'></div>朝廷近以计较逐路之兵，去冗留精，皆有定数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159964_comment'></div>俟向去春季，依法料简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159964_comment'></div>兼去岁不以亲卫兵戍边，此亦省兵实力之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159964_comment'></div>又曰绝利源以弊其国，谓朝廷岁赐并缘边和市，一宜绝之，贼势自窘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159964_comment'></div>岁赐、和市，如谅祚阻命，自当绝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159964_comment'></div>上三策，不待议论而利害可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159964_comment'></div>所谓慎经费以固其本，此乃方今至切之务，最要讲求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159964_comment'></div>盖经费若简，国财乃富，国富即兵强，兵强即蛮夷不敢内侮，而后制礼作乐，驯至太平，何欲而不可？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159964_comment'></div>今之言者，不计国用之丰寡，而欲轻举妄动，为国生事者多矣，惟朝廷审用而慎行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159964_comment'></div>兵一用，其费不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159964_comment'></div>茍力屈货殚，虽有智者不能善其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159964_comment'></div>向又以调度兵费，宜以康定为炮，其言尤为切当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159964_comment'></div>盖康定时兵久不用，人未知战，上下骚然，暴取横用，莫知纪极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159964_comment'></div>天下困弊，终无尺寸之功，亦可炮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159964_comment'></div>向云自宝元初，守官陜右，出入兵间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159964_comment'></div>今又主关中之漕，首尾七年，目睹心计，固宜详悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159964_comment'></div>其言诚有伦理，然谋攻料敌，老将所难，兵者大事，不可轻言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159964_comment'></div>古人论兵至慎至重，如向云取横山如反掌，捕西贼若设罝掩兔，谋虽可采，言亦似轻，诚愿慎之重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159964_comment'></div>愚虑如此，伏乞圣神详择。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1159964_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年9月27日</a>　拜司空。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　以种谔城绥州不妥。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　请归嵬名山部落。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年11月</a>　请两府、诸路帅臣、转运使审择久任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年12月</a>　乞戒励诸路将帅。作品：《乞戒励诸路将帅》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1159972' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159972' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159972?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞戒励诸路将帅奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159972")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159972_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159972'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159972'>今西事方兴，用兵有渐，欲预行戒励诸路将帅：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159972'>一、将佐逐日公共协心，讲求兵政边事，各务周知利害，蕴畜有素，临事不惑，则鲜有败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1159972'>一、将佐依时躬亲训练士卒，务令事艺习熟，人情相谙，免致仓卒误事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1159972'>一、将佐须各熟知山川险易，道路远近，敌人情状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159972_comment'></div>所贵用兵料敌，不失机会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1159972'>一、将佐等须熟询康定中用兵次第，炮当日之失策，则可以致今日之得计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1159972'>一、兵分势弱，取胜必难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159972_comment'></div>仰本路经略总管熟议战守之兵，各有定数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159972_comment'></div>兵有定，将量力应敌，必求全胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159972_comment'></div>无若康定中，累为诱兵所陷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1159972'>一、沿边小堡寨若遇大寇，不能支吾，即检详前后处置，临时或须并入大寨，不管落贼癚便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1159972'>一、贼寇大入，更相赴救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159972_comment'></div>或逐路牵制，仰细详前后指挥处置，不得至时观望不进，有误大事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159972_comment'></div>及不得轻有举动，致有败衄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1159972'>一、常切选得力勾当事人，探候贼中事宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159972_comment'></div>如所报得实及致官军胜捷，一依前后赏格施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1159972'>一、行军赏罚，常须检详，所贵仓卒易为处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1159972'>一、所须财粮，常须计会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159972_comment'></div>运司计置有备，仍须体认边储难得丰备，不得非理妄用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1159972'>一、经略司机宜官常须编排检详本司前后文书，务要习熟齐整，缓急处置报应，有所依据，不致差失稽违，有误大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159972_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1159972'>一、机宜官不得与本路兵官过从给纳，及赴筵宴，有妨行遣文字。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1159972'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1159972_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年</a>　主弃绥州，诛种谔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　奏请陕西沿边牒送降到番部于宥州收管。作品：《奏令陕西沿边牒送降到番部于宥州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159965' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159965' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159965?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏令陕西沿边牒送降到番部于宥州<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159965")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159965_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159965'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159965'>麟府路军马司奏，昨有军前杀降到西界番部结胜欲走归西界事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159965_comment'></div>奉圣旨，结胜放罪，量支盘缠、结口券，转送与赞延路经略司，令保安军牒送宥州收管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159965_comment'></div>今来夏国累遣使诣阙，贡奉如旧，朝廷广推恩恕，务遂物情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159965_comment'></div>昨来捉降到夏国人口，违去本族，岂无怀土思归之心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159965_comment'></div>宜令逐路经略司并依此送保安军民，令牒送宥州收管者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1159965_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　上章论夏国册命事。具列夏人所作过，以为夏人须别具誓表，方可议封册之事。作品：《论夏国册命》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159966' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159966' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159966?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论夏国册命奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159966")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159966_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159966'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159966'>薛宗道至，若所赍表止是告哀，别无陈诉，及宗道于押伴官处别无传达言语，欲令孙眐因聚会款曲间，癨作己意问之云：先国主薨谢，今来何人继嗣达？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159966_comment'></div>他若云某人继嗣，即却问云：是先国主之何亲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159966_comment'></div>云是子，即便问云是嫡子否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159966_comment'></div>若云是嫡，即与更问云：先国主盛年弃世，今来嗣子必是㬠幼小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159966_comment'></div>他若有对，更随机问答之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159966_comment'></div>少间，即更说与自古外国必须中国册命者，方可取重于诸番。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159966_comment'></div>今来西夏以累世贡奉，故当册命嗣子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159966_comment'></div>然朝廷以夏国自嘉皊以来，于麟州界上掩杀郭恩，及于泾原侵掠同家堡子，后又于大顺城作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159966_comment'></div>有违誓表，如此非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159966_comment'></div>以至先帝上仙，不时来祭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159966_comment'></div>今上登极，亦不入贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159966_comment'></div>然朝廷曲示含容，尚存事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159966_comment'></div>而夏国终不省过，又于去年十一月中于顺宁寨界上诱引杀害却知保安军杨定等三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159966_comment'></div>如此不道，今来朝廷必未肯便行封册之礼，须是与夏国重别商议，再具誓表，约信丁宁，务存久远，方可商议别行封册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159966_comment'></div>若依前却有侵犯边境，贡奉不时，岂是恭顺和好之理？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159966_comment'></div>若宗道别分疏，即随其言以理折难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159966_comment'></div>若云某祗是赍表来告哀，不敢与闻他议，即且说与今来使还，须是子细说与本国知委，候议定，别具誓表来上，朝廷须有商量，亦是使人了事之功效也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1159966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159966'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_1159966_0'>⑴ 若表中已有告终称嗣之文，即直便问其嫡否。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159966_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　支持减河北营兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　奏减广南东西路戍兵。作品：《奏减广南东西路戍兵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏减广南东西路戍兵<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159967")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159967'>检会广南东西两路，景祐中，屯泊两路就粮本城兵三万四千馀人，治平三年兵共五万一千馀人，比景祐年多一万七千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159967_comment'></div>盖自皇祐侬贼事宜后来添屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159967_comment'></div>今贼平已久，岭外无事，屯兵尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159967_comment'></div>况广西税入至薄，粮饷不给，皆向内地转输而往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159967_comment'></div>加以北兵往戍，不习水土，每至岁满戍还，瘴死者十有三四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159967_comment'></div>此乃守臣务固事权，兵官希望酬奖，张皇边事，诳惑朝廷，虚屯兵甲，枉费钱粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159967_comment'></div>不早更张，必大困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159967_comment'></div>检唐制，岭南五府经略守兵裁一万五千馀人，向时亦无北兵屯戍，遇有蛮事，止发邻近镇兵以助攻御，事定则兵还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159967_comment'></div>至于两汉命将，曰楼船、下濑，并为征蛮，因事立名，事毕即已，未有久屯兵于炎瘴之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159967_comment'></div>况侬贼平定之后，守土者固当经度减省，以宽民力，复如往日平时，方为了事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159967_comment'></div>若但因循，坐视劳费，岂副选任之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159967_comment'></div>兼朝廷近省诸路冗兵，二广尤宜裁节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159967_comment'></div>兼今有臣僚上言广西设官屯兵、增置镇寨事甚详悉，欲并下本路经略安抚张田子细相度，且擘画利害闻奏，并下广东经略使亦详前项事理，具本路见屯兵甲、合行减省利害奏闻。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1159967'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1159967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　以为不必理会契丹通刺两属人户充义军之举。作品：《奏雄州边事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159968' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159968' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159968?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏雄州边事<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159968")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159968_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159968'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159968'>张利一等奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159968_comment'></div>北界待通刺两属人户充义军，至时只行公牒理办，必恐不济事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159968_comment'></div>如北界果是刺丁手臂，欲却勾追照验，逐旋发遣赴唐、邓等州，给与田土居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159968_comment'></div>或乞却于两属人户上等内拣少壮之人，刺「雄州义勇」字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159968_comment'></div>已作圣旨，令张利一等更切密细体探。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159968_comment'></div>如果欲拣刺两属户充义军，即速行公牒，以理□婉顺争执止约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159968_comment'></div>况闻北界近里已通刺了义军，独迁延未便刺两属人充军，乃是自顾事体行之非便，故迟留未决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159968_comment'></div>又闻向前亦曾如此通刺，寻亦中辍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159968_comment'></div>兼据探报云，恐以为名，意在乞銂而已约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159968_comment'></div>若更以道理计术沮之，事应自罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159968_comment'></div>设若全不顾道理，刺却两属人户充军，亦于他无利，止是转失人心。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1159968_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　乞使者刘怤早过界。作品：《奏乞刘怤早过界》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159969' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159969' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159969?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞刘怤早过界<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159969")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159969_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159969'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159969'>臣准御批劄子，可据陆诜奏，如有宥州人来计会刘籅过界之时，须是应日令疾速如常前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159969_comment'></div>若谅祚以种谔事发，杀其使人，即举兵更是有名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159969_comment'></div>万一事或不来，则朝廷应期遣使往来，岂是中国先生闲隙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159969_comment'></div>臣伏详圣虑深切事机，已依准即时行下延州，令刘籅应日如常前去，不得稽留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159969_comment'></div>况自古兵交，使在其间，蠢尔夷狄，岂敢轻犯王人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159969_comment'></div>兼于他无济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159969_comment'></div>陆诜此奏，诚是疏阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159969_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1159969'>万一过虑，如唐时番贼执汉使犯边者，此亦无虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159969_comment'></div>向差刘籅，众谓此人坚悫有守，必能自保忠义。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1159969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1068&endYear=1068')">1068年</a>　反对修复延州北金明寨。作品：《论修复延州北金明寨》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一八。）</span><div id='poem_1159970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论修复延州北金明寨奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1068年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159970")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159970'>按《聚米图经》，延州之境，东自长宁塞以次带西北至德靖寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159970_comment'></div>沿边回远，接贼界地分约七百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159970_comment'></div>旧分三路，中路塞门大川，直至延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159970_comment'></div>北至金明、栲栳两寨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159970_comment'></div>上又分路东入安远寨<span class='inlineComment2'>（自背水川入。）</span>，北入塞门寨<span class='inlineComment2'>（自塞门川入。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159970_comment'></div>沿边虽是山谷，然诸处并有大路通行人马，有浑州、塞门两川，最是宽平，易行大军<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159970_comment'></div>故先朝常保芦关，以扼其冲要<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159970_comment'></div>自贼陷塞门、安远、金明、栲栳寨，熟户部落荡然一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159970_comment'></div>今虽脩复金明寨，然徒有城壁，其冲要之地，多陷于虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159970_comment'></div>加之蕞耳州城，不可不别为处置。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159970_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159970'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_1159970_0'>⑴ 先朝五路八界，范廷召自塞门川进军。向时元昊大入延州，亦自塞门川安然直至城下。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_1159970_0'>⑵ 芦关在塞门北十五里，所以置塞门者，守此关耳。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159970_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　乞禁止汉人与西人私相交易。作品：《乞禁止汉人与西人私相交易》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1159973' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159973' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159973?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞禁止汉人与西人私相交易奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159973")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159973_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159973'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159973'>检会累降指挥，沿边诸路经略安抚使严切禁止汉人与西界私相交易博买，非不丁宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159973_comment'></div>近访闻诸路沿边因循习俗，不切禁止，常有番汉私相交易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159973_comment'></div>盖缘官司不遵守条贯，明行赏罚，是致全无畏避，及无人发摘告陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159973_comment'></div>近又闻西界不稔，斛食倍贵，大段将牛、羊、青盐等物衷私博斛斗入番，不惟资假盗粮，兼妨沿边及时计收置籴军储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159973_comment'></div>今欲再下逐路经略安抚司，依累降指挥施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1159973_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月</a>　富弼罢判亳州，荐彦博为相。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　以陈升之为相，彦博拒班于陈升之之上。作品：《答诏札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　乞解枢柄，守外郡。作品：《乞罢重任·第一札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　言青苗钱不便，请罢之。作品：《言青苗钱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二○。）</span><div id='poem_1159979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言青苗钱奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159979")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159979'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159979'>臣位忝三公，职当论道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159979_comment'></div>事有所闻，深亏圣政，默而不言，则上负陛下眷倚之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159979_comment'></div>近日以来，中外喧传，以诸路散青苗钱，深为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159979_comment'></div>臣比不知本末，今访知其由，深可惊骇，不近人情，有玷圣化，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159979_comment'></div>臣谓此事岂可不达圣聪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159979_comment'></div>皆云朝廷主张，及诸路所差之官承禀风旨，威福<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作「逼」）</span>州郡，故无有敢言于朝廷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159979_comment'></div>臣会见河北转运司谇开折提举常平官约束条目云：所散青苗钱，每十户以上结成一保，须第三等以上有物力户充甲头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159979_comment'></div>此乃是恐向去收纳不足，勒令上户填纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159979_comment'></div>又欲散与坊郭人户，其钱不得过抵当家业所直价钱之半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159979_comment'></div>且谓之青苗钱，却支与坊郭户，皆是广图利息，不顾道理，兹岂常平散銂之旧法，朝廷救济之本意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159979_comment'></div>此法于乡村之民，行之惟旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159979_comment'></div>夏秋成熟，折还斛㪷丝帛，即谓之举放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159979_comment'></div>若癨令纳本利见钱，即谓之课钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159979_comment'></div>将新抵旧，迁延岁时，诸般折还，未尝了足，以其利债负，官司不许受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159979_comment'></div>今乃官自为之，从古以来，未尝有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159979_comment'></div>岂当圣朝而行此法，殊乖理道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159979_comment'></div>况闻乡县之民，有穷迫之甚者，即皆愿请钱，一时聊济窘急，向去必难填偿，此乃下民从来常态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159979_comment'></div>州县既以逋欠，必从散行催督，追呼笞责，何所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159979_comment'></div>兼闻诸路州县之民，犹有积欠税租贷粮，并预支䌷绢钱数甚多，将来一并催纳，何由取济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159979_comment'></div>所散官钱，又成积欠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159979_comment'></div>提举之官，徼冀旌赏，务成功利，剥下媚上，何恤于人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159979_comment'></div>州县承风，不敢申理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159979_comment'></div>臣恐缘此烦扰，必致兴起事端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159979_comment'></div>所有提举官，乞下本路勘验事件状，特行朝典，以戒非理聚銂之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159979_comment'></div>《书》曰：「商炮不远，在夏后之世」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159979_comment'></div>臣不敢以远事證之，且以唐开元末用宇文融、杨慎矜、王鵵等二十馀人，建中初用赵赞、陈京之策，百方裒銂，剥下害民，归怨于上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159979_comment'></div>当时执政议臣，以癚佞结党，专以财利媚上，方被宠信，不敢指言其非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159979_comment'></div>惟张说、陆贽苦言之，不蒙听纳，仍遭疏斥，驯致禄山、泾师之乱，鲜不由斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159979_comment'></div>《礼》云：「与其有聚銂之臣，宁有盗臣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159979_comment'></div>信不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159979_comment'></div>方今朝廷清明，表里无事，以天下之广，财赋所入，比之祥符以前，其增有及倍者，亦可谓无遗利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159979_comment'></div>若以用度稍乏，自当减节冗费，省罢不急之务，不作无益之事，济之以俭，示民不奢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159979_comment'></div>百姓自足，君孰与不足？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159979_comment'></div>《易》曰：「节以制度，不伤财，不害民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159979_comment'></div>此之谓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159979_comment'></div>夫与治同道罔不兴，与乱同事罔不亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159979_comment'></div>陛下视开元之末与建中之初，所用宇文融、杨慎矜、赵赞、陈京之法，治之道邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159979_comment'></div>乱之事邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159979_comment'></div>兹固不言可知，诚可为圣朝之商炮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159979_comment'></div>近时以来，中外臣僚上言兴利者甚众，大抵希时痈进，妄作者多，徒自纷纭，必寡成事，伏愿一切罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159979_comment'></div>惟内外计臣尤须慎选，州县长吏得忠厚廉良之人，台阁近臣无辸邪朋党之士，则不治自治，太平可期，陛下可以垂衣端拱而化成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159979_comment'></div>臣愚不识忌讳，发于至诚，昧冒以闻，伏增惶惧陨越之至<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1159979'></div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1159979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159979'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_41_1159979_0'>⑴ 《文潞公文集》卷二○。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一一四，《历代名臣奏议》卷二六七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159979_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年</a>　以神宗熙宁二年“期年听去”之旨，坚求补外。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年3月</a>　以拣退禁军不便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年5月</a>　以何郯提举成都府玉局观非当。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年8月己卯</a>　斩环庆路钤辖李信、庆州东路都巡检刘甫。彦博暴庆州帅李复圭妄奏李信、刘甫之罪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年11月</a>　奏国家承平，当刑用中典。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年12月</a>　奏差麟州、府州军马司元定得力将官领兵会种谔。作品：《差麟府军马司元定得力将民领兵会种谔奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160262' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160262' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160262?labeling=true' target='_blank'>差麟府军马司元定得力将官领兵会种谔奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁三年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160262")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160262_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160262'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160262'>欲令公弼如谔所请，速差麟府军马司元定得力将官领兵会谔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160262_comment'></div>仍多募乡导，远设斥堠，无致堕贼奸计。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1160262_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年1月</a>　举任逸。作品：《举任逸》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160230?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举任逸劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160230")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160230'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160230'>臣切见都官员外郎、通判邓州任逸赋性明敏，临事精详，臣今保举本官堪充皗陟繁难任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160230_comment'></div>如擢用后犯正入己赃，及不如举状，臣甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160230_comment'></div>伏候进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160230_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年2月</a>　议茶法之弊。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年3月</a>　反对开修漳河。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　以斩捕庆州叛卒功，赏蕃将赵余庆等。彦博以为蕃官赏不宜过厚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　以朝廷施为当以静重为先，兼采众论，慎于更张。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　言行交子不便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　言保甲扰民。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　言祖宗法制具在，不须更张以失人心。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　论兵制不宜遽有更易。作品：《论本朝兵政》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二○。）</span><div id='poem_1159985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论本朝兵政奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159985")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159985'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159985'>臣向因进对，蒙询及点民兵利害，臣与吴充即时略具大旨上对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159985_comment'></div>然而天威之下，顷刻之间，故未详悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159985_comment'></div>臣退而复思，自陛下临御以来，焦劳庶政，以兵者大事，尤所垂意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159985_comment'></div>三四年前，枢密院检录得开宝初至治平中内外兵马大数，颇甚详备，遂议酌中定为永额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159985_comment'></div>比至道前即差多，方庆历中即颇减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159985_comment'></div>内壮根本，外护边陲，去冗留精，适用损费，蒐补训练，皆有条理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159985_comment'></div>又以三路邻于羌胡，即有属户、蕃兵、弓箭手之类，以至次边州军，尽置义勇，缓急调发，以应征防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159985_comment'></div>若守将处之得宜，经久必无阙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159985_comment'></div>兼向时诸路郡县额外增置弓箭手，亦欲防虞盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159985_comment'></div>如此纪纲，臣以谓深协方今之宜，颇得备预之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159985_comment'></div>设有未至，或有废坠，即为弥缝振举之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159985_comment'></div>恭惟太祖、太宗之定天下也，止用此兵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159985_comment'></div>真宗、仁宗、英宗之守天下也，亦用此兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159985_comment'></div>累圣相承而无异道，历年弥久而无异法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159985_comment'></div>故臣以谓协当今之宜，得备预之理，有未至而废坠者，弥缝振举之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159985_comment'></div>今陛下以睿圣之德，承祖宗隆盛之业，中原之人，不识兵戈者几百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159985_comment'></div>历观前古致治，未有如此之安且久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159985_comment'></div>故生齿繁多，逾于二汉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159985_comment'></div>封疆广远，过于三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159985_comment'></div>所谓民不改聚，地不改辟，施之仁政而不烦扰之，则太平之效，又何如焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159985_comment'></div>陛下必欲舍此而别求治道，以致太平，更易兵制，以张威武，固非臣愚所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159985_comment'></div>况臣备位枢府，所主唯兵，不能上副盛意，委曲经画，尸禄之责，所不敢逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159985_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣前后累上章奏，听解枢机之重柄，并还将相之印绶，得以散秩，俾守外郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159985_comment'></div>从愚臣知止之分，全朝廷退人之理，臣不胜大幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159985_comment'></div>然臣久蒙天地之恩，敢忘犬马之报！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159985_comment'></div>窃谓兵民犹水，水能载舟，亦能覆舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159985_comment'></div>禁暴戢兵，武之七德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159985_comment'></div>不戢自焚，自古所戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159985_comment'></div>凡更制维御之方，深愿慎之重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159985_comment'></div>区区之诚，庶补万一，冒犯宸听，臣不任陨越惶惧之至。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1159985'></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1159985_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　乞令泾原路经略使体量保毅军利害。作品：《奏陕西保毅军利害》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1159974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏陕西保毅军利害<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159974")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159974'>据泾州保毅军人户程奉先等状，乞除放保毅军及乞免放送纳见钱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159974_comment'></div>检会熙宁二年八月终，据陜西沿边四路经略使与转运使薛向分析擘画到逐处保毅利害，看详赞延、环庆两路保毅军皆是于人丁上点差，寻并拨并充义勇外，泾原、秦凤两路保毅从初并于人户地亩上件差，只有相承祖名，元无正丁充役，皆是临时众户依地亩合钱顾人充役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159974_comment'></div>每遇典卖地土，于契帖上开坐，合著保毅分数，随地推送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159974_comment'></div>及至应役之时，出助钱数多不齐足，经官理索，即勾集典卖众户管认分摊，极烦追扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159974_comment'></div>寻牒两路保毅五千馀人，更不勾追，只令合著保毅每一名共纳钱三贯文，各于税簿内开坐，合著分数随夏税，只于本州县送纳见钱，不得支移折变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159974_comment'></div>如遇典卖地土，亦依分数于契内开坐，如两税法割移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159974_comment'></div>其纳到保毅钱，别作一项桩封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159974_comment'></div>如本路有修城或随军差役，却将上件钱顾人充役，即不得别将支用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159974_comment'></div>自行下此指挥后，秦凤路已依准施行，公私为便，别无词讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159974_comment'></div>惟泾原路据人户状称，乞依旧充役，免放纳钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159974_comment'></div>寻降指挥，例与减钱一贯，每名只共纳钱二贯文去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159974_comment'></div>今又据程奉先等状，乞免纳见钱，及乞除放保毅军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159974_comment'></div>体量得自前保毅人员与逐州典利在轮差保毅在州占使，因缘侵渔，弊痈不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159974_comment'></div>今欲令本路经略使更切体量利害，如果是本路保毅人户纳钱不便，即却令依旧充保毅，非时不得勾抽在州县及诸官下占使，除大段修筑城寨及随军般运军须，即得勾抽差役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159974_comment'></div>所有自前已纳不拆保毅钱，具数封桩，抵充和顾夫匠，修完城壁。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1159974'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1159974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　奏西夏誓诏事。作品：《奏西夏誓诏事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　乞益、利钤辖司定刑狱时，不再据彦博庆历六年川蜀饥灾之时权宜公牒，别定钤辖司画一条贯。作品：《乞别定益利钤辖司画一条贯》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1159977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞别定益利钤辖司画一条贯奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159977")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159977'>臣勘会益、利钤辖司以所部去朝廷远，承前体例，事由便宜裁决，所以上体倚寄之重，亦以安服远人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159977_comment'></div>二广虽亦遐远，权其事体，轻重不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159977_comment'></div>均顺之事，耳目未远，故朝廷择守，比他蕃镇绝重，举西南事一以委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159977_comment'></div>庆历六年臣知益州，时属饥蔺，列郡多事，贼盗兴起，刑狱淹延，事稍有疑，例欲奏决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159977_comment'></div>臣勘会得益、利路钤辖司多是承例酌情，便宜区断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159977_comment'></div>寻曾牒辖下州军，今后勘到合行奏听敕旨公案，且先申当司，以凭相度，其间有别无疑虑，或情轻法重，可以末减，情重法轻当从严断者，率皆便宜决遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159977_comment'></div>内有事状必难裁处，方敢奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159977_comment'></div>兼朝廷不以为非，在川蜀甚以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159977_comment'></div>迩来事体，与昔颇殊，处置之间，或多龃龉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159977_comment'></div>今本路提刑司累奏乞别定钤辖司画一条贯，犹恐本路钤辖司今来依旧引用臣庆历六年川蜀饥蔺之时权宜公牒，致监司官频有论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159977_comment'></div>欲乞送刑法司依本路提刑司别定钤辖司画一条贯，所贵经久遵守施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159977_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1159977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　论用人。作品：《论用人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一九。）</span><div id='poem_1159978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论用人奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159978")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159978'>臣屡被德音，将来西事宁息，更须精择守边之臣，积粟训兵，为经久之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159978_comment'></div>此乃陛下恭绍祖宗之丕基，慎守盈成之大法，将欲跻斯民于富贵，致天下于太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159978_comment'></div>臣退思之，不胜欣抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159978_comment'></div>又思以虚薄孱拙，不能上副陛下孜孜求治之意，伏增悚惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159978_comment'></div>今所择边臣，虽未得周才及已试之效，但思虑精审，不轻举妄动以求徼幸，茍图进身，则已善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159978_comment'></div>复能训兵积粟，节用爱民，恩威兼著，将使夷狄怀附，非但不敢侵侮而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159978_comment'></div>兹所谓长城巨屏，致朝廷高枕无虞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159978_comment'></div>若一用轻险躁妄之人，使之守边，为国生事，以规身利，则边无宁谧之岁，兵无休偃之时，中外扰然，民不聊生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159978_comment'></div>臣谓有唐天宝、建中之难，可为龟炮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159978_comment'></div>开元初，明皇励精求治，任姚、宋为相，驯致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159978_comment'></div>当时不赏边功，以防生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159978_comment'></div>及天宝之际，林甫、国忠作相，引用匪人，布在朝列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159978_comment'></div>时以承平既久，才力富盛，于是邀功之将务恢封略，以甘上心，欲荡灭契丹，剪除吐蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159978_comment'></div>丧师者失万而言一，胜敌者获一而言万，宠锡之极，骄矜遂增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159978_comment'></div>哥舒翰统西方二帅，安禄山统东方三帅，践更之卒，俱授官名，郡县之积，罄为禄山秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159978_comment'></div>于是骄将锐卒，萃于二统，边陲势强，朝廷体弱，禄山一唱，中原荡析。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159978_comment'></div>元和中，宰相李绛亦对宪宗云：「开元之末，癚臣说以兴利，武夫说以开边，天下劳役，以致大盗窃发，两都覆没」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159978_comment'></div>宪宗又尝问侍臣建中之难，朱泚盗据宫阙，德宗播迁梁汉，致乱之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159978_comment'></div>宰臣李吉甫对曰：「德宗之初，躬行节俭，任崔皊甫作相，动遵至道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159978_comment'></div>及皊甫殁，继其任者或非其人，忠谏不闻，小人乘间邀功，便已茍媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159978_comment'></div>当时以为河朔未宾，宜用力取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159978_comment'></div>甘言先入，主德致惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159978_comment'></div>是时国材不足，赵赞司国计，纤细刻急，括率京师商贾富民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159978_comment'></div>又谏官陈京献策税屋间架，立法峻急，人情愁怨，遂致泾师叛乱，鸾舆播迁，实由轻用兵，信小人剥下之谋，以致危乱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159978_comment'></div>是二臣者皆愿宪宗追念前朝之失，以为元龟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159978_comment'></div>臣今伏闻德音，以西事宁息之后，慎择边帅，为经久之制，实安边息民之远图，乃驯致太平之长策，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159978_comment'></div>然尚虑有邀功生事之将，希时取合之臣，睶为甘言，上惑睿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159978_comment'></div>伏望陛下炮前古治乱之由，更加详察，或付之外廷，公议可否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159978_comment'></div>兼枢密院每进拟用人，陛下累云：某人好作事，可用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159978_comment'></div>某人不肯作事，不可用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159978_comment'></div>臣愚以谓事有可作而不作，诚为过矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159978_comment'></div>未可作而作，失其宜矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159978_comment'></div>不可作而妄作，非惟害事，实害治道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159978_comment'></div>夫下之人不从上令而从上好，上好是焉，下有甚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159978_comment'></div>且中人常情，鲜克守经，趣时希旨，从上所好，则必勉强作为，不计后之利害，止图一时侥痈者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159978_comment'></div>伏望陛下察其言，观其行，原其始，要其终，可行而行，可作而作，庶无后害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159978_comment'></div>比者臣以刘邵《人物志》进说，未审陛下以谓如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159978_comment'></div>臣以邵之书主于详察人物，于任官择才之法，有可观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159978_comment'></div>故其序云：「明王之宜玩，宰相之宜览」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159978_comment'></div>又曰：「人之质量，中和最贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159978_comment'></div>中和之质必平淡无味，故能调成五材，变化应节」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159978_comment'></div>是以观人察质，必先察其平淡而后求其聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159978_comment'></div>至于人主任材，亦贵平淡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159978_comment'></div>若道不平淡，与一才同好，则一才处权，众才失任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159978_comment'></div>夫一才处权，则辸邪之人枉道附离而希进，朋比之风扇矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1159978_comment'></div>众才失任，则端方之士守分卷怀而思退，忠正之路梗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1159978_comment'></div>然则于任人求治之道，必有所偏，偏则必有所害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1159978_comment'></div>传曰：「远佞人，放郑声」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1159978_comment'></div>夫佞者，才智之称，盖邪佞之人，必有小小才智以饰身而干进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1159978_comment'></div>其事君也，务纳小忠、兴小利以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1159978_comment'></div>夫小忠必为大忠之贼，小利必为大利之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1159978_comment'></div>茍人主不早辨之，终必致于祸乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1159978_comment'></div>如圣人之于去佞，其戒尤为深切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1159978_comment'></div>《书》曰：「在知人，在安民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1159978_comment'></div>知人则哲，安民则惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1159978_comment'></div>能哲而惠，何忧乎巧言孔壬」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1159978_comment'></div>伏愿陛下贵平淡之道以用人，使群才不失其任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1159978_comment'></div>推哲惠之心以去佞，使群邪不干于正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1159978_comment'></div>尧舜所以致治而于变时雍者，由斯道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1159978_comment'></div>臣备位枢近，内省尸素，思竭区区，上裨圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1159978_comment'></div>干冒旒冕，伏候严诛。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1159978'></div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1159978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159978'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_24_1159978_0'>⑴ 所论天宝、建中事，皆出《唐书》，非臣附以臆说。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159978_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　乞守外藩。作品：《陈乞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三三。）</span><div id='poem_1160091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160091?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈乞堂弟大同西京差遣奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160091")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160091'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160091'>臣先准敕，于西京立家庙四室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160091_comment'></div>臣多在阙下守官，或外守方面，则西京常有子弟三两人在彼守官，以奉家庙四仲祭祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160091_comment'></div>今以臣劄子并丁母忧解官持服，并无子弟在西京守官奉祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160091_comment'></div>今有臣亲堂弟朝请郎大同，近因相州签判得替，欲望圣慈乞差充西京一合入差遣，所贵家庙岁时得人奉祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160091_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1160091_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年6月</a>　为明堂礼仪使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　乞河北监牧使周革罢兼提点刑狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　与王安石争论王韶言荒田及市易事，以为当罪韶。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年8月</a>　与王安石争论王韶招降西羌事，不欲招附西羌。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年11月</a>　请修中太一宫以简质。作品：《言修中太一宫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二○。）</span><div id='poem_1159984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言修中太一宫奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1071年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159984")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159984'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159984'>臣伏见修建太一宫，为民祈福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159984_comment'></div>臣闻太一，天神之贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159984_comment'></div>天道贵质，凡所营缮，谓宜简质，不务雕镂之巧，不事金碧之华，不重费，不太劳，不日成之，神明安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159984_comment'></div>虔洁之诚，内充天人之心，交感神应之福，其理必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159984_comment'></div>臣又见累年已来，禁中营造不已，般运木石，鸠集丁匠，殆无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159984_comment'></div>既有专切提举修内司，复置都大提举内中修造司，诚恐所司各以宏丽取悦上心，一作未毕，一作复兴，新旧相形，不极不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159984_comment'></div>国财民力，岂易支供？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159984_comment'></div>臣伏见陛下督责水官，以利农亩，必思夏禹卑宫室，尽力乎沟洫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159984_comment'></div>励精庶政，勤恤民隐，必思汉文罢露台，思百家之产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159984_comment'></div>臣伏愿陛下亟敕中外，应不急营造，一切权罢，即国用无穷，民力稍宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159984_comment'></div>臣又见继圣堂，祖宗燕射之地，今为造弩桩所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159984_comment'></div>运斧斤，置硄锻，喧烦亵渎，理恐非宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159984_comment'></div>《诗》云：「维桑与梓，必恭谨止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159984_comment'></div>况祖宗之旧迹乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159984_comment'></div>欲乞将制造弩桩移置他所，或归之有司，则重明丽正之廷，加之严洁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159984_comment'></div>奉先思孝之道，益以光显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159984_comment'></div>臣职在枢莞，主调兵匠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159984_comment'></div>官忝论道，义当献纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159984_comment'></div>区区下诚，伏望采察。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1159984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1159984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年12月</a>　与王安石争论俞龙珂及旺巴奇等举种内属事，持反对态度。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年12月</a>　请许降羌去留自便。作品：《言降羌事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二○。）</span><div id='poem_1159983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏降羌事<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159983")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159983'>李宪到臣处，具说赵卨为降羌去住事有所未便者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159983_comment'></div>臣以朝廷务推恩信，不使一物失所，许其去留自便，如天地之大，旷然无间，在于人情，必当感悦，书之史册，固为盛事，更复何疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159983_comment'></div>但令帅臣分明晓谕群羌，知朝廷恩意，欲去欲住，各从其愿，于理甚安，不当改易前命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159983_comment'></div>若但令只询问去年正月以来捉降到西羌，尤为简便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159983_comment'></div>为连日节假并宴，未及面奏，伏虑迟延，先具此奏闻，候至六日与中书同呈文字次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159983_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1159983'>环庆等路，皆不云未便，必恐已行前命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159983_comment'></div>兼河东经略司奏，捉到易浪瘅结愿归夏国，已牒宥州去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159983_comment'></div>又云：结胜却不愿归西界，亦当不须强遣，皆如朝廷指挥<span class='inlineComment2'>（《文潞公文集》卷二○。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1159983'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　乞解枢柄，守便州。作品：《乞罢重任札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年2月</a>　议木征言王韶违誓约事，彦博以为当专用郭逵，不当既用郭逵，又专以王韶招纳蕃部，致事任不专。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年5月</a>　反对保甲养马。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　论马监不可废。作品：《论监牧事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　谓张穆之生事邀功。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　不欲赐青唐大首领俞龙珂官赏过厚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　以文盈关乃险阨处，不可外属通远军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　王存破荡奄东不顺命熟户，彦博不欲以军赏待王存等。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年6月</a>　以逃去熟户中曾体问不愿归者须行法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年7月</a>　与王安石争雄州乡巡弓手事。以为不当罢乡巡弓手。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石争论逃走禁军处置事。以为当严惩逃走禁军，不宜轻改军法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石议雄州张利一修馆驿事，以为既修则不必拆毁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石议雄州张利一言罢乡巡弓手后，恐契丹移口铺占两属地事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石争河东保甲事。彦博等但欲为义勇、强壮，不欲别名保甲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年8月</a>　与王安石争夏国进表但谢恩不设誓事。欲夏国盟誓。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石争北人称“送纳”事。以为见无礼于君，当争之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年9月</a>　北界欲以兵来立口铺。彦博等欲争令拆却。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　以添差弓手事为当。认为口铺事当争，不须因惧用兵而一味示弱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与王安石争立西蕃结吴延征事，以木征若不受代，则恐用兵，以略近勤远非义。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年10月</a>　奏市易司与下民争利，致华州山崩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年11月</a>　支持以谙熟西事之张诜知庆州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　以台官张商英言枢密使副党庇密院吏人任远事，彦博与吴充、蔡挺不复入院，遣吏送印于中书。作品：《论台官言西府事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二一。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　论进筑河州事。以为不可。作品：《言洮河》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二○。）</span><div id='poem_1159982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>言洮河奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159982")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159982'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159982'>臣窃闻议论，欲至来春进筑河州，渐恢远略，臣窃思之，以为未可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159982_comment'></div>盖熙州初犹未完固，西蕃内附，尚要抚绥，积粟未丰，屯兵虽众，未宜多事，恐累成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159982_comment'></div>臣以谓且须增固熙城，使有保民之利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159982_comment'></div>安存蕃部，弥坚向汉之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159982_comment'></div>仓廪丰盈，士马壮健，以守则固，以战则强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159982_comment'></div>根本既深，枝叶自茂，然后洮河之役，可以指顾而就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159982_comment'></div>今欲务速，臣窃深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159982_comment'></div>古人谓「欲速则不达，见小利则大事之不成」，又云「劳于服远，不若脩近」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159982_comment'></div>斯言可炮，在理必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159982_comment'></div>夫趣时希旨，人之甚利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159982_comment'></div>犯颜违意，人之甚害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159982_comment'></div>中人之情，鲜不为利，多是顾身谋而谄说，岂肯为国计而危言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159982_comment'></div>臣待罪之所，地兼将相，若括囊无言，仰屋窃睵，辜祖宗之奖擢，负陛下之倚任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159982_comment'></div>是敢因事极论，违众立议，庶几万一有补涓毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159982_comment'></div>陛下以臣为纳忠报国，幸赐采择；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159982_comment'></div>以臣为害成沮事，甘俟诛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159982_comment'></div>臣无任惶恐陨越之至，谨具奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1159982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　陈升之拜枢密相。大敕系衔文彦博下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年</a>　与曾公亮有唱和，有诗记之。作品：《伏睹致政太傅侍中曾鲁公答枢密谏议吴留题斋阁诗依韵和呈》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　和枢密副使吴充频有唱和。作品：《和副枢吴谏议上元夜从驾至集禧观》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span>《和副枢吴谏议寄题广化寺东轩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span>《窃知今日于家园种山芋辄成拙诗奉呈副枢谏议》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span>《新酿酴醾酒送吴蔡二副枢》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年3月</a>　王素卒。彦博为挽词二首悼念之。作品：《故尚书懿敏王公挽词2》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_495133' class='_poem'><div
