href='/Writing/495132?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495132_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495132'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495132'>蚤预朋从谈燕熟，晚陪枢筦岁时多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495132'>心如金石坚无改，声似埙篪久更和。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495132'>丹凤临池犹未浴，白驹逢隙已先过。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495132'>相门馀庆簪缨盛，继述皆同谷与傩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495132_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495132'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495132_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　论保马。以为非其时。作品：《论保马》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1159996' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159996' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159996?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论保马奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159996")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159996_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159996'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159996'>诸州郡坊郭第四等、县郭第三等、乡村第二等以上户，生计从容，皆须养马，以代徒步之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159996_comment'></div>其物力高，则养马愈多，此皆不待官中劝率召募，固已家有而户畜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159996_comment'></div>若先时更使等第畜马，定以疋数，须壮嫩及格尺者，居常任民乘骑出入，岁时亦不得勾点烦挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159996_comment'></div>一旦官中须要，给以元契之直，可旦暮而集，人自乐输，比之急暴而科买，利害不侔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159996_comment'></div>今四等以上人户，类出役钱，所出役钱之多，悉在上等人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159996_comment'></div>今若蠲减上等租税，则下等人户所出，不充顾役之用，必见阙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159996_comment'></div>民既知缓急必取马于民，安得不家收户畜，以应一日之督责哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159996_comment'></div>丁产簿法以三岁一造，今非其时，又频岁灾伤，民流徙者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159996_comment'></div>今若非时重造，徒成搔扰，若同候至丰年，行之未晚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1159996_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　乞令诸路帅臣与副总管同议边事。作品：《乞令诸路帅臣与副总管同议边事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1159998' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159998?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令诸路帅臣与副总管同议边事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159998")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159998'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159998'>朝廷每差诸路副总管，所降宣命指挥，凡事并与都总管商量施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159998_comment'></div>访闻近年以来，逐路都总管凡关兵马公事及边防机宜，多是于经略司、安抚司一面行遣，副总管皆不预闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159998_comment'></div>况本路都总管如有边事，须合出兵，或不能自行，即遣副总管领兵出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159998_comment'></div>若本司公事及边防机宜素不预闻，临事仓卒，必不周详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159998_comment'></div>复又素不假以事权，临时节制，偏裨亦恐未甚仰服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159998_comment'></div>兼陜西诸路，因康定中自钤辖已下分定将官，训谏兵伍，盖欲兵将相谙，便于指踪号令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159998_comment'></div>然副总管实副大帅，尽护诸将，不曾分作次第将官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159998_comment'></div>亦闻近年以来，副总管亦分作第一将，即与偏裨一等，事体益轻，尤为非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159998_comment'></div>今欲下逐路经略安抚使、都总管，凡兵马公事及边防机宜，常须与副总管详熟同议，亦不得别作一将，却与钤辖都监等比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159998_comment'></div>所贵事体异于偏裨，缓急倚以出兵，可以节制诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159998_comment'></div>馀依前后宣命指挥，乃务协和，各副朝廷任使之意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1159998_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　辽使来贺同天节，生事妄请合使、副班为一，彦博以为不可许之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　坚求补外，终许彦博同天节（即四月十日）后听从外补。作品：《乞罢重任札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　同天节后，彦博又屡上札子，居家待命，坚请辞枢柄。作品：《乞罢重任札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年4月26日</a>　改判河阳。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0e9d796d8fde4a1f916ff75df2c2d38b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0e9d796d8fde4a1f916ff75df2c2d38b");'><span id='0e9d796d8fde4a1f916ff75df2c2d38b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>，75岁</div><div id='0e9d796d8fde4a1f916ff75df2c2d38b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　召彦博陪祠，并赐茶药。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月27日</a>　改判河南府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　奏刑狱枝蔓事。作品：《乞恤刑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1160016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞恤刑奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰三年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160016")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160016'>臣切见近年以来，中外刑狱颇有枝蔓淹延，大暑盛寒，缧系囹圄，其间岂无冤滞感伤和气？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160016_comment'></div>朝廷每至盛夏，必行疏决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160016_comment'></div>或水旱为灾，原减轻系，此圣慈钦恤之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160016_comment'></div>然守臣狱官鲜能上副陛下之意，有伤仁厚之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160016_comment'></div>夫刑者，所以辅教，圣人不得已而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160016_comment'></div>故三王任德不任刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160016_comment'></div>以德为阳，居大夏生成之时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160016_comment'></div>以刑为阴，居大冬不用之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160016_comment'></div>所施轻重，居然可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160016_comment'></div>臣不敢以经史远事言之，切以唐之宪宗，号为中兴，任德任刑，颇得其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160016_comment'></div>尝谓宰相曰：「于頔怀癚，劝朕任刑狱，朕失人心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160016_comment'></div>且圣人感人心而天下和平，人主而失人心，邦本何由宁固？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160016_comment'></div>臣谓今之牧守监司，宜得明惠厚重之人，宣布朝廷宽大之泽，施恺悌之政，变刻薄之风，则太平之隆，可垂拱而至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1160016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　乞凡有罪奏乞不赦原者，并送刑部据情理轻重定夺。作品：《论赦事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1160017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赦事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰三年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160017")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160017'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160017'>臣伏睹陛下躬行大享之礼，前期洁斋于路寝，朝谒于灵宫，孝享于太庙，乃格明堂，以严宗祀，祀礼之重，莫重于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160017_comment'></div>既而御端闱，孚大号，霈惠泽于天下，号令之重，莫重于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160017_comment'></div>然号令之出，在于必行，不惟其反。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160017_comment'></div>谨详辛巳赦文，释系缧，贷逋负，比常赦至宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160017_comment'></div>自杀人已死及监主自盗、官吏枉法外，罪无轻重，悉除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160017_comment'></div>而近岁以来，中外臣僚多不详罪犯与情理之轻重，皆乞遇赦不原，朝廷或从其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160017_comment'></div>臣恐轻重之间，有所未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160017_comment'></div>且臣下迎格赦令，则礼为不恭，朝廷遂从其请，则令有不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160017_comment'></div>臣乞今后凡有罪，奏乞不赦原者，并送刑部，候具狱上，一系朝廷临时特旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160017_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160017'>臣伏睹近降赦书，文官员犯罪，依条不以赦降原减者，许于刑部投状，具元犯闻奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160017_comment'></div>未断者案后声说取旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160017_comment'></div>盖朝廷必以情理轻重而区处之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1160017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月</a>　进史论。作品：《进史论》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1160018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160018?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进史论奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰三年九月进）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160018")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160018'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160018'>臣读汉史鱳错之策云：「五帝神圣，其臣莫能及，故自亲事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160018_comment'></div>臣谓错之言乖谬颇甚，因试论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160018_comment'></div>夫《易》之《乾》曰天道也、君道也，《坤》曰地道也、臣道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160018_comment'></div>天地既位，君臣之象著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160018_comment'></div>君臣交济，邦家之治隆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160018_comment'></div>而错乃云臣不及君，故自亲事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160018_comment'></div>然则古之圣帝明王，安用辅相而致治乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160018_comment'></div>所谓五帝者，尧、舜为圣之优，故仲尼删《诗》《书》，则断自唐虞，为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160018_comment'></div>二《典》之载，尧则有命羲和为天地四时之官，允矨百工，庶绩咸熙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160018_comment'></div>舜则命禹平水土，弃为稷官，契作司徒，鲇陶作士，垂为共工，益为朕虞，伯夷秩宗，夔典乐，龙纳言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160018_comment'></div>皆选于众而后用其人，各任以职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160018_comment'></div>且云「佥曰汝谐」，慎拣之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160018_comment'></div>所以百工允矨，熙帝之载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160018_comment'></div>如此，则尧舜果自亲事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160018_comment'></div>仲尼曰：「舜何为哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160018_comment'></div>端拱正南面而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160018_comment'></div>错所谓自亲事，岂非乖谬乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160018_comment'></div>若后之人君谓错言为是，乃以一身一心、两耳两目独任自用，以周天下之万务，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160018_comment'></div>又将使厥后自圣，无复察迩言好问之裕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160018_comment'></div>仲尼云「一言几于丧邦」者，谓人莫己若，则错之言亦几于兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160018_comment'></div>臣故著论深切以明之，庶几有所补益。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1160018_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年闰9月22日</a>　彦博子及甫换承事郎，为秘阁校理。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年闰9月23日</a>　陛辞。神宗留之禁中，面问彦博至和三年建储事。彦博奏其本末，与王同老所言合。神宗誉彦博为定策社稷之臣。作品：《对圣问》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1159995' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159995' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159995?labeling=true' target='_blank'>对圣问奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1080年闰9月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159995")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159995_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159995'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159995'>臣昨因登对圣问，为故王尧臣之子同老进状，陈述其父至和三年为参知政事日，与仁宗前曾与臣等乞立英宗皇帝为嗣，谓臣必知其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159995_comment'></div>臣即时略记忆当时大概上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159995_comment'></div>续圣旨，令臣作一文字述当时事实进呈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159995_comment'></div>臣记至和三年正月六日，仁庙服药，罢朝两月馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159995_comment'></div>是时以根本未立，中外人情未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159995_comment'></div>四月初，仁宗圣体康宁，始复御殿，中书辅臣愿念正二月中，禁中侍药，忧虑百端，尧臣乃与臣及刘沆、富弼切议曰：方今朝廷根本不可不早定，以安人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159995_comment'></div>时亦不暇与枢密院同谋，亦不敢显言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159995_comment'></div>臣以尧臣久居禁近，多知朝廷事，因谓之曰：「必得贤嗣，以厌人心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159995_comment'></div>尧臣曰：「岂不知养育于宫中者耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159995_comment'></div>臣应之曰：「久在外任，殊未悉宗室间事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159995_comment'></div>所谓育于宫中者，外亦传之，甚著而贤，得非以『萛』为名者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159995_comment'></div>兼臣不敢显言，以指书于案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159995_comment'></div>尧臣复以指书案，作下贯字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159995_comment'></div>臣等各言：「无易此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1159995_comment'></div>至上前伏奏，得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1159995_comment'></div>此大事，不可如常例退殿庐，令堂吏书圣旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1159995_comment'></div>刘沆云：「沆欲袖纸笔于上前亲书」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1159995_comment'></div>翌日，于垂拱殿呈进一两件常程文字，臣等四人共奏春中仁庙服药时事，中外人情非常忧恐，盖为储副未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1159995_comment'></div>乃引西汉故事，人主初即位，建储，今当以时立嗣，以固根本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1159995_comment'></div>臣等既叨辅相之重，当任社稷之大计也，乞赐开纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1159995_comment'></div>时仁宗渊默寡言，而欣然嘉奖曰：「知卿等尽忠，然大事，朕更熟思之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1159995_comment'></div>臣等恐迁延不决，乃再三论奏曰：「知臣莫若君，知子莫若父，料此重事，陛下必素垂意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1159995_comment'></div>兼常选贤者育于宫中，计无易此<span class='inlineComment2'>（臣等不敢斥名，欲仁宗自言之。）</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1159995_comment'></div>仁宗虽默，而首肯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1159995_comment'></div>臣等拜贺且谢，乞明谕圣旨，尧臣之语尤激切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1159995_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「既是大事，未可轻出，翌日当尽议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1159995_comment'></div>时五月，恐圣体热，仁宗初康复，旰食不便，内侍尽前，臣等且退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1159995_comment'></div>是日晚，臣等再聚议，为翌日必得旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1159995_comment'></div>且谓尧臣久居禁林，敏于文诏，请尧臣密作诏意，欲进呈施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1159995_comment'></div>尧臣然之，云归第乃密草诏意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1159995_comment'></div>然未及示臣等，曰：「此诏意尧臣不敢示人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1159995_comment'></div>既登对，复申前请，如昨日之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1159995_comment'></div>时臣在御榻之左，弼次之，沆在右，尧臣次之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1159995_comment'></div>尧臣越之而奏曰：「愿陛下早定此议，付外施行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1159995_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「朕意既已定矣，卿等无忧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1159995_comment'></div>臣等既得此意旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1159995_comment'></div>谓无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1159995_comment'></div>时亦旰矣，遂退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1159995_comment'></div>是年八月，臣等因枢密院阙官，议于上前，乞召韩琦充枢密使，盖以琦忠义，必能当重事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1159995_comment'></div>仁宗可之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1159995_comment'></div>自后继有议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1159995_comment'></div>未几，臣得请判河南，尧臣寻卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1159995_comment'></div>蝲绅间多知其忠于国计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1159995_comment'></div>臣所记忆当日之事，大概如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1159995_comment'></div>今蒙圣问，令臣条列之，犹恐遗忘，谨具进呈。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1159995'></div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1159995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年闰9月24日</a>　赐彦博筵于琼林苑，中书枢密院臣僚同赴。神宗亲为诗送彦博，章惇为作诗序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　王圭有诗相送。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　刘挚有诗相送。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年闰9月26日</a>　加彦博河东、永兴军节度使，固辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>　子宗道授承事郎。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d38048b321af4a4095f362b9ed6c5926_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d38048b321af4a4095f362b9ed6c5926");'><span id='d38048b321af4a4095f362b9ed6c5926_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>，79岁</div><div id='d38048b321af4a4095f362b9ed6c5926' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　入觐，神宗置酒垂拱殿，赐御樽亲劝彦博。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　神宗手诏谕彦博留过清明再还洛，为其特备二舟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　神宗问彦博养生之道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年2月</a>　举范祖禹。作品：《举范祖禹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举范祖禹劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰二年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160233")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160233'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160233'>臣切见奉议郎、编修《资治通炮》范祖禹，文行操守，为众所推，臣曾论荐堪文馆任用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160233_comment'></div>臣以谓古之用人，必因其器能，如祖禹之才，实堪文馆任用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160233_comment'></div>伏乞检臣前奏，特赐任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160233_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160233_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年2月丙戌</a>　乞每年于河南府公使库逐家庙岁祭寄造酒十石。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　赐宴于琼林苑，神宗亲制诗以赐彦博。苏颂等有和诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年3月2日</a>　为诗以谢神宗。作品：《臣伏蒙圣恩今月二日就琼林苑特遣中使宠赐御诗仰味圣言恭披宸翰曲推恩礼过奖愚臣感愧之深负荷弗克辄课愚陋恭和圣制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。苏颂《三月二日奉诏赴西园曲宴，席上赋呈致政开府太师三首》）</span><div id='poem_495035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>臣伏蒙圣恩今月二日就琼林苑特遣中使宠赐御诗仰味圣言恭披宸翰曲推恩礼过奖愚臣感愧之深负荷弗克辄课愚陋恭和圣制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年3月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495035")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495035'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495035'>老臣为感圣恩殊，趣治轻装觐帝居。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495035'>锡宴便藩亲凤扆，赐章重叠捧龟书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495035'>康时有志才终短，报国无功术已疏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495035'>身在洛阳心魏阙，愿倾丹恳上公车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495035'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年4月5日</a>　清明日，赐宴玉津园，彦博即宴赋诗以为别。王圭、蔡确、刘挚等有诗为献。作品：《清明日玉津园赐宴即席》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。王圭《送致政太师潞国文公以赐燕玉津园感恩述怀》；蔡确《清明日赴玉津园宴》；刘挚《清明日玉津园奉陪赐宴文太师》）</span><div id='poem_495032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>清明日玉津园赐宴即席<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495032")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_495032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495032'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495032'>节应桐华始，筵开禁苑新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495032'>推恩缘旧物，如惠及陈人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495032'>众乐闻天奏，同寅会柄臣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495032'>兰肴享丰洁，桂醑釂芳醇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495032'>覆育需云广，涵濡湛露均。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495032'>桑榆垂晚景，何路报尧仁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495032'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_495032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年4月6日</a>　神宗以彦博诗韵属和，就第赐彦博。王圭有和诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　彦博归洛阳日，赐宴琼林苑，彦博即席赋诗。王圭、苏颂、李籍、毕仲游、钱长卿等有诗为赠。作品：《西归日琼林苑赐宴即席》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。王圭《琼林苑御筵奉送致政太师潞国文公归西洛》；苏颂《次韵开府太师留别诸公》；苏颂《开府潞公太师得谢西归，谨赋七言四韵诗五首拜送》；刘挚《送致政太师归洛》；王安礼《谨赋五言一章赠别致政太师》）</span><div id='poem_495033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西归日琼林苑赐宴即席</a><span class='authorDate'>（1084年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495033")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495033'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495033'>窃禄叨荣四纪馀，退思侥倖亦无如。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495033'>趋朝再睹新宫省，解绂还归旧里庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495033'>报国丹心明皎皎，恋轩疲足去徐徐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495033'>群公尽出都门祖，盛事光于汉二疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495033'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495033_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='80c27813fa364bf1a7031a95dd1364b0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80c27813fa364bf1a7031a95dd1364b0");'><span id='80c27813fa364bf1a7031a95dd1364b0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1090')">1086-1090年</a>，81-85岁</div><div id='80c27813fa364bf1a7031a95dd1364b0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月</a>　赴阙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月</a>　赐彦博子贻庆金紫章服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年4月15日</a>　授彦博太师、平章军国重事。一月两赴经筵，六日一入朝，遇军国机要事，入预参决。俸赐依宰臣例。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　论差役法。作品：《论役法》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二六。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　乞罢详定局，只委户部详定役法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　令彦博独班起居，位在宰臣之上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年6月</a>　举楚建中、李之纯、唐义问、范育、杜纯、黄景。皆擢用。作品：《举楚建中等》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷四○。）</span><div id='poem_1160241' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160241' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160241?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举楚建中等劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160241")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160241_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160241'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160241'>臣昨在西京，蒙圣恩差勾当内东门梁惟简赍赐臣手诏，曲有咨询，臣勉竭愚虑上对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160241_comment'></div>仍询及臣之所知贤才，亟当论荐，用副柬求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160241_comment'></div>臣当时粗举三人应诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160241_comment'></div>以久在外藩，后来新进少所知识，容臣博访，续具奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160241_comment'></div>臣今蚤延和殿进对，蒙圣旨更有荐论，令进入文字来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160241_comment'></div>今有续具在外臣僚，皆是已试有效，可以因其所能而任之，伏乞圣明更赐采察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1160241'>一、正议大夫、天章阁待制致仕楚建中虽年逾七十，精力强明，累任重路转运使及三司判官、副使，环庆、真定路经略安抚使，在京主判剧司，皆有风绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1160241'>一、中散大夫、直龙图阁、知沧州李之纯累任转运使，忠厚淳正，颇有时誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1160241'>一、河北提点刑狱唐义问中正有守，恬于进趋，颇有学识，善议论，通时务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160241'>一、知秦州、直龙图范育曾为言事官，颇有学识，议论不屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1160241'>一、河北转运判官杜纯中正有守，累以公事黜降，众谓理直，终不自明，搢绅多称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1160241'>一、知怀州、朝散郎黄景学行敦笃，有古儒士之风，可备劝讲之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160241_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1160241'>右，谨具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160241_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1160241_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　西夏求兰州米脂等五寨，司马光欲与之。彦博论与光合。作品：《论西边事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1160027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论西边事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160027")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160027'>臣伏蒙太皇太后陛下、皇帝陛下不以老臣不才，以其逮事四朝，出入藩府垂五十年，追起于休退之中，令平章军国重事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160027_comment'></div>臣敢不极尽所蕴，上副虚伫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160027_comment'></div>臣于帘前累蒙宣谕，将来西人求复疆界，令与三省执政熟议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160027_comment'></div>臣以所议地界，不出二理：其一论义理曲直，其一计利害大小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160027_comment'></div>所谓论义理曲直者，昨者出兵取其地土，皆边臣望希功赏，欺罔朝廷，为国生事，取怨夷狄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160027_comment'></div>今若推朝廷恩信，因秉常诉求而赐与之，有以怀复夷狄之心，光大朝廷之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160027_comment'></div>所谓计利害之大小者，今所得堡寨并兰、会并荒徼沙漠之地，本无城邑人眕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160027_comment'></div>惟是朝廷创筑城垒，屯兵戍守，岁费百万以上，困竭中国生民膏血，以奉无用之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160027_comment'></div>但恐不能支久，却须自弃，如向时砮兀城之比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160027_comment'></div>其兰州本属董毡，夏人得之已三十八九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160027_comment'></div>董毡元不藉其地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160027_comment'></div>夏人得之已久，亦不曾筑堡戍守，只有一小颓废城堑，如中国荒僻村落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160027_comment'></div>朝廷不知，将谓如中国小小郡县，徒烦兵守，所费不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160027_comment'></div>兼会州又未知在甚处，盖是李宪当时怯懦，不曾领兵赴灵州城下，只领兵过兰州废垒之下，遂欺罔张大，云收复兰、会，以图茍免不至灵州城下军令之诛，遂误朝廷，以至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160027_comment'></div>臣亦闻议者谓地界，彼求而与之亦用兵，不与之亦用兵，语尤欺罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160027_comment'></div>但向去欲免主议，不与起衅之责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160027_comment'></div>且秉常来求我，如其意而得之，必须感戴恩德，三数年间，当且保无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160027_comment'></div>朝廷近经灵州、永乐不振之后，可以粗整齐兵势，完养民力，异时或有边事用兵，庶几有备无患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160027_comment'></div>今若不推恩赐信与其地，犬羊凶狠之性，因此不遂所求，便作点集酬报之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160027_comment'></div>朝廷方此多事之际，兵力未完，可得高枕乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160027_comment'></div>近年以来，为新进书生不晓蕃情、边事、兵政者，误朝廷多矣，愿陛下审察而详处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160027_comment'></div>老臣年过八十，感陛下厚恩，惟知竭尽补报，固无观望希进之言，不胜区区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160027_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1160027'>臣今检到祖宗以来处分边事诏书、西人事迹共几件进入，乞赐详览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160027_comment'></div>或曰：兰州宜如充国，可置屯田，添助兵食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160027_comment'></div>今若有田，多属蕃族，不可尽夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160027_comment'></div>向时王韶谓熙河可耕，以助兵食，人、牛、种子，徒有所费，终无所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160027_comment'></div>今闻转运司判官节减兰州岁计犹须一百馀万，又当计会知州并帅臣保认可以足用否。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1160027_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　为富弼求恩泽。作品：《举富绍庭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举富绍庭劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年七月十三日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160234")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160234'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160234'>臣切以故相富弼直道逢辰，昌言致主，始终一节，华夷具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160234_comment'></div>向与王安石同在中书，议论趣向不合，义难共事，乃请出藩，遂不待年，亟求致政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160234_comment'></div>闲居十稔，不幸亡殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160234_comment'></div>今闻配享神宗庙庭，公论极为允惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160234_comment'></div>今弼之子惟绍庭一名监中岳庙，伏望圣慈，以今来配享特推恩礼于弼之子孙，更赐优加录用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160234_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　论罢保马，修复马监事。并荐崔台符知相州。作品：《论监牧》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月</a>　司马光卒，彦博赠挽词四首。作品：《司马温公挽词4》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_495144' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495144' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495144?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司马温公挽词<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495144")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495144_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495144'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495144'>莫逆论交司马丈，君心知我我知君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495144'>同谋同道殊无间，一死一生今遂分。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495144'>八十衰翁如槁木，一千馀日是残曛。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495144'>前途若有相逢处，尚以英灵解世纷<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495144'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495144_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495144'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_495144_0'>⑴ 自注：公赍志而没，犹不忘利泽生民，心在王室。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495144_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495145' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495145' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495145?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495145_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495145'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495145'>留滞周南十五年，成书奏牍过三千。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495145'>东山方起为霖雨，大厦俄倾叹逝川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495145'>密有忠言如药石，别加优礼赐貂蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495145'>两宫痛悼<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>皆临奠，祗为皋夔志未宣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495145_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495145_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495146?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495146'>昔有乡贤阳<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>道州，亦闻比近有松楸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495146'>新阡便合开三径，同气相求好并游。<div id='poem_title_495147' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495147?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1086年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495147_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495147'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495147'>傅岩旧迹今犹在，兼与安平祖庙邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495147_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495147'>贤相裔孙还卜宅，先畴吉土是归真。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495147_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495147'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495147_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年9月2日</a>　举王钦臣。作品：《举王钦臣》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷四○。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　乞罢男贻庆与理转运判官资序与居中差宗正寺簿恩赏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月17日</a>　举孔文仲、叶祖洽、钱长卿。作品：《举孔文仲等》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举孔文仲等劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十一月十七日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160235")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160235'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160235'>臣切见朝廷近置馆阁职名，修复祖宗育才养士之法，诏许大臣各举所知三人以充其选，仍立法以秘书省官任校书郎二年，正字四年，并除校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160235_comment'></div>伏见礼部员外郎孔文仲蚤应制举，学行纯正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160235_comment'></div>兵部员外郎叶祖洽熙宁初进士选首，殆今一十七年，学术优深，众谓淹滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160235_comment'></div>比部员外郎钱长卿词艺精敏，问学该通，先帝尝令撰高丽书本称旨，遂蒙奖拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160235_comment'></div>三人皆曾任秘书省校书郎，偶于未复馆职以前，就迁省郎，不该新制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160235_comment'></div>缘逐人各在先朝已经采擢，备秘府文学之任，宜在今日之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160235_comment'></div>新条试职之人，京官以上并除校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160235_comment'></div>今来逐人已系省郎，欲乞详逐官资地比附，各除充馆阁近上职名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160235_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160235_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160235'>勘会复馆职新制以前，曾任秘书郎者止有此三人，今后即无人援例。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1160235_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　乞罢男贻庆升理运判官，及乞明堂之赐减半。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　举叶祖洽、钱长卿、孔文仲、胡宗炎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　奏尚书省六曹行遣迂滞事，并荐苏颂同共详定。作品：《奏尚书省六曹行遣迂滞事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二七。苏轼《德威堂铭》）</span><div id='poem_1160035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏尚书省六曹行遣迂滞事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160035")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160035'>臣窃见尚书省二十四司主判郎官转移迁改，频数不定，往往未知本案事务及文书义理，以致行遣迂回，稽滞中多，所请多不得可否之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160035_comment'></div>臣欲乞令左右司郎中、员外点检勘当，使逐案行遣文字明白简易，可否公当，不致留滞，定为式例，庶得永久遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160035_comment'></div>况左右司主本省纲辖，亦乞委得覆视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160035_comment'></div>刑部尚书苏颂素推熟知前代及本朝台省典故，乞委之同共详定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160035_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1160035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年12月</a>　契丹使来贺兴龙节，契丹使誉彦博为天下异人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年1月</a>　再举荐黄景。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月8日</a>　请以厢军册籍置枢密院。作品：《乞兵部厢军密院置籍》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞兵部厢军密院置籍奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160051")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160051'>臣以枢密院应内外厢禁军自来并系密院置籍所管，今以新制，并不管厢军，皆送尚书兵部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160051_comment'></div>且密院谓之本兵之府，岂可内外五十万厢军却无籍拘管，缓急出军行师，厢、禁皆用，况厢军不独用于诸般营造杂役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160051_comment'></div>兼自来如广南枪手、纲丁及诸州乡兵，亦是密院有籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160051_comment'></div>欲乞令密院只于兵部取索厢兵等人数，于兵籍房置簿拘管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160051_comment'></div>逐年揭帖常见实数，亦不烦费，缓急差使，易为照会，即不妨尚书兵部依近制主管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160051_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160051_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160051'><span class='label'>按：</span>《文潞公文集》卷二九。又见《宋会要辑稿》职官一四之四（第三册第二六八九页）、刑法七之二一（第七册第六七四四页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1160051_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月</a>　举杜欣、李周、杨国宝、吕太临。作品：《举杜欣等》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷四○。）</span><div id='poem_1160243' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160243' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160243?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举杜䜣等劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160243")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160243_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160243'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160243'>臣伏以近者奖恬退之士，抑躁竞之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160243_comment'></div>切见卫尉少卿杜䜣，贤相之后，能世其家，久历省府之任，素有老成之称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160243_comment'></div>太仆少卿李周恬静有守，当官不挠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160243_comment'></div>向为监司，以直道被黜，久安闲职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160243_comment'></div>宣德郎杨国宝安贫守道，恬于仕途，器识深远，才力有馀，虽近除太常博士，未尽其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160243_comment'></div>试太学博士吕大临强学笃行，有古儒之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160243_comment'></div>杜门十年，以讲学自乐，经术通明，闻誉夙著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160243_comment'></div>虽蒙召寘太学，以亲嫌未极其用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160243_comment'></div>以上四人伏乞特赐擢任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160243_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1160243_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年3月</a>　乞定立制度，以改僭侈之风俗。作品：《奏乞立制度使》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　进《尚书》、《孝经》解。作品：《进〈尚书〉〈孝经〉解》<div id='poem_1160070' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160070' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160070?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进尚书孝经解劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160070")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160070_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160070'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160070'>臣伏以皇帝陛下间日御迩英阁，令讲官讲《尚书》，又阁之南壁张《孝经图》，出入观览，有以见陛下祖述尧舜，宪章文武，以至德要道，孝治天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160070_comment'></div>臣今辄于《尚书》诸篇中节录十篇，及《孝经》诸章中节录六章进上，以备禁中清盻之暇，研究义味，或时令讲官节录疏义进入，上资圣德稽古求治之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160070_comment'></div>臣伏读《尚书序》云：「孔子生于周末，睹史籍之烦文，惧览之者不一，遂乃讨论坟典，断自唐虞以下，迄于周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160070_comment'></div>举其宏纲，撮其机要，典谟训诰之文，凡百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160070_comment'></div>所以恢宏至道，示人主以轨范也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160070_comment'></div>帝王之制，坦然明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160070_comment'></div>以其上古之书，谓之尚书」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160070_comment'></div>然则后代圣帝明王，莫不祖述，宝为大训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160070_comment'></div>恭以皇帝陛下聪明文思，稽考古道，日御迩英，延访经义，方命讲官讲解《尚书》，孜孜不倦，所以圣德日新，比隆尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160070_comment'></div>臣以叨侍经筵，辄于《尚书》三十二篇，采其切于资益圣治，宜于重复温故者，凡十篇录进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160070_comment'></div>篇别有后序，所以发明本篇之大旨，所冀便于乙夜之观。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160070_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　乞以三类之法选人任职。作品：《奏吏部三类法》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二七。）</span><div id='poem_1160038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏吏部三类法</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160038")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160038'>臣观《六典》三铨之法，以三类观其异，优者擢而升之，否者量而退之，所以正权衡，明赏罚，抑贪冒，进贤能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160038_comment'></div>今之典选，一守定格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160038_comment'></div>选格中有以多举主、有军功者为上，多举者或善请求，有军功者或容妄冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160038_comment'></div>如近时买人得赏官者极多，有同配官，故多失才，亦容滥进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160038_comment'></div>臣欲乞委吏部尚书、侍郎大略依三类之法，定本选之人，合入知州、通判、知县、县令，考其才德功效，为上中下三品，送中书门下覆验可否，定讫，判选官引对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160038_comment'></div>一经圣炮，物无遁形，便有去留，孰不激劝？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160038_comment'></div>又判铨之官，亦当上体朝廷委付之重，以衡炮自任，处之不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160038_comment'></div>间或以人才高下绝异者，特以名闻而进退之，乃为称职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160038_comment'></div>取进止<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160038_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160038'>「人」字下原衍「头」字，据《续资治通炮长编》删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1160038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160038'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_8_1160038_0'>⑴ 《文潞公文集》卷二七。又见《续资治通炮长编》卷三九六，《宋史》卷一六○《选举志》六，《历代名臣奏议》卷一六七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1160038_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年3月29日</a>　乞致仕。苏轼制诏曰：“昔西伯善养老而太公自至，鲁穆公无人子思之侧而长者去之。卿自为谋则善矣，独不为朝廷惜乎？”彦博读诏耸然，不复敢言去。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年4月</a>　诏彦博可自今后每十日一赴朝参。因至都堂议事。仍一月一赴经筵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　乞令唐义问带馆阁职名知荆南。作品：《举唐义问》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷四○。）</span><div id='poem_1160244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举唐义问劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160244")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160244'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160244'>臣切闻就差河东转运副使唐义问知荆南，缘荆南带湖北一路都兵钤兼统押近界蛮夷，地望重于湖南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160244_comment'></div>又闻广西蛮人潜结荆湖两路蛮酋作过，极要弹压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160244_comment'></div>今来唐义问只以近下散官知荆南，虑事体不重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160244_comment'></div>兼近有谢麟自知邠州移知潭州，带直秘阁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160244_comment'></div>叶均以秘书少监知荆南，带直龙图阁，从来体例甚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160244_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷特与检会诸例，令唐义问兼带馆阁职名知荆南，所贵夷夏称呼，有所增重方面事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160244_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1160244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月18日</a>　请举行太皇太后尊号册礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　请以昔之三司使之职悉归户部，并慎择久用户部官员。作品：《奏户部事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏户部事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160052")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160052'>臣以户部尚书乃昔之三司使之任，掌邦计，财赋出入，无不周知，则国用取济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160052_comment'></div>今当以昔之三司使之任，悉归户部，财赋盈虚，可以经制，不误大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160052_comment'></div>自尚书、侍郎以下，慎选而久用之，庶几集事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160052_comment'></div>尚书、侍郎即是三司使副之职，郎中、员外乃昔之判官之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160052_comment'></div>此国之大计，乞蚤留圣意。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1160052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　奏吏、户、刑部官久任。作品：《奏吏户刑部官久任》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160056?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏吏户刑部官久任</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160056")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160056'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160056'>臣伏睹先朝复尚书省六部二十四司，欲其分治职事，悉如唐制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160056_comment'></div>臣窃以尚书省吏部典选，户部掌邦计，刑部主国法，此三部最为重，而侍郎、郎中、员外多不久任，迁转频数，未熟本部职事，已见迁改，必致胥吏乘隙作弊，行遣迂滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160056_comment'></div>臣欲乞三部郎中、员外，须令并满四年，理为两任，逐任与皗资序，立为定制，经久遵行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160056_comment'></div>内吏部、户部司封、司瞕、考功、度支、金、仓部亦须再任，与逐任皗资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160056_comment'></div>上件三部郎官佐本部长官主判逐曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160056_comment'></div>任官材，掌邦计，主国法，皆是国之重事，伏望圣慈详察，蚤赐施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160056_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　奏中外官久任事。作品：《奏中外官久任》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏中外官久任事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160058")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160058'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160058'>臣以中外任官，移替频速，在任不久，有如驿舍，无由集事，何以致治，故累曾上言，乞中外官各令久任，须满资考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160058_comment'></div>近日以来，迁改尤为频数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160058_comment'></div>盖由风俗躁竞，例欲速迁，执政者或避怨谤，不能镇静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160058_comment'></div>欲望中外治安，未可期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160058_comment'></div>臣欲今后凡差除中外官，并具见在任官年月满未满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160058_comment'></div>须令任满，方得交替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160058_comment'></div>如是急速藉才，须要其人，则不拘此制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160058_comment'></div>其任满得替之官，须具在任实有劳绩，方与照会合关皗差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160058_comment'></div>所贵官吏自此不敢茍简欲速，百职自然修举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160058_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160058_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1160058'>臣累曾上言，以吏、户、刑部官属，主大选、大计、刑罚，并外任监司及亲民之官，并须久任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160058_comment'></div>此系朝廷致治之本，不可忽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160058_comment'></div>今乞与三省更申明祖宗旧法，遵守施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1160058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　在讲筵，彦博贺哲宗用纸扇，以其示人君俭德。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　乞以俭德付史册。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年8月6日</a>　除改旧制甄别资品除授之法。作品：《奏除改旧制》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏除改旧制</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160053")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160053'>臣近面奉圣旨，具自来除授官职次序一本进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160053_comment'></div>臣今略具除改旧制节目如后：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1160053'>吏部选人两任亲民，有举主，皗通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160053_comment'></div>通判两任满，有举主，皗知州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160053_comment'></div>自此已上叙皗，今谓之常调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160053_comment'></div>知州军有绩效，或有举荐，名实相副者，特擢皗转运使副、判官或提点刑狱、省府推、判官，今谓之出常调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160053_comment'></div>转运使有路分轻重远近之差，河北、陜西、河东三路为重路，岁满多任三司副使，或任江淮都大发运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160053_comment'></div>发运使任满，亦充三司副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160053_comment'></div>成都路次三路，任满，亦有充三司副使，或江淮发运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160053_comment'></div>京东西、淮南又其次，江南东西、荆湖南北、两浙路又次之，二广、福建、梓、利、夔路为远小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160053_comment'></div>已上三等路分转运使副任满，或就移近上次等路分，或归任省府判官，渐次擢充三路重任，以至三司副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160053_comment'></div>内提点刑狱则不拘路分轻重，除授转运使副、省府判官，或逐急藉才，差知大藩镇者，其归亦多任三司副使，或直除修撰、待制者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1160053'>三司副使岁满，即除待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160053_comment'></div>有本官是前行郎中、少卿或除谏议大夫者，有资浅而除集贤殿修撰，充都转运使，后亦除待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1160053'>三院御史，旧制多是两任通判已上举充，岁满多差充省府判官，或诸路转运副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160053_comment'></div>累迁至三路，岁满充三司副使，又岁满除待制、御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160053_comment'></div>或言事称职，公论所推，即非次拔擢，系自特恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1160053'>正言、司谏，自来迁擢无定制，或兼带馆职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160053_comment'></div>文行著闻，或议论识体，方正敢言，朝廷所知，临时不次擢用，本无常法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160053_comment'></div>三馆职事本育才待用之地，例当在馆久任，其间资地人品素高者，除修起居注<span class='inlineComment2'>（即今起居舍人。）</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160053_comment'></div>遇知制诰有阙，即试补<span class='inlineComment2'>（即今中书舍人。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1160053'>已上并旧制，甄别资品履历次第，除注之法与今来官制或小异而大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160053_comment'></div>更乞与三省参详进呈<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1160053'>殿：原无，据右引补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1160053_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160053'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1160053_0'>⑴ 《文潞公文集》卷二九。又见《续资治通炮长编》卷四○四，《容斋四笔》卷二。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1160053_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　夏国挑衅，彦博乞不与夏国计较，严加守备，静以待之。作品：《奏夏国事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏夏国事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160054")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160054'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160054'>中外臣僚上言：夏国受朝廷封册，恩礼极优，锡赉尤厚，而敢忘恩背惠，辄行公牒，传达疆吏，自绝于天，不修贡奉，天地所不容，人神所共怒，乞行天讨，以正有罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160054_comment'></div>欲乞降诏边帅，及出敕谇以谕中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160054_comment'></div>若朝廷姑务息民，推天地之大德，曲示含容，抑群情之怒忿，不与丑羌计较，即乞明谕边臣，严加守备，静以待之，必取全胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160054_comment'></div>所有朝廷续遣大兵，且令分屯次边州军，以备缓急边上勾抽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160054_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年9月</a>　再乞致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　奏吏、户部长贰保任郎官治状法。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年10月</a>　彦博生日，赐生日诏及生日礼物。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　进汉唐故事，以备上以史为鉴。作品：《进汉唐故事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　进《无逸图》作品：《进无逸图》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进无逸图奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160055")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160055'>臣伏观周公作《无逸》，以戒成王，后代圣君，皆奉为至戒，以成治化，以克永世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160055_comment'></div>臣又观唐史，见宰相崔植对穆宗云：「玄宗初得姚崇、宋瞡为宰相，二人者夙夜孜孜，致君以道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160055_comment'></div>瞡尝手写《尚书·无逸》一篇，为图以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160055_comment'></div>玄宗置之内殿，出入观省，记念在心，每睵古人至言，后代莫及，故任贤戒欲，心归冲漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160055_comment'></div>开元之末，因《无逸图》朽坏，始以山水图代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160055_comment'></div>自后既无座右箴规，又信奸臣用事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160055_comment'></div>天宝之末，稍倦于勤，王道于斯缺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160055_comment'></div>今陛下虚心求治，伏望以《无逸》为元龟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160055_comment'></div>穆宗善其对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160055_comment'></div>臣恭惟皇帝陛下聪明稽古，向学思道，间日御迩英，延儒臣讲读经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160055_comment'></div>臣又观迩英北壁有仁祖朝讲官王洙所写《无逸图》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160055_comment'></div>臣虑禁中或未有此图，辄敢写录四轴并一卷上进，望于殿内张挂，置于几案，以便圣览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160055_comment'></div>臣愚不胜区区之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1160055_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年12月</a>　乞致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年3月</a>　韩绛卒，彦博作挽词悼念之。作品：《赠太傅康国韩公绛挽词三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_495148' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495148' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495148?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司马赠太傅康国韩公挽词<span class='inlineComment2'>（三首　（四库本题下有小注绛字））</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495148")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495148_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495148'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495148'>朝路相从三纪馀，更陪国论对钧枢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495148'>康时远术推贤业，造膝嘉猷协帝俞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495148'>盘结方资庖刃解，旱乾犹望傅霖苏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495148'>寝门遽有人琴叹，老伴调零道转孤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495148_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495148'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495148_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495149' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495149' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495149?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495149_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495149'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495149'>洛城曾与公相别，已为人生老别难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495149'>今作绋讴成永诀，满襟悲泪转汍澜<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495149'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495149_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495149'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_495149_0'>⑴ 自注：别此三年，公赴北都，饶于上东门，愚尝有诗云樽前不制泪汍澜，大抵人情老别难之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495149_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495150?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1088年3月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495150'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495150'>西豪居在许东偏，丹旐遥遥过<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>许田。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495150'>欲问相君真宅处，高平吉地是新阡<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495150'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495150'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495150_0'>⑴ 二字原缺，据四库本补</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_495150_0'>⑵ 自注：公家始卜葬地，问于野人，此是吉地，吉，乃野人之名。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495150_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年5月</a>　荐张守约。作品：《举张守约》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷四○。）</span><div id='poem_1160245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举张守约劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐三年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1160245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160245'>臣切见东上閤门使、鄜延路马步军副总管张守约，累经陕西任使，熟知边事，深晓兵政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160245_comment'></div>但以忠勤孤直，进身不茍，今虽年过七十，精力甚强，而官止横行使额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160245_comment'></div>欲望朝廷察其人材履历，特赐擢充正任，以奖久劳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年</a>　请外处州县刑狱急速断放，以乞雨。作品：《奏疏决刑狱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160057' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160057' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160057?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏疏决刑狱</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160057'>臣今日蚤延和殿奏，为圣慈闵雨，二十二日御殿疏决禁系罪人，当日降雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160057_comment'></div>尚恐外处州县有未雨足处，乞下逐路监司，令分巡部下州军，催促刑狱，疾速断放，免有魾滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160057_comment'></div>因录先朝御批劄子进呈。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1160057'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160057_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　奏请阿里骨使人见鬼章。作品：《奏鬼章事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　乞知州、通判遵用三年一任之法。作品：《奏知州通判理任》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏知州通判理任</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160063")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160063'>臣伏睹熙宁敕并元丰四年条贯，内地知州、通判、知县，并以三年为一任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160063_comment'></div>此正合《舜典》三载考绩之义，甚为稽古之美法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160063_comment'></div>盖亲民之官久于其任，则民安其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160063_comment'></div>故汉唐以来，郡太守或有善政，则增秩赐金，留以久任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160063_comment'></div>近睹元祐元年四月初敕旨，知州、通判并以三十个月为一任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160063_comment'></div>臣以谓三年为一任，不惟稽古之美法，乃先朝之定命，施于官政，极以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160063_comment'></div>此必是吏部以在部守待知州、通判待阙之官甚多，少得近阙差注，遂欲促其年限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160063_comment'></div>殊不知虽时下差注，得一番待阙之官即替回者却多，待阙者却众，徒有更张，并不济事，又非三载考绩之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160063_comment'></div>臣欲乞且遵用三年一任之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160063_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160063_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1160063'>若通判以三十个月为一任，即五年成两任，便皗入知州，则知州之阙转多。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年8月</a>　刘安世言彦博子孙所得恩赏不当。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年9月</a>　复求致仕。诏彦博要以周公、召公、毕公、史佚四子之心为心，以天下为任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年</a>　刘安世劾胡宗愈，以其辟彦博孙婿李慎由为御史台主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1088&endYear=1088')">1088年11月</a>　主回河之议。<br id='poem_sentence_0_1160247_comment'></div>先帝以其德望之重，擢为辅臣，未尽其才，不久薨谢，举朝痛惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160247_comment'></div>今其子绶见任宣义郎、签书濠州判官，能世其家，恬静自守，不苟求进，士人称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160247_comment'></div>臣伏见近奖用刘敦夫、吕由诚，皆以其父吕诲、刘庠之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160247_comment'></div>如包拯之后，惟绶一身，孤立不倚，臣以谓宜蒙奖擢，以旌名臣之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160247_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160247_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_1160174_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1089')">1089年</a>　乞在京院坊监牧马草地依旧听民间出课租佃。作品：《奏坊监草地令百姓出租》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二九。）</span><div id='poem_1160060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏坊监草地令百姓出租</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160060")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160060'>臣窃知太仆寺在京苑坊监牧马草地，其间甚有自来水占、牧马不到去处，系人户断扑，租佃客贫民采捕蒲鱼，种植莲藕，入城货卖，以资口食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160060_comment'></div>今闻太仆寺为系牧马地内一例勾收入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160060_comment'></div>臣闻得本寺官及供到细状，称上件水占牧地，可以依旧令人断课租佃，济贫民，并无妨阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160060_comment'></div>况今来下民艰食之际，伏望圣慈特降指挥，令依旧出课租扑，以纾近京贫下之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160060_comment'></div>取圣旨。</div><div class='articleSentence' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160092'>臣切闻太中大夫致仕程珦身亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160092_comment'></div>珦素履清介，守分安贫，久历外任，皆有声称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160092_comment'></div>身没之后，家事索然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160092_comment'></div>只有一子程颐，素蕴学行，见推士林，向为迩英讲官，因缘经义，开陈治体，上资圣政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160092_comment'></div>今其父之亡，窘于襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160092_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜悯，优与赙恤，以周其急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160092_comment'></div>伏候进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1160092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　范祖禹请听彦博解军国重事，以太师就第留之京师以备访问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年2月8日</a>　荐通判同州赵亢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　以太师致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　玉津园赐彦博宴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年4月</a>　以彦博乞，与其曾孙文常假承务郎之职。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
翼城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a1cb9a29dbf741d6aa23174e3ec4e477_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1cb9a29dbf741d6aa23174e3ec4e477");'><span id='a1cb9a29dbf741d6aa23174e3ec4e477_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1029')">1027-1029年</a>，22-24岁</div><div id='a1cb9a29dbf741d6aa23174e3ec4e477' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　授知翼城县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　以李本献策治县中豪猾，终公之任，邑中无敢肆横者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　修河亭，并亲书岁月榜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　修至圣文宣王庙。<br /></div>
