-----title
新绛（翼城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d3b035aff22b46bfa22b89d909f1b5d6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d3b035aff22b46bfa22b89d909f1b5d6");'><span id='d3b035aff22b46bfa22b89d909f1b5d6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1030')">1029-1030年</a>，24-25岁</div><div id='d3b035aff22b46bfa22b89d909f1b5d6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　在知翼城县任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年9月5日</a>　至圣文宣王庙成，为作碑记。作品：《绛州翼城县新修至圣文宣王庙碑记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1160316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>绛州翼城县新修至圣文宣王庙碑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1030年9月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160316")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160316_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160316'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160316'>圣宋四叶，上继明之五年，某以进士举中甲科，得大理评事，宰是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160316_comment'></div>秋八月二十九日始莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160316_comment'></div>故事，守令始至，则郡县之祠庙悉诣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160316_comment'></div>恭于神，训于民，政之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160316_comment'></div>由是询于邑吏，质之县图，载祀典、享庙食者，惟宣圣之祠焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160316_comment'></div>翌日，伸祠谒之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160316_comment'></div>已事而退立于庑下，观其石记，则后唐长兴三年创是庙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160316_comment'></div>岁月滋久，庙貌弗严，屋瓦皆隳，梁木其坏，上不庇于风雨，下不容于俎豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160316_comment'></div>县署直其北十数步，日有敲扑之喧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160316_comment'></div>浍水流于东不三四尺，岁虞漂溺之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160316_comment'></div>虽「贤哉回也，不改其乐」，「君子居之，何陋之有」，而守土事神者，崇奉之礼岂不阙欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160316_comment'></div>乃谋为僚，规是改作，方营善地，将构新宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160316_comment'></div>而县西北隅适有废庙，俗老承传为汤王行宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160316_comment'></div>事出不经，礼无常祀，既绝蘋蘩之荐，鞠为荆棘之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160316_comment'></div>像设都亡，廊庑全陊，独有正殿，岿然中立，虽丹垩已晦，而甍栋颇崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160316_comment'></div>异乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160316_comment'></div>天将以斯室遗夫子耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160316_comment'></div>不尔，则胡为十室九废，而独完兹中宇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160316_comment'></div>虚其正位者，安所俟乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160316_comment'></div>宜其即是遗构，以正两楹之坐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160316_comment'></div>起兹颓垣，以崇数仞之墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160316_comment'></div>踵其故以谋新，材则易备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160316_comment'></div>变其本而加饰，工不告劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160316_comment'></div>命薙氏以芟夷，集扰人而涂塈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160316_comment'></div>兴废起坠，务实去华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160316_comment'></div>昔之湫陋者，耽耽而云荫矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160316_comment'></div>曩之荒秽者，殖殖而底平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160316_comment'></div>翼以东西二室，增之屏树闬闳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160316_comment'></div>凡屋壁之间堵，其数百楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160316_comment'></div>危昏中而戒事，日南至而卒功，动适其时，不愆于素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160316_comment'></div>邑人张会元以文行称于乡曲，累举进士，败于垂成，运舛事违，退而讲授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160316_comment'></div>一日，睹新庙之既成，以殊像之未备，乃率其徒，躬营其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160316_comment'></div>明年春，募工于别郡，得绘塑之妙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160316_comment'></div>于是塑宣圣暨十哲之像，逾十旬而告就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160316_comment'></div>八月上丁，行释奠之礼落之，且曰：「能事毕矣，不可无闻于后，盍书以志」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160316_comment'></div>故述其经始之因，直记夫岁月而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160316_comment'></div>杜牧云：「称夫子之德，莫如孟子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160316_comment'></div>称夫子之尊，莫如韩吏部」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160316_comment'></div>孟所谓：「生人以来，未有夫子，贤过尧舜远矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160316_comment'></div>韩所谓：「自天子至郡邑守长，得共祀而遍天下者，惟社稷与孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160316_comment'></div>社稷坛而不屋，岂如孔子巍然当座，用王者礼，以门人配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160316_comment'></div>自天子而下，北面拜跪，礼如亲弟子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160316_comment'></div>然则夫子之德之尊，韩、孟之言详矣，今兹为记，是用略诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1160316_comment'></div>时天圣八年九月五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1160316_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年9月7日</a>　改知榆次县。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
榆次
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f825d4f523b44d72a9e48db228b2bbc1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f825d4f523b44d72a9e48db228b2bbc1");'><span id='f825d4f523b44d72a9e48db228b2bbc1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1033')">1031-1033年</a>，26-28岁</div><div id='f825d4f523b44d72a9e48db228b2bbc1' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年1月4日</a>　到榆次县任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年1月4日</a>　题诗。作品：《戏题诗于榆次县新鞔衙鼓》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》佚诗。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　在榆次知县任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　建思凤亭，题诗以记之。作品：《思凤亭诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》佚诗。）</span><div id='poem_1160317' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160317' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160317?labeling=true' target='_blank'>思凤亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道元年二月四日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160317")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160317_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160317'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160317'>杨盈川所居廨舍，好治亭榭，其榜额皆制美名，大为远近所笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160317_comment'></div>夫考室命名者众矣，或即其地号而著，或因其事实而称，揭而书之，斯用无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160317_comment'></div>苟异于是，则徒丰其额，美其名，必为有识者之抚掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160317_comment'></div>天圣庚午岁九月七日，彦博受命宰榆次，越明年春正月四日始到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160317_comment'></div>邑之生齿受地而附籍者五万二千户，乔居而末业者不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160317_comment'></div>河东之邑，斯最为大，啧言控诉，庭无虚日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160317_comment'></div>敏政者莅之犹惮弗及，顾予菲劣，岂敢逸豫？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160317_comment'></div>盖夙夜而在公者迄三时矣，未窥园圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160317_comment'></div>岁聿云暮，适西成告丰，而邑中之园亭得以睹览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160317_comment'></div>县令表位之南，旧有小园，颓废已甚，乃荣垣薙草，惟涂暨茨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160317_comment'></div>无变本而增华，但踵故而加饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160317_comment'></div>亦既成室，必也命名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160317_comment'></div>可书者有三，而思凤是其一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160317_comment'></div>询于父老之口，质以往图之载，皆曰荀浪尝宰是邑，治有善迹，凤集其境，后人思之，乃用名乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160317_comment'></div>今县南有荀政乡焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160317_comment'></div>愚谓贤宰之迹，未可遽泯，因扁是亭曰「思凤」，所谓即地号而著，因事实而称者，斯得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160317_comment'></div>自是，居是亭者诚能修荀公之政，致祥禽之集，则后之人思之，亦如今之思荀公者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160317_comment'></div>诗曰：荀令吟琴地，吁嗟集凤兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160317_comment'></div>想同桑雉扰，应并棘鸾栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160317_comment'></div>承乏今无敢，思贤古若稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160317_comment'></div>我来求旧址，即署改亲题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160317_comment'></div>不独怀希骥，聊将警割鸡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160317_comment'></div>一窥循吏表，芳躅愧攀跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160317_comment'></div>明道二年五月四日<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160317_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1160317'>原作「明道五年二月四日」，明道仅两年，显误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160317_comment'></div>据雍正《山西通志》改。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1160317_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160317'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_1160317_0'>⑴ 《古今图书集成》职方典卷三○四。又见雍正《山西通志》卷二一二，光绪《山西通志》卷九九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1160317_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　为思凤亭诗作序。作品：《思凤亭诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　作文悼念祖父文锐。作品：《赠尚书祠部员外郎文府君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1160327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠尚书祠部员外郎文府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（明道二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160327")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160327'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160327'>夫水之有原，原出之深者，其流长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160327_comment'></div>人之本祖，祖德之厚者，其嗣昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160327_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160327_comment'></div>原深而德厚者，见之于吾祖祠部府君矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160327_comment'></div>府君讳锐，字挺之，本姓敬，当晋室，以犯高祖御名，改赐今姓，取文之象也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160327_comment'></div>至圣朝，以避翼祖庙讳，遂不复旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160327_comment'></div>有妫之裔，迁育于姜，子完之孙，以谥为姓，自时厥后，胄绪益蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160327_comment'></div>或占数于平阳，或派居于蒲坂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160327_comment'></div>八代祖、太尉平阳王有大勋力于中宗，载于国书，可以复视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160327_comment'></div>高祖晤，大和中由鸿胪丞辟北都留守判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160327_comment'></div>曾王父穟时，以明经中第，守汾州参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160327_comment'></div>未几，留判归老于西河，参军荣侍于膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160327_comment'></div>且又嘉是山水，乐其土风，乃自河东县之同果里徙居于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160327_comment'></div>故府君今为西河介休县人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160327_comment'></div>王父沼，泽州录事参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160327_comment'></div>烈考崇远，长兴中守辽州平城簿，与晋高祖有丰沛之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160327_comment'></div>天福初，龙兴大夏，凤起晋阳，遂以协赞之功，亟升出宰之任，授代州崞县令，稍迁并州太谷县令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160327_comment'></div>虽幄中之助居多，而绵上之封盖薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160327_comment'></div>方将偕隐，以保天和，属刘氏偏霸于太原，选用俊贤，縻以要职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160327_comment'></div>而又两宰剧县，载更郡辖，而考终于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160327_comment'></div>有子二人，其长蚤亡，府君即其次也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160327_comment'></div>始以荫补郊社署丞，寻辟石州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160327_comment'></div>太平兴国中，武车载驾，王师有征，后主率并民因垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160327_comment'></div>太宗皇帝霈阳春之泽，封归命之侯，凡刘氏之旧臣，率度材而被用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160327_comment'></div>时府君方以疾退，便于家居，且以颐养为怀，无复出处之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160327_comment'></div>虽诏书搜访，州司敦遣，竟以疾辞，不克上道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160327_comment'></div>常以杖履浮沉于乡里，颇用文酒燕乐于友朋，故与进士温梦说、诗僧崇果、绍休辈有世外莫逆之契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160327_comment'></div>药喜弗验，坏梁斯及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160327_comment'></div>以至道二年九月三日启手足于晋陵里之第，享年五十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160327_comment'></div>府君始娶王氏，故户部郎中丕之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160327_comment'></div>生庆善之门，禀柔懿之德，天夺其算，先府君而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160327_comment'></div>有子三人：长曰洎，今为司勋员外郎、荆湖南路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160327_comment'></div>次曰淳，郊社斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160327_comment'></div>次曰渊，未仕而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160327_comment'></div>有女一人，适史氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160327_comment'></div>再娶郭氏，有子一人，曰渭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160327_comment'></div>府君以长子之登朝遘庆，凡四追命为尚书祠曹员外郎，夫人追封临沂县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160327_comment'></div>洎娶耿氏，有子一人，曰彦博，即府君之嫡孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160327_comment'></div>天圣五年春登进士甲科，今为殿中丞、知并州榆次县，权倅西河郡事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160327_comment'></div>而耿氏蚤亡，亦以彦博预殿闺之引籍，遘农坛之展礼，得援恩例追封扶风县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160327_comment'></div>再娶申氏，封永乐县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160327_comment'></div>有子一人，曰彦若，应进士举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160327_comment'></div>有女二人，长适将作监主簿鞠齐卿，故天章阁待制咏之子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1160327_comment'></div>次适进士成伟，殿中丞元吉之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1160327_comment'></div>府君之次男淳，始娶郭氏、冀氏，皆蚤亡，今娶武氏，有子四人：长曰彦先，次曰彦国，其次皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1160327_comment'></div>渭娶王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1160327_comment'></div>斯皆府君贻谋积德之至厚，故子孙锡美流光之寖昌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1160327_comment'></div>彦博之生也后，不获逮事，捧遗砚以出涕，瞻画像而下榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1160327_comment'></div>尝立侍于父、叔，因习闻于话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1160327_comment'></div>曰：惟府君局量闳深，性资端厚，信行著于乡党，仁爱洽于族姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1160327_comment'></div>希蜀严之沉冥，达羲《易》之素履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1160327_comment'></div>善教诸子，俾绍家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1160327_comment'></div>尝曰：「扶阳之门，满籯非宝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1160327_comment'></div>刘氏之室，七业俱成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1160327_comment'></div>吾素志也，尔曹勉之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1160327_comment'></div>惟以清白传家，不以业产为事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1160327_comment'></div>识者以府君为林宗、干木，西河之后出也，所不至者寿尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1160327_comment'></div>府君弃代之年，权窆于里第之西原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1160327_comment'></div>今岁在作噩，利即真宅，即以明道二年十月十七日己酉得吉卜于灵石县之孝义原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1160327_comment'></div>祖母临沂太君，先葬于介休县之西原，陪祖考之旧封，松槚美茂，不复迁祔，从古礼也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1160327_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1160327'>王父之德，柔嘉维则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1160327_comment'></div>行有枝叶，信著金石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1160327_comment'></div>州党胥化，宗姻是式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1160327_comment'></div>跌宕文石，涵泳典籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1160327_comment'></div>美璞中存，含华内蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1160327_comment'></div>道屈当世，庆流后昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1160327_comment'></div>祠曹追命，密印推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1160327_comment'></div>绵山南峙，汾流东㳽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1160327_comment'></div>吁嗟佳城，兹焉宁止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1160327_comment'></div>圆石勒铭，徽音无已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1160327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160327'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_59_1160327_0'>⑴ 《礼》曰：「铭者称先祖之美，旌孝孙之心也。」庸刻沈础，以识佳城。铭曰：</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1160327_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
太原
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　至河东转运副使任，于长平驿舍题诗。作品：《长平怀古》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_494787' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494787' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494787?labeling=true' target='_blank'>长平怀古<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span "poem_title_494787")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494787_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494787_0'>① 原注：康定元年任河东转运副使，入境题长平驿舍。先是，先令公任河东漕使，捐馆，公服除，继为漕，初至部，赋此。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494787'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494787'>此子徒能读父书，兵降始信蔺相如。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494787_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494787'>却令后代承家者，每到长平戒覆车。<div id='poem_title_494834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送福州通判陈铸殿丞<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为殿中侍御史河东转运使）</span></a><span "poem_title_494834")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494834'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494834'>泽宫登甲第，殿省滞时英。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494834'>闽国题舆贵，稽山昼锦荣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494834'>轶才犹绊骥，美俗仰诚衡<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺，据四库本补）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494834'>寿母平返喜，迎知讼牒清<span class='inlineComment2'>（末三字原缺，据四库本补）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494834_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494834'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年6月16日</a>　乞隰、宪州、宁化、保德、苛岚、火山军处，各差通判，省职官一员。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年8月</a>　于河东转运副使任上，乡老欢迎，有诗记之。作品：《某天圣四年叨充乡赋明道二年夏假副车于本郡今年夏忝外计于本道实嗣世职八月行部率遵故常乡老欢迎邀留累日追惟畴曩因成拙诗二章题于行署》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_494839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>某天圣四年叨充乡赋明道二年夏假副车于本郡今年夏忝外计于本道寔嗣世职<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>八月行部率遵故常乡老欢迎邀留累日徘徊旧地追惟畴曩因成拙诗二章题于行署<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494839")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494839_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494839_0'>① 前此三年先大夫为河东转运使</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494839'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494839'>不才惟侍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>高门庆，奕世皆为外计臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494839'>乡老相逢频教我，尽忠思孝报君亲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494839'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_494839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_494839'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_494839_0'>⑴ 二字原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494839_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_494840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494840?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1040年8月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494840'>昔年乡赋议兴贤，曾接诸君砚席间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494840'>屈指岁华逾一纪，锦衣怀绶过稽山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494840'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_494840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　复麟州（今陕西神木）唐时故道，益其储粟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　乞重惩王元康德舆。作品：乞重惩王元康德舆奏。<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160251' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160251?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞重惩王元康德舆奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160251")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160251'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160251'>昨西贼围丰州及宁远寨，其并代州都部署、通判、团练使王元，麟府州钤辖、东染院使、昭州刺史康德舆，只在府州闭垒自守，并无出兵救援之意，以致八月七日宁远寨破，十九日丰州破。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160251_comment'></div>二十一日西贼引退已远，麟州路通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160251_comment'></div>二十三日，元等乃牒府州索随军十日粮草，计人粮马料九千石，草五万六千束，以二十六日出军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160251_comment'></div>臣寻急令保德、火山、岢岚军人户各备脚乘于府州，请搬上件随军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160251_comment'></div>其王元、康德舆只于府州城外五七里下寨，坐食所搬粮草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160251_comment'></div>经三日，复将所部兵马入城，亦不先告人户令知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160251_comment'></div>其人户等见军马入城，谓是西贼将至，皆仓皇奔窜入城，弃所搬粮草脚乘并在野寨，明日方令人户搬所馀粮草于仓场回纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160251_comment'></div>窃缘人户请搬粮草、雇脚乘，所费至重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160251_comment'></div>臣取得人户雇脚契帖，每搬随军草一束、粮一斗，不以远近日数计钱一贯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160251_comment'></div>如此费耗，若一两次，何以任之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160251_comment'></div>若或出军击贼，远救城寨，须要粮草先行，虽有重费，不可辞劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160251_comment'></div>其如贼退已远，麟州道路已通，方领军马出城，又不前去追袭，却只在府州城外五七里劄寨，令人户运粮，元辈何以自安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160251_comment'></div>方今西事未平，捍边全藉良将，若王元、康德舆驽下之材，如此举动，必致败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160251_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷明行重典，以戒懦夫，别择武臣，付以边事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1160251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　乞河东依陕西例每三丁点一丁充强壮。作品：《乞河东依陕西例点强壮》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞河东依陕西例点强壮奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159937")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159937'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159937'>右，臣于去年二月初曾上言，乞于河东路每三丁点一丁充强壮，缓急为守御之备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159937_comment'></div>自后朝廷差吴遵路等于河东路点差到强壮共一十四万三千馀人，内一十三万三千馀人是主户，九千馀人是客户，是皆两丁内点一丁充强壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159937_comment'></div>臣今遍巡历到诸州军，切见所点到强壮太多而不精，兼颇妨夺农事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159937_comment'></div>臣检会咸平中曾降敕点差强壮，本路除晋、绛、慈、隰、麟、府六州不点差外，其点差到强壮四万四千馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159937_comment'></div>今来虽添晋、绛、慈、隰四州点差强壮，即比咸平旧几及三倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159937_comment'></div>况本路主客人户共三十一万三千，勘会才及陜西人户之半，昨来陜西所点弓手只十万人，以此况之，即河东所点集太多而妨农也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159937_comment'></div>臣欲乞依陜西体例，每三丁点一人充强壮，犹可得八万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159937_comment'></div>所贵务农作者不致妨废，习武事者颇得精专。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159937_comment'></div>如允臣所奏，更不行钞点丁口数目而去留之，并不搔扰动众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159937_comment'></div>谨具奏闻，伏侯敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159937_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　请罢以军法约束强壮。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　乞将并州、代州总管王亢、钤辖康德舆、杨怀志正典刑。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年6月24日</a>　迁河东路都转运使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年10月14日</a>　实未赴知渭州任。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='20b126f270d744c68da0a58a43ea45df_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("20b126f270d744c68da0a58a43ea45df");'><span id='20b126f270d744c68da0a58a43ea45df_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>，57岁</div><div id='20b126f270d744c68da0a58a43ea45df' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　求龙门宝应寺证大师改刘几秘监庵作潞公庵。作品：《诗寄龙门宝应寺证大师》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_494916' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494916' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494916?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诗寄龙门宝应寺證大师<span class='inlineComment2'>（求改刘几秘监庵作潞公庵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494916")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494916_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494916'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494916'>山人去作山西将，岫幌岩扉掩翠岚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494916'>欲问證师求正住，凭师改作潞公庵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494916_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494916'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_494916_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
天水
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c0e6e021ca544ef2aa169b9e9d836b98_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c0e6e021ca544ef2aa169b9e9d836b98");'><span id='c0e6e021ca544ef2aa169b9e9d836b98_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1044')">1042-1044年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='c0e6e021ca544ef2aa169b9e9d836b98' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年11月12日</a>　改知秦州兼秦凤路都部署、经略安抚招讨使，到任作谢两府启。作品：《知秦州谢两府启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一○。）</span><div id='poem_1160283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知秦州谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年11月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160283")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160283'>伏奉敕差知秦州，已于某月某日到任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160283_comment'></div>古秦之封，中夏为蔽，久所择守，难其得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160283_comment'></div>自惭拙愚，寖服华宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160283_comment'></div>出涖边绝，讫无勋勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160283_comment'></div>敢希上恩，乃俾易地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160283_comment'></div>即政之始，观风有殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160283_comment'></div>山川旷夷，羌汉丛会，俗尚不一，师屯且繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160283_comment'></div>迩复拓固封圻，建宅城堡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160283_comment'></div>守备之戒，当有远谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160283_comment'></div>事役之兴，剧于他道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160283_comment'></div>所任益重，非蒙克堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160283_comment'></div>盖遇某官协亮天工，总持政柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160283_comment'></div>慎牧师之选，切方面之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160283_comment'></div>启言至公，汲用平进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160283_comment'></div>谨精措置，勉罄朴忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160283_comment'></div>图靖塞虞，讲求民理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160283_comment'></div>庶几修职，无玷于人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1160283_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　以修水洛城（今陕西庄浪境内）为不便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　乞秦凤都监冯诰复为太子中允、通判秦州。作品：《冯诰复文资故官奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>冯诰复文资故官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160252")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160252'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160252'>本州西路蕃部李宫等八族寇永宁、来远寨，都监齐再升为贼追袭，坠崖而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160252_comment'></div>其后数入寇钞，而诰能于来远寨北八里野勺口筑堡以扼其要冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160252_comment'></div>贼计窘，于是入献甲器，愿纳质内附及以再升之丧来还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160252_comment'></div>诰初以太子中允换崇仪副使，寻责授礼宾副使，今不愿预赏，止愿复文资故官。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　夏，彦博请加强秦州边备，以备防秋。作品：《答奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　四月，泸州界夷人作过，欲发秦凤路兵，彦博言秦州距泸州地远，赴救不便。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年12月27日</a>　改知益州。<br /></div>
-----end

成都

class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160254")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160254'>右，臣职忝枢近，寄之藩服，间求遗逸，思补休和，期于上闻，不敢自默。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160254_comment'></div>臣窃见本州将仕郎、试国子四门助教龙昌期气正行介，学纯虑深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160254_comment'></div>究古今治忽之原，穷圣贤变通之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160254_comment'></div>旁贯百氏，阐发微言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160254_comment'></div>别注六经，颇有新义，高出诸儒之疏解，洞见圣人之指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160254_comment'></div>□□注《周易》、《尚书》、《毛诗》、《孝经》、《道德经》，并撰《礼论》、《八卦图》等书，凡六十馀卷，今资政殿大学士范雍旧尝与之通进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160254_comment'></div>宝元中，本路安抚使韩琦、知益州张逸、转运使明镐并曾奏举，遂授初命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160254_comment'></div>而昌期疏于声利，乐于丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160254_comment'></div>试经诲人，取重乡闬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160254_comment'></div>著书传道，动成简编。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160254_comment'></div>年踰七十之龄，家无斗升之禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160254_comment'></div>观其所守，益励初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160254_comment'></div>臣伏见故国子监丞、江宁府学说书张元用，并兖州说书杨光辅，并自布衣，荐为京秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160254_comment'></div>今昌期生于遐僻，学有本元，惜其暮年，止于散试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160254_comment'></div>臣欲望圣慈依张元用等例改昌期一京官，充本州州学讲说，以激颓俗，以劝远方，使野无滞才之嗟，朝有养贤之咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160254_comment'></div>干冒宸扆，臣无任惶悚激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160254_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1160254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　赏识文同。誉其“襟度洒落如晴云秋月，尘埃不可到”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　好宴集，上遣何郯伺察之。张俞为彦博智喜宴集之劾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　从容沮卒乱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　尝击球钤辖廨，斩不服管之士卒，竟球始归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　益州大旱，民诉旱情，彦博罢宴祈雨，即日下雨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年12月</a>　请立法训练本路兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　送果州李推官赴阙，有诗记之。作品：《送果州李推官赴阙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_494829' id='poem_title_494841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送益利路承受梁供奉回京</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494841'>秋晚华轩去，江滨祖席开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494841_comment'></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　举高惟几。作品：《举高惟几》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160217' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160217?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举高惟几劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160217")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160217_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160217'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160217'>臣切见益州路提点刑狱高惟几材干明敏，长于治繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160217_comment'></div>臣顷任河东都转运使，惟几通判麟州，用兵之际，供意百端，悉能应办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160217_comment'></div>昨任益州路转运判官日，适值岁饥，臣在益州，首先劝诱人户发粟赈济，遂请高惟几出巡外郡，劝诱人户出粟，一如益州之法，甚济饥民，绩状可奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160217_comment'></div>其高惟几伏乞朝廷特赐皗擢任使，以劝劳吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160217_comment'></div>如经擢用后本官犯正入己赃，臣甘同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160217_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160217_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　举杨文举。作品：《举杨文举》<span "poem_title_1160218")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160218_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160218'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160218'>臣切见利州路提点刑狱杨文举廉勤干敏，前年利州路大饥，臣累牒本官体量救济，备见用心集事，以致流民不致重困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160218_comment'></div>伏望朝廷特赐旌奖，皗陟任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160218_comment'></div>如经擢用后犯正入己赃，臣甘同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160218_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160218_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　举田瑜。作品：《举田瑜》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160219'>臣切见益州路转运使田瑜才识通敏，自到本路，岁月未久，而办集财赋，更张弊原，皆有伦理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160219_comment'></div>今臣保举堪充皗陟任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160219_comment'></div>如经擢用后犯正入己赃，臣甘同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160219_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1160219'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160219_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　请复利州路昭化县驿程。作品：《乞复昭化县驿程》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞复昭化县驿程奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159939")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159939'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159939'>去年臣僚上言减废利州昭化县驿程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159939_comment'></div>臣闻行路之言，皆为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159939_comment'></div>臣昨亲自经由相度，诚为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159939_comment'></div>昭化驿去利州虽近，又因东有桔鲵津大江之阻，西有木瓜原重山之险，夏秋二时，雨潦留滞，行役之人，进退无据，古来置驿，良因于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159939_comment'></div>今既废驿，即经过使命不免裹粮留宿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159939_comment'></div>其如过军稍多，即宿食有所阙乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159939_comment'></div>臣欲乞依旧驿支给券料，所费甚少，所济则多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159939_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1159939_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　请令审官院选差川峡州郡知州。作品：《乞选差川峡州郡知州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞选差川峡州郡知州奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159940")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159940'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159940'>臣切见祥符中，先帝轸念川峡远民，精求循吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159940_comment'></div>以为审官院依资次差移官员，多不得人，故特颁诏书，令冯拯以下各举川峡知州、通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159940_comment'></div>臣切以西川近年以来，生齿繁庶，比祥符中数倍，全藉长吏安辑，稍不得人，即烦朝廷西顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159940_comment'></div>臣以为川峡知、通，若尽须举差，恐难得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159940_comment'></div>所有益、梓、利三路内邛、蜀、嘉、眉、彭、汉、陵、绵、果、阆、遂、合、剑州、兴元府十四处，户口繁多，屯兵稍众，所有知州、知府，臣欲乞今后令审官院拣选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159940_comment'></div>差官须是历任内无私罪，升朝后有举主，年甲未高者，方得差任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159940_comment'></div>如任内别败阙，得替日与先次优便差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159940_comment'></div>或别有殊尤治状，灼然可验，即升陟酬奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159940_comment'></div>所贵远方得人，兼举先朝故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159940_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1159940_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　请本路诸州供钱拨充益州交子务。作品：《请诸州供钱拨充交子务》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159941' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159941' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159941?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞诸州供钱拨充交子务奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159941")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159941_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159941'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159941'>益州交子务所用交子，岁获公利甚厚，复又民间要藉使用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159941_comment'></div>盖比之铁钱，便于赍持转易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159941_comment'></div>今因秦州入中粮草，两次支却六十万贯文交子，元有未封桩见钱，准备向去给还客人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159941_comment'></div>深虑将来一二年间，界分欲满，客人将交子赴官，却无钱给还，有误请领，便至坏却交子之法，公私受弊，深为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159941_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷指挥本路转运司，于辖下诸州军内每月须管共收聚诸般课利钱三五万贯，拨充益州交子务，准备给还客人交子钱，免致向去坏却旧法，官私困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159941_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1159941_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　乞罢将校举留。作品：《乞罢将校举留》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一四。）</span><div id='poem_1159942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢将校举留奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159942")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159942_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159942'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159942'>唐末及五代已来，方镇守臣每有替移，或召赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159942_comment'></div>其间倔强武臣，多是妄皏军情，不时受代，因致跋扈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159942_comment'></div>国初惩方镇之弊，尽去此态，禀朝廷进退约束，无敢违异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159942_comment'></div>臣窃见近日以来，沿边征镇总兵帅守，累有本辖将吏例状举留者，此风不可启其渐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159942_comment'></div>欲乞下诸路转运使，今后更不许诸军将校使臣等列状举留本辖帅守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159942_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1159942_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　以时属饥灾，列郡多事。彦博牒辖下州军，刑狱承例酌情，便宜决遣。作品：《乞别定益利钤辖司画一条贯》<div id='poem_1159977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞别定益利钤辖司画一条贯奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159977")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159977'>臣勘会益、利钤辖司以所部去朝廷远，承前体例，事由便宜裁决，所以上体倚寄之重，亦以安服远人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159977_comment'></div>二广虽亦遐远，权其事体，轻重不侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159977_comment'></div>均顺之事，耳目未远，故朝廷择守，比他蕃镇绝重，举西南事一以委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159977_comment'></div>庆历六年臣知益州，时属饥蔺，列郡多事，贼盗兴起，刑狱淹延，事稍有疑，例欲奏决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159977_comment'></div>臣勘会得益、利路钤辖司多是承例酌情，便宜区断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159977_comment'></div>寻曾牒辖下州军，今后勘到合行奏听敕旨公案，且先申当司，以凭相度，其间有别无疑虑，或情轻法重，可以末减，情重法轻当从严断者，率皆便宜决遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159977_comment'></div>内有事状必难裁处，方敢奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159977_comment'></div>兼朝廷不以为非，在川蜀甚以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159977_comment'></div>迩来事体，与昔颇殊，处置之间，或多龃龉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159977_comment'></div>今本路提刑司累奏乞别定钤辖司画一条贯，犹恐本路钤辖司今来依旧引用臣庆历六年川蜀饥蔺之时权宜公牒，致监司官频有论列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159977_comment'></div>欲乞送刑法司依本路提刑司别定钤辖司画一条贯，所贵经久遵守施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159977_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1159977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　为灯笼锦以献张贵妃。张文为世交，贵妃父尧封尝为彦博父洎门客，张贵妃认彦博为伯父。或曰乃彦博夫人遗张贵妃，彦博不知。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1569d567e355440683eeb26ce4d21a41_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1569d567e355440683eeb26ce4d21a41");'><span id='1569d567e355440683eeb26ce4d21a41_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1047')">1046-1047年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='1569d567e355440683eeb26ce4d21a41' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　举李九言。作品：《举李九言》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160220?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举李九言劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160220")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160220'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160220'>臣切见太常博士李九言明经登第，学术精深，施行为政，动有规法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160220_comment'></div>前任益州通判，益州适值歉岁，与臣协力赈济饥民、备见绩效，今已得替到阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160220_comment'></div>切缘益州通判得替旧例，皆有皗陟差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160220_comment'></div>近因臣僚争授益州通判，遂停旧例，止得循资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160220_comment'></div>而九言之职劳未录，首为新制所限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160220_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷体察，特赐皗陟任使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160220_comment'></div>或悉其学术，任以检讨之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160220_comment'></div>如经擢用后犯正入己赃，或举不如状，臣甘连坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160220_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1160220_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年3月21日</a>　拜枢密副使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年3月23日</a>　改参知政事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　张俞为文送彦博归觐。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1f52b07d0e67428c89f4187fab4bf7c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1f52b07d0e67428c89f4187fab4bf7c3");'><span id='1f52b07d0e67428c89f4187fab4bf7c3_link' id='poem_title_494892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题纪太尉庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494892")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494906'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494906'>脩竹荫清溪，潺湲阙塞西。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494906'>石床平有藓，沙路润无泥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494906'>粉白松围古<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，蓝生草带齐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494906'>难留批敕字，救旱作云霓<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：李藩少时隐居溪上。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494906'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494906_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_494906'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_494906_0'>⑴ 自注：有古松皮绿而粉，生《本草》艾纳香，真庙爱之，驻跸良久。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494906_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494904")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494904'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494904'>赫奕晨霞照万灯，路穿阙口势如吞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494904'>桥边杨柳垂青线，林下鞦韆挂䌽绳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494904'>平地伊流不一抹，半天嵩岳翠千层。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494904'>行行渐入吾疆理，竹坞松阡间绮塍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494904_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494904'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　作慈照大师真赞。作品：《慈照大师真赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一三。）</span><div id='poem_1160324' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160324' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160324?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈照大师真赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160324")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160324_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160324'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160324'>嘉祐中，余保釐洛师，屡游阙塞，始见幽公于宝应精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160324_comment'></div>听其言简而旨，睹其相静而定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160324_comment'></div>又其朋智渐，法苑之秀也，亦谓余曰：「幽公博通教典，潜悟禅那，苦行精进，为流辈所推」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160324_comment'></div>余后数与之谈，渐之言信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160324_comment'></div>伊西竹坞，积庆兰若，爰集净众，日严钟梵，以奉先公之卜宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160324_comment'></div>幽公乐是胥宇，惠然肯来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160324_comment'></div>亦既宴止，遂有终焉之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160324_comment'></div>未几寂化，其徒悲涕慕思，图形瞻礼，以永归依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160324_comment'></div>谓余为大檀越，来乞赞云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160324_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160324'>师行惟幽，师心为寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160324_comment'></div>就名观义，循理索迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160324_comment'></div>性相皆空，了不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160324_comment'></div>胡为形容，设色之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160324_comment'></div>即空即空，传写无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160324_comment'></div>四众瞻仰，悚然信恭。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1160324'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1160324_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　乞赐何涉赠官，优录其子孙。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　力荐龙昌期。后诏赐龙昌期五品服，绢百匹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　被龙昌期责备不能为其辨明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月17日</a>　封潞国公。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_494946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494946'>两桨夷犹去，双凫上下逢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494946'>馀波通洛浦，倒影浸嵩峰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494946'>荷动闻鱼跃，沙平见鹤踪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494946'>岛蒲森剑戟，岸柳亚虬龙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_494946_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_494946'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_494946_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游楚谏议园宅，有诗记之。作品：《游楚谏议园宅呈留守宣徽留守端明王君贶司马君实》<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494947'>五里依仁宅，西邻数仞墙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494947'>主人为屏翰<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：楚今帅环庆。）</span>，园吏占风光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494947'>藓色沿茶灶，松阴覆石床。<div id='poem_sentence_4_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_494947'>一区诚可乐，三径莫令荒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_494947'>有木皆交荫，无花不并芳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_494947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_494947'>相期挂冠后，同此事琴觞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495088'>如今白发游河叟，半是清朝解绶人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495088'>喜向园林同燕集，更缘樽酒长精神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495088'>欢言预<sup class='reference ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年1月3日</a>　为文记御赐诗事。作品：《御赐诗记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》佚文。）</span><div id='poem_1160318' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160318' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160318?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御赐诗记<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰四年正月三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年1月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160318")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160318_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160318'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160318'>元丰三年季秋，皇帝行大飨之礼于明堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160318_comment'></div>臣方守魏，被召侍祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160318_comment'></div>大礼庆成后四日，特蒙制恩进位太尉，保釐洛郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160318_comment'></div>臣犬马之年，七十有五，前此累年章十数上，以求致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160318_comment'></div>圣慈俯怜旧物，曲念老臣，皆未之许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160318_comment'></div>今复优进公位，俾守别都，自顾衰残，非敢当克，俯伏辞避，至于再三，讫不获命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160318_comment'></div>乃以闰月二十三日陛辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160318_comment'></div>翌日出都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160318_comment'></div>仍锡宴于琼林苑，悉以二府大臣押伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160318_comment'></div>既又临遣中使，内出宝器，俾釂天醴，以极鱼藻之乐，及赐御诗以宠其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160318_comment'></div>臣伏思蒙厚恩，荷殊渥，自近世逮本朝以来，未有其比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160318_comment'></div>则有弼臣惇奉诏作序，事义详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160318_comment'></div>臣虽穷极语言，不能尽意，惟知负戴天地生成之德，感极而继之以泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160318_comment'></div>恭惟陛下聪明睿智，焕乎有文，帝庸作歌，光绍前典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160318_comment'></div>伏自临御以来，十有四载，而英韶之韵，云汉之章，百执愿闻，万物思睹者久矣，曾未之得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160318_comment'></div>夫何老臣，首蒙天赐，至荣至幸，超绝等伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160318_comment'></div>始在都门，则已传布于宫省；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160318_comment'></div>寻抵洛宅，又得诊示于吏民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160318_comment'></div>是用图金刻石，以永其传，将与夫日月并期，天地同久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160318_comment'></div>复使臣之子子孙孙相继率励，保之守之，亦克永世，至于老臣为不朽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160318_comment'></div>元丰四年正月三日，河东节度、管内观察处置等使、守太尉、开府仪同三司、行太原尹、判河南府事、西京留守司公事、兼畿内劝农使、上柱国、潞国公、食邑二万三千六百户、食实封一万一百户臣文彦博谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1160318_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160318'><span class='label'>按：</span>《六艺之一录》卷九六，文渊阁四库全书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1160318_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年</a>　洛人于资圣殿为彦博建生祠，名曰“伫瞻”堂。请司马光为文以记之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年4月</a>　奏民间承佃牧马草地事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年6月</a>　乞体量西京灾伤。作品：《奏西京灾伤事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1160024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160024?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏西京灾伤事<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰四年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1081年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160024")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160024'>臣体量得西京畿内诸县，今春以来，麦苗极盛，有望丰登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160024_comment'></div>无何自四月、五月中直至收获之际，大雨频并，继日不止，遂至颇损麦苗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160024_comment'></div>所存者三四分，须且趁时收割上场，所冀收拾残馀，粗救饥困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160024_comment'></div>臣体访得所收多者，仅及三四分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160024_comment'></div>日有人户经官披诉苗伤，又缘官吏拘文，为已收割在场，及有持打了者，不以为凭，须得存留，查苗在地，方可验覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160024_comment'></div>今若不与检放，必致人户逃移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160024_comment'></div>况今夏多雨害稼，众所明知，难为巧诈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160024_comment'></div>伏望朝廷特降指挥，下本路转运司子细体量，实有灾伤，即早与减放分数，所贵人户不致逃移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160024_comment'></div>更望朝廷矜察，早降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160024_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1160024_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年7月</a>　兵分五路，大举伐西夏。彦博拒内侍王中正募禁兵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1081&endYear=1081')">1081年12月</a>　奏以民间疾苦，恳请恤民，乞师不可再举。作品：《论西事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年10月</a>　彦博生日，时知徐州赵鼎送彦博黄石茶瓯、怀素千字文作为生日贺礼。作品：《彭门贤守器之度支赵鼎记余生日过形善祝并惠黄石茶瓯怀素千字文一轴辄成拙诗仰答来意》<span id='poem_content_494726'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494726'>使从徐方来，执讯如双鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494726'>遗我黄石器，副之怀素书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494726'>素书与黄石，得之宜在徐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494726'>或在圯桥下，或在留城墟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494726_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495099'>春光垂欲尽，夏景渐增添。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495099'>郁郁松篁茂，萧萧风雨兼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495099'>花心随絮落，屐齿被苔粘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495099'>巧啭莺迁木，惊飞燕入帘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495099'>虾须穿曲沼，虎爪度前檐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495099'>坐久香销炷，吟多笔费尖。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495099'>云容方霭霭，日色未炎炎。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495099'>舞鹤倾丹顶，游龟散绿髯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495099'>命宾常务率，出令更须严。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495099'>诗咏当阶药，书寻傍架签。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495099'>兰芬衣可袭，露润草俱沾。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495099'>贵近辞金马，编脩赐玉蟾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495099'>高欢<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作怀）</span>惟自适，独乐未尝厌。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495099'>赤白曾咨丙，丹青每诮阎。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495099'>冲和缘养浩，寂寞为安恬。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495099'>身处贫无愧，心贪道不廉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495099'>成文推大手，济用鄙轻缣。<div id='poem_sentence_16_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_495099'>视履循清节，祈恩陋杂占。<div id='poem_sentence_17_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_495099'>闻韶欣凤舞，在藻爱鱼潜。<div id='poem_sentence_18_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_495099'>鲈鲙思鱼艇，貂冠望酒帘。<div id='poem_sentence_19_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_495099'>圣时非吏隐，贤业系民瞻。<div id='poem_sentence_20_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_495099'>抚事惟公论，摛辞乃自谦。<div id='poem_sentence_21_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_495099'>保躬诚易退，康世义难淹。<div id='poem_sentence_22_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_495099'>颣句惭无取，酬言幸不嫌。<div id='poem_sentence_23_495099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_495099'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_495099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年4月</a>　乞运河至白马寺与洛河会合。作品：《奏西京漕河事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二五。）</span><div id='poem_1160025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160025?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏西京漕河事<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰六年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160025")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160025'>本府勘会自会通桥下至白马寺洛河水路，滩碛浅涩，难行纲运，遂奏乞开淘古漕河旧道，稍令深阔，抵至白马寺，却合洛河，回避二十馀里滩碛，所贵通行纲船，不致滞碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160025_comment'></div>今蒙朝旨依奏施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160025_comment'></div>看详中诸内更带下白波辇运司奏，乞开浚漕河至偃师县界，合洛河，通济舟船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160025_comment'></div>虽与本府所奏事状大抵皆同，只是称至偃师县界漕口合流，必添展地里稍远，须至更差官觑步所碾添开浚故道地步、长短及地形高下，是与不是有古来河道，确实计定功料申上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　作亭于河上，名曰“漕河新亭”<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_495017_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　夏，与韩绛、司马光会饮，有诗记之。作品：《留守相公和提举端明作三寿公字韵诗辄继前韵》<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　秋，彦博与洛下诸贤饮于东田池上苇间，浩然有江湖之趣，作诗以记之。作品：《余前此二纪，保厘西郊，与判台李少师及洛社诸君游龙门，饮伊上。有渔者献鳜鱼十数尾……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_495028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>余前此二纪保釐西郊与判台李少师及洛社诸君游龙门饮伊上有渔者献鳜鱼十数尾因作羹鲙坐客有思鲈之兴余后守魏累请休致久而未遂曾为忆鳜诗寄洛下诸贤今年秋累与诸君饮于东田池上苇间鲙鱼炊香稻以佐酒浩然有江湖之趣因作是诗并录忆鳜诗如左<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰中留守西京作）</span></a><span class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495019'>八节惊涛鼍振鼓，千花宝塔雁翔云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495019'>岩隈雨过飞泉涨，谷口风回堕叶纷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495019'>龛穴隆穹三像列，楼台华焕两崖分。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495019'>方陪茜旆来寻胜，不就蒲飧趁茹荤。<div id='poem_sentence_4_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_495019'>北里笙竽皆拥从，东山罗绮半酣醺。<div id='poem_sentence_5_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_495019'>升堂共睹皤仙貌，策杖同寻古士坟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_495019'>喜脱貂冠亲野老，幸随态轼附邦君。<div id='poem_sentence_7_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_495019'>林峦岑寂真堪赏，市井喧哗渐厌闻。<div id='poem_sentence_8_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_495019'>人度长川犹隐映，香销古殿尚氛氲。<div id='poem_sentence_9_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_495019'>周生归后兰重佩，荀令行时蕙更薰。<div id='poem_sentence_10_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_495019'>晓露未晞珠滴泪，秋花争发锦挑文。<div id='poem_sentence_11_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_495019'>群娃散步尘生袜，小舫争登水溅裙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_495019'>钓叟傍观皆叹羡，禅师迎谒尽欢欣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_495019'>既无冗局羁闲迹，忍促回轩背夕曛。<div id='poem_sentence_14_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_495019'>得向石头溪上饮，从今遂不畏移文<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_495019'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_495019_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_495019'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495019_0'>⑴ 原作浅，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_495019_1'>⑵ 自注：旧说禹凿龙门以泄汝海之水。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_495019_0'>⑶ 自注：某在北都，累求致政，时驾曹林员外以《映山红》曲词见赠，寻答之。其末章云：遂请后，顾频醉石楼溪口。今饮于石楼，有小娼独得此曲，因此佐饮。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_495019_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1084&endYear=1084')">1084年</a>　席汝言在洛城种金橘，秋结六实，以其四献彦博，彦博、韩绛、司马光均有诗纪此事。作品：《次韵留守相公洛中金橘》<span id='poem_sentence_3_495125_0'>⑵ 自注：臣受命判河南府，蒙赐御诗一章。自后得请致政归洛，又蒙赐御诗二章。恩礼之厚，中外荣观。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_495125_0'>⑶ 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月</a>　奏请受西夏内附之请，以安边。作品：《缴进元丰答诏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二六。）</span><div id='poem_1160028' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160028' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160028?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴进元丰答诏奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160028")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160028_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160028'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160028'>臣数年前判河南府日，见调发师兵进讨西夏，受国恩深，形于过计，遂累具章疏论列利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160028_comment'></div>蒙先帝圣恩，专差臣男贻庆赐臣答诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160028_comment'></div>仰详诏意，乃知先帝本意，止务安边，不欲轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160028_comment'></div>皆是边臣希望功赏，为国生事，侥痈万一，以致兵食困匮，财力殚耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160028_comment'></div>今闻于道路之言，西人欲求内附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160028_comment'></div>臣以谓蛮夷猾夏，尧舜之时，所不能免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160028_comment'></div>伏望陛下恢天海之量，广示开纳，御四夷之术，羁縻而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160028_comment'></div>由此可以偃兵，止固吾圉，外夷怀服，中夏安宁，太平之风，浸隆浸久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160028_comment'></div>臣又以朝廷举事，必较利害，唯务开疆以希功赏，即不知用兵之时所费钱粮若干，得地之后所入租赋若干，凡一岁屯戍兵马所费粮草之直若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160028_comment'></div>若所得不偿所费远甚，即是竭中原生民之膏血，以事荒远无用之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160028_comment'></div>此乃唐开元之末，务赏边功，边臣各求徼幸，致中原困竭，唐业下衰，可为商炮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160028_comment'></div>今因西人请命，伏望朝廷熟计而审处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160028_comment'></div>老臣不胜区区忧国之心，迫于倾输，言无伦次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160028_comment'></div>所有前者蒙先帝所赐降诏书，辄敢进呈，所贵详知先帝素志，惟在安边，不务轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160028_comment'></div>谨具奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160028_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1160028'>元丰五年，李舜举过洛，先帝意旨止令边臣自固边鄙，多如臣所受诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160028_comment'></div>尔后以徐禧南方书生，不晓边事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160028_comment'></div>继之李稷急于官赏，妄有开陈经画，遂至永乐败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160028_comment'></div>臣荷先帝异恩，去年钦蒙赐御诗，云「嘉言时幸寄东车」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160028_comment'></div>臣亦仰和圣制，有「愿倾丹恳上公车」之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160028_comment'></div>去年三月，西人由熙河路入朝，求内附，臣即欲密启所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160028_comment'></div>未几，先帝不豫，遂止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160028_comment'></div>今西人复来，须至有此开陈，望圣明照察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1160028_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年闰2月</a>　司马光左仆射兼门下侍郎。再荐彦博。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年3月15日</a>　答太皇太后咨访诏。作品：《答奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年</a>　司马光又上奏，坚拒位彦博上，乞文彦博行左仆射事，己行右仆射事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='27ed9c97135d40b180c9774f6c76d39a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("27ed9c97135d40b180c9774f6c76d39a");'><span id='27ed9c97135d40b180c9774f6c76d39a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1091')">1090-1091年</a>，85-86岁</div><div id='27ed9c97135d40b180c9774f6c76d39a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　琼林苑设宴饯送彦博。苏辙、苏颂有赠别诗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年4月29日</a>　至洛阳，范纯仁有诗相迎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　西都留守韩缜赠诗迎彦博归，并惠台什，赞誉彦博。作品：《某再获谢事归老洛师留守相公玉汝宠惠台什过形奖予谨达来贶》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_495038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>某再获谢事归老洛师留守相公<span class='inlineComment2'>（玉汝）</span>宠惠台什过形奖予谨达来贶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495038")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495038'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495038'>二圣恩深念老臣，许从休退乐伊滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495038'>重观景物皆尘迹，喜见居留是故人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495038'>林下放怀无检束，樽前道旧长精神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495038'>公难久作东田伴，却作黄枢秉化钧。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495038'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年5月</a>　洛下旱灾，彦博奏勤恤民隐。作品：《奏勤恤民隐事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_1160067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏勤恤民隐事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐五年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160067")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160067'>臣于四月二十九日至西京，见本京进奏官申状录报皇帝、太皇太后诏书，以历时灾旱，宿麦几尽，秋稼未立，上轸圣念，引咎归己，特减常膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160067_comment'></div>有以见圣心焦劳，得尧汤罪己应天之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160067_comment'></div>然臣向在都下，每见西来使命，询其雨泽稼穑次第，多云近已得雨，苗稼滋茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160067_comment'></div>臣既出京到洛，见缘路民田宿麦秋稼，悉如圣诏所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160067_comment'></div>深虑向去小民艰食，即聚为寇盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160067_comment'></div>伏望严敕监司，觉察守令，勤恤民隐，勿致烦扰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160067_comment'></div>及督责巡检、县尉，屏除贼盗，令境内清肃，人户安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160067_comment'></div>救荒之政，各在疚心，诸事预防，庶无后患。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1160067_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年5月8日</a>　洛下大雨。彦博与韩缜有喜雨诗唱和。作品：《留守相公宠示喜雨雅章曲有推借……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_495039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>留守相公宠示喜雨雅章曲有推借谨抒鄙意上答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年5月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495039")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_495039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495039'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495039'>嵩阴累昼结层阴，一夕霶沱济物深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495039'>稼穑首资千亩籍，焦劳顿释两宫心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495039'>高台便有凉风至，奥室全无暑气侵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495039'>利泽定知均率土，保釐再起作商霖。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495039'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_495039_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　庶民急于田事，彦博乞暂罢词讼追扰，以免有妨田事。作品：《奏久旱乞不追扰事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三○。）</span><div id='poem_1160068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏久旱乞不追扰事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐五年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160068")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160068'>臣闻化国之日舒以长，盖不夺农时，不妨民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160068_comment'></div>故日力有馀而岁收有望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160068_comment'></div>臣窃以自春以来，时雨愆亢，人情惶惶，谓必艰食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160068_comment'></div>至今月八日，大雨鳏霈，庶民鼓舞，急于田事，老幼就功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160068_comment'></div>力穑有秋，正在今日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160068_comment'></div>臣虑州县亲民之官，不知农事之急，以小小词讼，勾追證逮，禁系淹延，至于随司门留，亦皆拘系，颇妨农作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160068_comment'></div>臣欲乞下诸路久旱郡县，当此农事急切之时，民间小可词讼鲑争，一切且罢追扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160068_comment'></div>除事干人命及劫贼急切公事，即依常施行。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1160068'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1160068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　诏依前任宰臣添赐彦博公使钱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　苏辙有书贺致仕。<br /><a id='poem_sentence_3_495067'>昔日相君曾降顾，常忧蜗陋不容车。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_495067'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年</a>　韩缜于中和堂之西特设毡帐，题曰“醉眠庵”，供彦博休憩，彦博有和诗。作品：留守相公玉汝于中和堂之西偏别设毡帐……仍改题所憩为醉眠庵……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span>《前日蒙留守相公玉汝延饮于中和新堂仍别设毡帐令羸老暂憩……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_495046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前日蒙留守相公玉汝延饮于中和新堂仍别设毡幄欲令羸老暂憩翌日小娃已传其说辄成小诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1090年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_sentence_0_495046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495046'>何似奇章南涧上，别开一室待焦先。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495046'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年8月</a>　言官言彦博荐邓温伯事，以为黄景善邓温伯，故嘱彦博召之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年9月</a>　楚建中亡，作挽词悼念之。作品：《楚正议建中挽诗三章》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_495165' class='_poem'><div href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495165")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495165'>出处交游五十春，洛城晚岁卜亲邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495165'>东斋锦襻清谈处，今日重来泪满襟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495165_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495165'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495165_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_495166' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495166' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495166?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495166'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495166'>大抵神存体不留，万安山<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>下宅松楸。<div id='poem_note_495166_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_495167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495167?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span id='poem_content_495167'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495167'>每读龟书鸿范篇，人间五福是高年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495167_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
