id='poem_sentence_2_495167'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_495167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　偶遇洛中士人张起宗，与彦博生辰同，彦博邀之共案而食近九个月。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年6月</a>　温锡心献马于彦博以修敬。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　辞子文及进职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年7月</a>　赐温锡心所献马与彦博。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年8月</a>　西夏生事，彦博奏请为计以缓之，勿以争小利而开边隙。作品：奏西边事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三○。）</span><div id='poem_1160069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏西边事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐六年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160069")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160069'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160069'>臣近得赵卨书云：「金城疆界未定，止缘新垒侵占稍多，虏情未易弃舍，至今迁延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160069_comment'></div>若非朝廷坚守大信，终始羁縻，必恐再开边隙，民力岂易堪邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160069_comment'></div>臣又见卨之奏草云：「宥州累牒称，兰州等处将自来无人守把城寨，设计暗差人骑守把，却称是元丰年修筑，乃是昏赖之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160069_comment'></div>验此南界边官，不欲夏国与朝廷通好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160069_comment'></div>况延州是自来有事计会之所，今又一向就利自党，此等事情，何处分雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160069_comment'></div>若又一向固拒，全不听采，夏国亦虑难尽臣子之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160069_comment'></div>今来贼意己穷，兼称无处分雪，必恐作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160069_comment'></div>此隙一开，边吏邀功之人，乘间盗利，冒昧朝廷恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160069_comment'></div>彼诚自甘其心，生灵何所负耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160069_comment'></div>臣重惜朝廷顿累年恩信，一旦争尺寸之利，而失安边之大计」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160069_comment'></div>臣详赵卨之奏甚切，亦恐边吏争小利以邀功赏，为国生事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160069_comment'></div>臣伏睹二圣临御以来，威抚夷狄，皆得其心，边境不耸，中夏安宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160069_comment'></div>今来夏国有此赴诉，赵卨又有奏陈，臣虽未知其详，伏望令三省熟计而审处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160069_comment'></div>若事未明白，未能便决定可否间，且令赵卨徐报之，如唐郭元振之答吐蕃，论钦陵之请，无直塞其来意，且为计以缓之，使其恶意不得顿萌，亦御戎之中策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160069_comment'></div>臣又料此贼计，见朝廷以其恭顺，不疑其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160069_comment'></div>自去冬今春，以边储有限，直罢西边戍兵数万，即谓边备已解，恐乘此作过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160069_comment'></div>臣以谓不得不过虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160069_comment'></div>谨具奏闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1160069_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年11月</a>　韩缜徙判太原府，彦博有贺诗。作品：贺经略太尉相公玉汝移镇太原》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_495068' id='poem_sentence_0_495126'>九年四海被清晖，瑞彩重轮照殿帏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495126'>间日视朝觐<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作勤）</span>旰食，未明思政事宵衣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495126'>存心庶务劳千虑，决意真游厌万机。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495126'>下土颙颙望霄汉，仙舆直指厚陵归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_495126_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_495127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495127'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495127'>老臣八十惭尸素，挂了貂冠归洛阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495127'>芝诏荐临优眷注，蒲轮促起预平章。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_495127'>重辞禁幄犹如昨，今迓灵舆益自伤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_495127_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_495127'>勉<sup class='reference -----title
青州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='086c807ef956473bbf199bbcef7bf7ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("086c807ef956473bbf199bbcef7bf7ce");'><span id='086c807ef956473bbf199bbcef7bf7ce_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　荐黄庶于朝廷，授黄庶青州通判，庶有谢启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　书青州布衣张在诗于兴龙寺老柏院壁以传之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　与知许州宋庠有诗唱和。作品：《予移守青社同年宋学士代予守璧田会有来诗……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_494860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>予移守青社同年宋学士代予守壁<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作璧）</span>田会有来诗因成四十言为答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494860")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494860'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494860'>旧许陪原郡，时清偃息优。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494860'>羡君熊轼去，夺我鸭坡游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494860'>草树秋方密，禽鱼晚思幽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494860'>相凭皆与问，犹忆醉翁不<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494860'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_494860'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_494860_0'>⑴ 自注：予在许昌，务闲多适，湖上吟醉，月三四焉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494860_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　作题裴晋公画像，并序。作品：《题裴晋公画像赞并序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一三。）</span><div id='poem_1160323' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160323' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160323?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题裴晋公画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160323")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160323_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160323'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160323'>尚书郎武功苏才翁得裴晋公画像于大资政富公，谓与家藏旧本正类，因以相示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160323_comment'></div>予尝读裴公自题《写真赞》，有「灵台莫状」之句，意公负其所蕴，谦不自言，俟他人发明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160323_comment'></div>而当时多嫉公勋德，或云平蔡者愬，公何与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160323_comment'></div>又逢吉党谬为谣言以倾公，独赖正人讼其诬枉，仅免于祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160323_comment'></div>虽宗闵素出其门，犹憾不引为相，挤公于梁，则于其时孰肯扬公之羭？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160323_comment'></div>后世史官于公无嫌，追书公美，近乎实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160323_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160323_comment'></div>岂群邪丑正，见抑于当时耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160323_comment'></div>将贵远贱近，人之常情耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160323_comment'></div>予仰公之风，睹公之像，因原公意，辄续公赞：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160323'>绘事虽巧，传神写照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160323_comment'></div>公之灵台，孰观其妙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160323_comment'></div>灵台崇崇，含和处中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160323_comment'></div>经始勿亟，积善累功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160323_comment'></div>贤人之业，仗义资忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160323_comment'></div>人不吾誉，吾不为沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160323_comment'></div>人不吾毁，吾不为喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160323_comment'></div>窃揆公意，如是而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1160323_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年闰7月4日</a>　徙知秦州，实未赴。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7ade963e966c42828d8382fbf6dcf4d4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7ade963e966c42828d8382fbf6dcf4d4");'><span id='7ade963e966c42828d8382fbf6dcf4d4_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年8月12日</a>　徙知永兴军兼秦凤路兵马事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　黄庶有贺彦博徙永兴军启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　举陈湜。作品：《举陈湜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举陈湜劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160199")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160199_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160199'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160199'>臣奉敕差充永兴军一路都部署、安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160199_comment'></div>切见太常博士陈卜久在河东、陜西差遣，深晓边事军政，欲乞差本官管勾永兴军一路都部署安抚使司机宜文字，只理本官合入差遣资序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160199_comment'></div>右取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　举冯诰充秦凤路置制勾当公事。作品：《举冯诰任允孚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160200' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160200' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160200?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举冯诰任允孚劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160200")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160200_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160200'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160200'>臣奉敕差充永兴军一路都部署兼置制秦凤路军马司公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160200_comment'></div>缘秦凤日近频有番界事宜，须藉经谙本处事体才干官吏，逐急差使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160200_comment'></div>一、臣切见屯田郎中冯诰，曾任秦凤路都监及通判秦州，首尾六年，并准朝廷指挥，令管勾番部公事，深谙秦州东西路番情边事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160200_comment'></div>本官见合入知州差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160200_comment'></div>臣欲乞差充秦凤路置制勾当公事，兼不妨本官待阙差遣，亦无侥痈，只候沿边置制稍有伦序，却令发赴本任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160200_comment'></div>一、臣切见太常博士任允孚，自庆历三年差管勾秦凤路经略司机宜文字，及通判秦州，至去年方替，在彼十年，深谙事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160200_comment'></div>臣今欲乞差本官管勾秦凤路置制司机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160200_comment'></div>右，取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1160200_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　举任允孚差本官管勾秦凤路置制司机宜文字。作品：《举冯诰任允孚》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160200' class='_poem'><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　举邵叔元充伏羌寨监押。作品：《举邵叔元》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160201' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160201' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160201?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举邵叔元劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160201")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160201_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160201'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160201'>臣切见三班奉职李昌来臣处公参，云：奉宣差权秦州伏羌寨监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160201_comment'></div>切缘伏羌是秦州西路最大城寨，控三都谷、文嬴开两路自来屯兵之处，及体当西路事宜，全藉得力寨主监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160201_comment'></div>兼向来多近上或带职班行充寨主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160201_comment'></div>今来寨主是殿直谢育，又差李昌权监押，恐不能弹压番汉公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160201_comment'></div>臣勘会秦州三阳寨监押、殿直邵叔元在秦州差遣十馀年，深谙彼处番情边事，兼有心力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160201_comment'></div>欲乞就差邵叔元充伏羌塞监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160201_comment'></div>勘会东路治坊寨监押已及二年，却乞差李昌权治坊监押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160201_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1160201_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　举曹弼充宁远寨主。作品：《举曹弼》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160202' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160202' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160202?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举曹弼劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160202")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160202_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160202'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160202'>臣切见秦州陇城寨监押、侍禁曹弼好人材，有胆勇方略，在秦州差遣首尾十年，深谙边情，今欲满替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160202_comment'></div>勘会秦州宁远寨在西路极边，兼寨主尹宝臣自到任三年有馀，欲乞就差曹弼充宁远寨主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160202_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160202_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　乞特赐门客张度一试衔名目。授其将作监主簿。作品：《举张度》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160203' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160203' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160203?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_1160203_comment'></div>况近制奏荐门客，更不理选出官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160203_comment'></div>张度欲乞特赐一试衔名目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160203_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1160203_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　乞分屯秦州戎兵于永兴、泾原、环庆三路。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　奏请秋收以前，差人晓谕秦凤泾原番部，为清野之计。作品：《乞令团结秦凤泾原番部》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159953?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令团结秦凤泾原番部奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159953")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159953_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159953'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159953'>臣切见秦凤、泾原沿边熟户番部，比诸路最多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159953_comment'></div>至秋成以来，禾稼牛羊满野，以致饵寇诲盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159953_comment'></div>臣乞下逐路经略使，每至秋成以前，散差得力知番情使臣、牙校，赍番字委曲晓谕部族，逐急早收田稼，凭附险固，窖藏斛㪷，收拾老小牛羊，为清野之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159953_comment'></div>其强壮人马，各令常切团结，探候番寇若来钞掠，量力御敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159953_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1159953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　乞指挥诸路帅开报。作品：《乞指挥诸路帅开报事宜》<span target='_blank'>乞指挥诸路帅开报事宜奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159954")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159954_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159954'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159954'>臣切见西人康定、庆历中每犯边，即于诸路各张声势，务欲牵制，疲弊汉兵，其实入寇，即并力从一路而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159954_comment'></div>故边兵常苦寡少，分布不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159954_comment'></div>臣欲乞严切指挥诸路帅臣，每探得事宜，更相开报，常须各作出师之备，先为牵制贼势，庶几贼兵亦自后顾，不敢并力专从一路而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159954_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1159954_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　乞令边帅练兵约束诸将。作品：《乞令边帅练兵约束诸将》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159955' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159955' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159955?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令边帅练兵约束诸将奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159955")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159955_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159955'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159955'>臣切见自庆历初，陜西四路之兵，逐路始分数将，每将马步不下三二千人，各自训练，务要精熟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159955_comment'></div>兼得兵将相谙，使唤之际，尽知人人所能，则鲜败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159955_comment'></div>近闻诸将多不和同，大帅罕能统制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159955_comment'></div>教阅部分，各立异见，宽猛之节，不得中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159955_comment'></div>徇情銂怨，由此而生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159955_comment'></div>师克在和，有异于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159955_comment'></div>伏乞严戒逐路大帅讲求军法，精加训练，约束诸将，务在和同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159955_comment'></div>兵声稍振，边寇自畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159955_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159955_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1159955'>旧法，逐路分诸将者，盖欲居常则兵将相谙，临敌则指纵如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159955_comment'></div>小警即量遣一将而出，稍重即又加一将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159955_comment'></div>或岁月更番，出屯外寨，若遇大敌，即诸将尽合为一军，大帅亲总而节制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159955_comment'></div>此制军之法，颇得其要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159955_comment'></div>近时兵官多不原本此意，欲罢旧制，乞朝廷详察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1159955_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　乞差译语官。作品：《乞差译语官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159957' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159957?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞差译语官奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159957")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159957_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159957'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159957'>臣切见秦州每有蕃部过陈番字及口说事理，只凭本州逐寨引领译语官翻译。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159957_comment'></div>其间多是回避事理，改易情状，番部汉官各不知觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159957_comment'></div>缘此欺弊，致失番情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159957_comment'></div>臣切虑今秦州有属户番官知臣致任，乞来公参，或陈过番字，若只凭本处引领译语官，恐依前欺罔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159957_comment'></div>乞于泾原路译语官内抽差二人于臣处祗应，准备互换翻译，以防癚弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159957_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1159957_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　聘张载为学官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　于居处作见山楼。作品：《见山楼小饮偶作》<span id='poem_title_494891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答王龙图咏山见寄<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本下有素字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494891")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494891_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494891'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494891'>分得鱼符守雍州，垂帷闭阁再经秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494891'>眼看岩岫将登览，身似匏瓜苦滞留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494891'>杜曲朱坡虽已到，圭峰紫阁未曾游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494891'>却输假道归朝客，上遍终南寺寺楼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494891_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494891'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　有石苍舒所藏褚遂良《圣教序》墨迹摹本，客以公所临本为真迹，笑客之谀。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　智息陕西铁钱风波。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　奏请增贵铁价，以绝私铸铁钱事。作品：《奏陕西铁钱事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159958' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159958' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159958?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏陕西铁钱事</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159958")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159958_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159958'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159958'>陜西私铸铁钱，虽严行禁捕，抵法者甚众，终不能止绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159958_comment'></div>盖以铁本至贱，获利甚厚，以致见行钱货薄恶者多，物价增长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159958_comment'></div>稍禁行用，或令拣选，即市井嚣然，买卖难阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159958_comment'></div>其弊已极，须当制置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159958_comment'></div>若便变钱法，即恐未能，徒成惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159958_comment'></div>不若使铁价增贵，即私铸无利，薄恶之钱，亦将矪为器用，自然百物价平，民不犯禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159958_comment'></div>欲乞令陜西转运司依河东路事体擘画，权住铁冶三五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159958_comment'></div>或恐伤冶户，即官榷数年，增起铁价，公私有利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159958_comment'></div>候钱法平定，即弛铁禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159958_comment'></div>议者或虑铁贵则农器鼎釜之属，民家乏用，此必不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159958_comment'></div>且农器鼎釜，民家各素有之物，非日日市易而用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159958_comment'></div>或破碎，即故铁尚在，创买者亦少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159958_comment'></div>设有小害，须从大利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1159958_comment'></div>乞蚤赐指挥陜西都转运使疾速相度施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1159958_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　奏永兴军衙前理欠事，乞体量衙前欠折之苦。作品：《奏永兴军衙前理欠陪备》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一七。）</span><div id='poem_1159961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏永兴军衙前理欠陪备</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159961")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159961'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159961'>臣见永兴军枷固衙前催里欠折官物者不少，遂一一根问，多是主管仓场、馆驿、清酒务之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159961_comment'></div>迹其欠折之由，悉非侵欺盗用，皆因陪备不充，官中又不与体量处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159961_comment'></div>如清酒务年计出卖煮酒，而官不给煮酒柴，或量给而用不足者，般请曲米、合使脚力及诸杂琐细用具，尽令衙前专副陪备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159961_comment'></div>又仓场贮纳，只令专副自办铺衬之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159961_comment'></div>馆驿当东西大路，使命如织，供应馆券，多要本色，省估之外，亦是专副陪备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159961_comment'></div>被刑破产，率由于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159961_comment'></div>凡此数事，惟永兴军方令官自擘画，粗有条理，稍纾衙前欠折之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159961_comment'></div>其馀州军，亦乞更下陜西转运司体量施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159961_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1159961'>已上件事，臣在永兴日，与傅永、田京等方欲商议，节次施行，值臣被召赴阙，切虑中辍，故乞举行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1159961_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月11日</a>　除昭文相。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='aa12ee17d4054b94a0d32907c3d477c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa12ee17d4054b94a0d32907c3d477c3");'><span id='aa12ee17d4054b94a0d32907c3d477c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年4月</a>　移判永兴军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　举张掞。作品：《举张掞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　举刘航、李希逸、赵士宏。作品：《举刘航等》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举刘航等劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160228")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160228'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160228'>臣切见屯田郎中、白波都大提举辇运刘航，驾部员外郎、提举在京仓草场李希逸，知永州、比部员外郎赵士宏，并才术优长，临事精敏，臣今保举各堪充皗擢繁难任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160228_comment'></div>如所举不如状，甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160228_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160228_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　举张宗益。作品：《举张宗益》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三九。）</span><div id='poem_1160223' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160223' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160223?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举张宗益劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1160223_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160223'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160223'>臣切见湖北转运判官、都官员外郎张宗益学识精深，议论宏博，莅官为政，所至有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160223_comment'></div>臣今保举堪充台阁清近之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160223_comment'></div>所举不如状，臣甘谬妄之坐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　举杨遂。作品：《举杨遂》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160226'>臣切见绛州团练使杨遂出于行阵，累有战功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160226_comment'></div>历军厢主，落权泾原州总管及沿边都巡检使，颇有绩效，兼年齿方壮，臣今保举堪充管军及边上重难任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160226_comment'></div>如蒙朝廷擢用后不如所举，臣甘连坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160226_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160226_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　举赵士宏。作品：《举赵士宏》<span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160224'>臣切见驾部员外郎、知永州赵士宏识虑详明，敏于从政，试以繁剧，必能干济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160224_comment'></div>臣今保举堪充皗陟繁难任使。<div class='inline' -----title
郑州

class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，50岁</div><div id='f268447fc9a64fe195d3e7a7562c8957' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　途经郑州，丢失银杯，曾公亮智破案，彦博以为神明。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d1564b0adb8244e491d0ba958e71f29a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d1564b0adb8244e491d0ba958e71f29a");'><span id='d1564b0adb8244e491d0ba958e71f29a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，50岁</div><div id='d1564b0adb8244e491d0ba958e71f29a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　为高若讷作神道碑。作品：《观文殿学士尚书左丞谥文庄高公神道碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一二。）</span><div id='poem_1160326' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160326' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160326?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观文殿学士尚书左丞谥文庄高公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160326")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160326_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160326'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160326'>昔者两汉之盛也，辅相以清静宁民，公卿以经术决事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160326_comment'></div>故文、景、显、肃之际，为贤主、为治世，炳焉几与三代比隆，盖公辅得人之效欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160326_comment'></div>若夫本经术以熙治，载清净以镇浮，翊我昌运，高迈于三五，泽斯生民，永济于富寿，而赋命不融，赍志莫究，愚于北海高公殄瘁之叹深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160326_comment'></div>公讳若讷，字敏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160326_comment'></div>其始齐之公族，于春秋时甚显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160326_comment'></div>逮汉而后，名德轩冕，赫奕相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160326_comment'></div>从仕屡迁，今为太原榆次人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160326_comment'></div>曾祖讳某，赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160326_comment'></div>王父讳某，仕崇仪使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160326_comment'></div>考讳某，仕右侍禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160326_comment'></div>并赠太师、中书令兼尚书令，考封祁国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160326_comment'></div>曾妣王夫人，祖妣马夫人，妣阎夫人，封魏、晋、秦三大国，悉用公贵而追锡命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160326_comment'></div>太师藏器弗辉，天爵自高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160326_comment'></div>二令君虽起家登仕，而位不充量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160326_comment'></div>济美载德，贻谋积庆，必复其始，至公嗣兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160326_comment'></div>公蚤有奇节，挺然不群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160326_comment'></div>祁公之捐馆，公始十岁，奉母夫人寓汲郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160326_comment'></div>在陋安贫，嗜学乐道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160326_comment'></div>天圣初，举进士，中甲科，调彰德军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160326_comment'></div>秩满，改著作佐郎，迁秘书丞、太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160326_comment'></div>三治剧邑，所居不尚赫赫之誉，去后人皆思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160326_comment'></div>台举御史，改监察，迁主客员外郎，殿中里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160326_comment'></div>未几，除右司谏、直史馆，赐服五品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160326_comment'></div>迁起居舍人、知谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160326_comment'></div>改刑部员外郎，兼侍御史知杂事，赐三品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160326_comment'></div>公迭居谏宪，当职论事，不烦细激讦，以要虚名，务举大体，中时之急病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160326_comment'></div>若犍为土豪，缘戚里为郎，得大郡，公谓玷郎选，轻郡寄，亟论罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160326_comment'></div>内侍长居中任事，恃恩而肆，公率同列极言而斥出之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160326_comment'></div>复言：「今执政，古三公之任，所谓坐而论道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160326_comment'></div>今进对立侍，裁移刻而罢，于咨诹体貌之礼，固有未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160326_comment'></div>宜复坐论，以通上下之情，以究都俞之美」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160326_comment'></div>上以为识治体而深器之，于是益有大用之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160326_comment'></div>除天章阁待制、知永兴军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160326_comment'></div>诏复留弗遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160326_comment'></div>麟府宿兵，高选外计，乃迁礼部郎中、河东路都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160326_comment'></div>上思公学术优深，议论精敏，亟召还，兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160326_comment'></div>丁秦国忧，累诏夺情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160326_comment'></div>沥恳哀诉，祈终三年丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160326_comment'></div>国朝故事，官待制以上遭丧，类卒哭起复，今许终服，自公始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160326_comment'></div>服除，还旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160326_comment'></div>寻改龙图阁直学士、史馆修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160326_comment'></div>迁吏部郎中，除谏议大夫，权御史中丞、理检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160326_comment'></div>上悯雨旰食，因公奏事，问雨旸所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1160326_comment'></div>乃推本《洪范》五事，稽合时政及救旱之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1160326_comment'></div>上大感悟，益嘉公之博洽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1160326_comment'></div>数日，擢拜枢密副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1160326_comment'></div>居二岁，以工部侍郎参知政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1160326_comment'></div>又二年，由户部侍郎、检校太傅为枢密使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1160326_comment'></div>公践历二府，始终七年，循守法度，奉行故事，简静慎重，不轻改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1160326_comment'></div>常曰：「蒿目而忧世者，非致治之心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1160326_comment'></div>每被顾问，必傅经以对，条理明畅，极尽治乱之原，上未尝不前席以欣纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1160326_comment'></div>故愚谓本经术以熙治，载清静以镇浮，有两汉贤公卿之风，为得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1160326_comment'></div>其在政府也，凡侥倖干泽、事从中出者，请格而不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1160326_comment'></div>后妃之族，当避权保恩，请不预执政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1160326_comment'></div>悉降诏为永法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1160326_comment'></div>在枢府时，属盗发甘陵，婴城负固，王师攻围，逾月未克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1160326_comment'></div>时议欲开其自新之路，许以容贷，且使凶党离解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1160326_comment'></div>公谓贝于河朔，兵屯素盛，今不穷讨，后启乱阶，威灵不振，将为夷狄轻笑，当济师易将，必行天诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1160326_comment'></div>蛮寇邕管，岭外骚然，承平岁久，武备阙习，荆广之甲，若驱市人，故屡战屡败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1160326_comment'></div>公议遣大帅总北兵及陇西之劲马以往，则计日可平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1160326_comment'></div>或谓北兵不习南风，贼必守险以老王师，虽多马，恐不足施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1160326_comment'></div>公曰：「贼狃数胜，理必迎战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1160326_comment'></div>以我训士精骑，出其不意而夹攻之，蠢尔虽众，胡能为哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1160326_comment'></div>二寇既平，悉如公算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1160326_comment'></div>又患兵冗而费浮，议罢召募，并汰疲老，要在节用彊本，人给家足，为太平长久之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1160326_comment'></div>性冲澹，不喜夸耀，累奏章祈解枢柄，辞情切至，确不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1160326_comment'></div>上重违其志，久之，乃除尚书左丞、观文殿学士、同群牧制置使，不许外出，且兼进读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1160326_comment'></div>盖将用其所长，以须爰立乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1160326_comment'></div>公既释重务，遂所愿，自退朝，即杜门燕居，观书为乐，搢绅高其静退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1160326_comment'></div>以至和二年八月二十九日遘疾，薨于宣阳里之第，享年五十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1160326_comment'></div>上闻讣震悼，趣辇临奠，既伤名臣之不憖，又视其居处俭陋，叹其清节者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1160326_comment'></div>赙赗加等，废翌日视朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1160326_comment'></div>赠尚书右仆射，太常谥曰文庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1160326_comment'></div>以是年冬十月己酉葬于开封府开封县褒亲乡之原，从祁公之兆，礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1160326_comment'></div>初，公寓汲时，秦国有疾，公左右奉养，药剂必亲，遂精意于医书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1160326_comment'></div>且曰：「是术也，前世名儒巨公能者多矣，况人子奉亲，可不知耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1160326_comment'></div>因研究，得其妙，以是秦国终享寿康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1160326_comment'></div>及公感疾之始，自诊其脉，曰：「吾殆不起」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1160326_comment'></div>诸子泣，请召国医高手者，公坚曰止，虽和缓，不可为已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1160326_comment'></div>又戒其子毋辄奏，以贻上忧，吾死，殆不得有所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1160326_comment'></div>及东首，神爽不乱，恬然以逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1160326_comment'></div>非达生知命、安时处顺之有素，其能若是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1160326_comment'></div>公既葬，上追思之深，亲迂宸笔，以表其隧，曰「儒贤之碑」，有以见君臣始终之义厚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1160326_comment'></div>公以誉望，凡朝之华选剧任必与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1160326_comment'></div>同知礼部贡举者再，取士得人，近特为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1160326_comment'></div>又为京西路安抚使，入契丹国信使，领吏部流内铨、三班院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1160326_comment'></div>间被诏定黍尺以协乐律之正，制兵契以严军师之兴，裁损祠祭服器，复古之法，今悉用之，朝议推其精密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1160326_comment'></div>愚与公布衣时为友，自登宪署，司外计，居政府为僚，故知公尤深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1160326_comment'></div>公性资方介，中立无党，惟道是信，不以世俗毁誉为得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1160326_comment'></div>所学非茍记问而已，必穷其理，适于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1160326_comment'></div>每谈历代治乱之迹，贯穿明白，如视诸掌，听者释然，更仆忘倦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1160326_comment'></div>文集二十卷，尤学之粹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1160326_comment'></div>娶王氏，封寿安郡夫人，夙有贤范，闻于族姻，后公一年而殁，以明年正月五日祔公之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1160326_comment'></div>嗣子彦辅，内殿崇班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1160326_comment'></div>次保衡、安石、吉甫，光禄寺丞，元规，大理评事，皆脩谨笃学，能世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1160326_comment'></div>长女适游奎，次适祠部郎中、秘阁校理林亿，次适太常博士张谊，次适王宗诰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1160326_comment'></div>彦辅及诸弟泣叙先烈，见托论撰，将附于《儒贤》之下，以永其传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1160326_comment'></div>愚自视拙鄙，而义不可辞，姑用直书，传信无愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1160326_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_98_1160326'>维高氏先，盖姜姓后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1160326_comment'></div>表海以还，历祀寖久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1160326_comment'></div>爵德世济，忠贤代有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1160326_comment'></div>发源汤汤，其流固长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1160326_comment'></div>储因积粹，挺生文庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1160326_comment'></div>文庄岳岳，照邻先觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1160326_comment'></div>大器长才，奇文奥学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1160326_comment'></div>公初逢时，奋自布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1160326_comment'></div>绝尘遐鹜，垂天迅飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1160326_comment'></div>白简触邪，凛然霜威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1160326_comment'></div>皂囊纳忠，弥缝阙遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1160326_comment'></div>曰党曰附，吾所弗与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1160326_comment'></div>不激不讦，罔干虚誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1160326_comment'></div>人不我知，吾不为沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1160326_comment'></div>信道而往，若省于度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1160326_comment'></div>进直内阁，联侍迩英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1160326_comment'></div>左右献纳，据古援经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1160326_comment'></div>帝御宣室，雨旸是恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1160326_comment'></div>公陈五行，沃心造膝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1160326_comment'></div>乃预大政，乃总中枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1160326_comment'></div>嘉猷辰告，基命吁谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1160326_comment'></div>事必师古，袭于常故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1160326_comment'></div>毋作聪明，毋越彝矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1160326_comment'></div>付之至当，百职咸举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1160326_comment'></div>挠法挠赏，凭宠怙权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1160326_comment'></div>绳之以正，金石其坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1160326_comment'></div>歼蛮于邕，殄寇于贝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1160326_comment'></div>多算隃度，审于蓍蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1160326_comment'></div>我思至言，名遂身退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1160326_comment'></div>斯言足践，其志克从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1160326_comment'></div>毋处于外，惟帝念功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1160326_comment'></div>论思殿内，劝讲禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1160326_comment'></div>师宾之地，礼厚恩隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1160326_comment'></div>显允君子，宜锡难老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1160326_comment'></div>方胡不然，曾未华皓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1160326_comment'></div>轸于天衷，抚几震悼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1160326_comment'></div>帝曰儒贤，表其新阡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1160326_comment'></div>宠以宸翰，冠于碑颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1160326_comment'></div>崇封维屹，扶树维郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1160326_comment'></div>令仪则閟，遗芳永苾。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_137_1160326'></div><div id='poem_sentence_137_1160326_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
登封
-----detail

class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494909'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494909'>鹤发庞眉二老仙，林间老屋十馀间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494909'>斋粮不蓄惟栽菊，道眼长明祇看山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494909'>朋侣过从应绮用，比邻掩映是嵩辕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494909'>暂游自愧尘劳迹，解帢临溪濯腻颜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494909_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494909'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494909_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年4月1日</a>　游少林寺。作品：《宿少林寺诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_494908' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494908' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494908?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿少林寺<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494908")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494908_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494908_0'>① 清乾隆《河南府志》卷一○一引此诗题下注：一作楼异</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494908'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494908'>六六仙峰绕静居，俗尘至此暂消除。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494908'>西来未悟禅师意，北去还驰使者车<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予方被命移守北都。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494908'>五品封槐今尚在，九年面壁昔何如。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494908'>心知一宿犹难觉，花藏重寻贝叶书。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494908_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494908'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494908_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年3月</a>　游岳寺。作品：《游岳寺》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_494910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游岳寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494910")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494910'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494910'>寺占嵩颜景最多，奇峰列刹共嵬<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作嵯）</span>峨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494910'>依岩宝砌砻清础，出谷飞泉逗素波。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494910'>下瞰长川穷渺邈，傍观列岫极陂陁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494910'>缁林法乐堪随喜，钟磬声清呗梵和。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494910_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494910'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494910_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

大名

id='poem_title_1160215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举李师锡劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年五月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160215")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160215'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160215'>臣切见河阳通判李师锡才资朴茂，处事干勤，前为陜西转运判官，深晓盐马之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160215_comment'></div>切闻以议论寡合，皏以慢公，非时差替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160215_comment'></div>近又以前任按察之误，与转运使一例降官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160215_comment'></div>原情颇轻，降夺差重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160215_comment'></div>伏望圣慈体察，早赐牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160215_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年6月</a>　言处置怀、卫州民聚为盗事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年7月25日</a>　岁灾，乞免人户折变蚕盐钱，只纳见钱。作品：《乞免人户折变蚕盐钱》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免人户折变蚕盐钱奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年7月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160002")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160002'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160002'>臣检会近准大名府牒，为人户今岁大段灾伤困乏，其羜盐钱只乞特许并免折变，合纳见钱，候向去丰熟，却令依旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160002_comment'></div>已于六月二十九日具劄子申奏去讫，至此未奉朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160002_comment'></div>今又据怀、卫州状申：逐县人户，各为灾伤，乞将羜盐钱送纳本色见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160002_comment'></div>州司勘会今年夏税已系全放，今体量得人户委是累年并值灾伤，贫困不易，所有蚕盐钱伏乞详酌指挥者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160002_comment'></div>臣勘会上件，逐州府人户委实大段灾伤，必是难以了纳，切虑别致逃移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160002_comment'></div>欲望朝廷检详臣前奏及今来怀、卫州所申事理，早赐指挥，许将人户今年羜盐钱并免折变，只令送纳见钱，候向去丰熟，却令依旧折变，所贵灾伤贫民易为了纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160002_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1160002_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　乞罢河北预雇车牛。作品：《乞罢河北预雇车牛》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢河北预雇车牛奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160001")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160001'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160001'>臣勘会本道所管八州内，怀、卫属河北西路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160001_comment'></div>近累准西路转运司牒：准朝旨，逐将下合用太平车一百六十乘并牛畜，于逐将所领军马住营州军，预令民间结保承认，遇兵行日，量支顾钱，随军前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160001_comment'></div>民间闻之，将为官军不测，便有举动，颇亦惊扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160001_comment'></div>况河北人户例有车牛，乃是民间日用之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160001_comment'></div>兼逐将所须车牛，其数不多，缓急或顾或差，旦暮可集，不误军期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160001_comment'></div>乞更不须预令民间结保承认，免致先有烦扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160001_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160001_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1160001'>澶、魏、博州三将合用车牛，东路转运司并不曾行下逐州，必是别有擘画，亦恐民间烦扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160001_comment'></div>若遇兵行，于民间顾倩车牛，人情必不敢避免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160001_comment'></div>即未明所出车牛之家，至时更合备人力随行否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160001_comment'></div>此一事人情所惮，如不用逐家人力随行，亦乞明降指挥。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　请严谕雄州、霸州、广信军、安肃军注意刺探辽人军情。作品：《乞严诫河北安抚司探报事宜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160004' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160004' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160004?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞严诫河北安抚司探报事宜奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160004")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160004_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160004'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160004'>臣近累据雄、霸州、广信、安肃军关申到体探事宜，并皆循常闲慢事节，兼久应验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160004_comment'></div>今来北界既频有生事，不比常时，乞朝廷严谕前项四州及沿边安抚司，精选勾当事人，比旧日优与钱物，入深体探。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160004_comment'></div>务要的当事宜，不误边防准备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160004_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1160004'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160004_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　请火山知军体探西夏、辽遣使相过情状。作品：《乞体探西北遣使相过事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞体探西北遣使相过事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160003")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160003'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160003'>臣见诸处关报探到事宜，西人北虏遣使相过稍频，深虑癚谋诡计，以利相诱，牵制边兵，乞令河东经略司、麟府军马司专委火山知军于下寨子常切体察西北遣人相过情状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160003_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160003_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1160003'>下寨子属火山军，在西北两界之中，内殿崇班燕复是火山军人，有心力，见在麟府守官，可委之同察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1160003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>　沮李稷，以其陵慢魏公。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　请即修北京（即大名府）楼橹。作品：《论修楼橹事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160005' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160005' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160005?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论修楼橹事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160005")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160005_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160005'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160005'>河北平壤，其城池楼橹之设，尤严于它道，凡遣使行边，所以督责于守臣、按察之吏者必先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160005_comment'></div>夫岂以有事整完，无事则废弛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160005_comment'></div>比者命安抚使以修完属郡之城壁，周相其摧坏褊狭，将易而新之，使士民有以容，兵械有以施，诚善矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160005_comment'></div>茍虑事计材，趣会期于岁月之顷无不完者，此固足以代守国之险，而严御戒之备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160005_comment'></div>命方行，而反令依瘾制度，造作熟材，堆积盖藏于官舍之中，以俟楼橹之大坏而易之，未见其利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160005_comment'></div>北京楼橹之当修者九百馀所，凡八千馀间，若欲概修于数月之间，虽尽鸠天下之良工，亦不可卒焉而就，必在次第而修作之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160005_comment'></div>旧材之中，尚有可用者，亦兼取焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160005_comment'></div>然犹要之一二年，仅可完矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160005_comment'></div>今乃以成熟之材，委积于虚间之处，敌来而后立，患至而后兴，无乃不及于事乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160005_comment'></div>今若据楼橹见在区数，内有庳下不及制度并欹侧朽弊者，计其数，且修其半，仍间隔一座，折一座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160005_comment'></div>所贵城上不至计然空缺，年岁之间，便得周遍完备。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1160005'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160005_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年2月</a>　李师中许以中春来访。作品：《诗答郓州分司李待制许中春宠访师中》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494996' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160006' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160006' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160006?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答神宗咨访诏奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁九年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160006")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160006_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160006'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160006'>臣伏奉诏书，询及疆事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160006_comment'></div>臣以衰拙昏贷，何足仰承圣问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160006_comment'></div>然以久当柄任，蒙国恩深，义激于中，敢不罄露，庶伸补报之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160006_comment'></div>夫戎狄之情，贪利忘义，从古以来，载于书史者详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160006_comment'></div>自真宗朝与通好，所以息民几八十年，未尝犯顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160006_comment'></div>惟庆历初，乘我西事未弭，故有邀求，饵之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160006_comment'></div>当时载立誓书，亦古寻盟之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160006_comment'></div>历观前代中国与夷狄通好，未有如今之悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160006_comment'></div>盖朝廷谨守信誓，至虽琐琐细故，亦不创生变改，是以戎人亦不敢轻有希求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160006_comment'></div>自数年前，累来望理白沟馆地，及要拆去铺屋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160006_comment'></div>况誓书之中，明载雄州所管白沟，两朝遵守已久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160006_comment'></div>且信誓之词，质于天地神癨，告于宗庙社稷，此而可渝，何以享国？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160006_comment'></div>今萧禧重来，又决于雄州北亭交割礼物，其意欲以雄州北亭为界，其如誓书何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160006_comment'></div>誓书若不为凭，即代北之地，止以图籍照验，宜其不以为据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160006_comment'></div>原其贪心，亦因庆历初西事未平之际，求黄嵬之地，朝廷容易弃与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160006_comment'></div>又至今日，妄有侵理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160006_comment'></div>诚如圣诏所谓「虏情无厌，势恐未已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160006_comment'></div>臣亦谓虏因此妄起衅端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160006_comment'></div>圣意谓：「万一不测，何以待之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160006_comment'></div>臣以谓，中国御戎，守信为上，必以誓书为證，彼将何词以亢，纵骋诡词，难夺正论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160006_comment'></div>臣又以事理度之，事固有逆顺，理固有曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160006_comment'></div>顺而直，天必助之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1160006_comment'></div>逆而曲，人不与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1160006_comment'></div>若虏人不计曲直利害，肆其贪狠犯顺之心，朝廷固已严于预备之要，足食足兵，坚固城壁，保全民人，以战则胜，以守则固，止此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1160006_comment'></div>臣又闻用兵之道，兵应者胜，不得已而用之，此所以天必助之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1160006_comment'></div>大抵中国之兵，利在为主，以主待客，以逸待劳，理必胜矣，亦应兵之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1160006_comment'></div>臣伏详诏书曰：「思所以待遇之要，御备之方」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1160006_comment'></div>切料圣意慎于举动，尚虑发言盈庭，容有异论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1160006_comment'></div>或曰先发制人，意在轻动；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1160006_comment'></div>或曰乘其未备，袭取燕蓟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1160006_comment'></div>事不审处，恐将噬脐，非王师万全之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1160006_comment'></div>伏愿陛下垂意熟察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1160006_comment'></div>今朝廷分置将官，整齐器械，固得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1160006_comment'></div>然将校偏裨，更须慎择其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1160006_comment'></div>又河朔频岁饥荒，粮饷用度窘乏，尤索计置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1160006_comment'></div>若兵连未解，物力殚屈，即误国大事<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1160006_comment'></div>切要先事而辨，乃无后艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1160006_comment'></div>至于不急烦费，事须裁节，在臣本道者，亦当续次奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1160006_comment'></div>臣识浅才薄，思虑不周，伏望圣慈稍垂省览，宽其罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1160006_comment'></div>臣无任惶恐之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1160006_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1160006'>臣虑萧禧之来，亦议及白沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1160006_comment'></div>况白沟载于誓书明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1160006_comment'></div>河朔城壁，非要害之处，亦当且后之，所贵专力于合修之处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1160006_comment'></div>臣顿首上奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1160006_comment'></div>河北近西山州军，城壁未须添展，枉劳民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1160006_comment'></div>盖万一有事，军民皆出山寨，不肯入城，盖山寨之中，易得薪水，出入自便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1160006_comment'></div>当时沮臣议者，谓今之西山林木伐尽，无险可恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1160006_comment'></div>本以山为险，非在林木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1160006_comment'></div>况珀谷之间，戎马必能散掠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1160006_comment'></div>景德间山寨之名，至今颇有存者，可以检问。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1160006_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1160006'><span class='label'>按：</span>原奏前有《神宗咨访诏》，诏后云：「臣于今月十日准入内供奉官裴昱至，赐臣实封手诏一道，询及疆事，令臣密具以闻。臣今具手诸一道进呈。」<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_35_1160006_0'>⑴ 金汤非粟而不守，守尚不可，况用兵出师而粮饷不给，何以取济。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1160006_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年4月</a>　乞追夺修范济口被赏官吏之赐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　编《药准》作品：《药准序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_1160305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>药准序<span class='inlineComment2'>（此下二序，熙宁八年北都作。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160305")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160305'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160305'>余曾苦头眩，治之多方，弥岁不解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160305_comment'></div>会国医龚世昌诊脉，问状，乃云：「鬲有寒痰，久之使然，非他苦也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160305_comment'></div>授余香芎散并其方，服未半剂而愈，遂不复发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160305_comment'></div>余既神其效，又观其立方有法，不与常类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160305_comment'></div>方用九物，物别为之解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160305_comment'></div>凡药性之温寒，味之甘辛，并其主疗，略具于左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160305_comment'></div>虽简而备，使观之者有据，服之者无疑，无疑即有效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160305_comment'></div>犹夫任人，各知其才之所长，用之无疑，事罔不济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160305_comment'></div>乃知古之良医治病，必考于本草而立方，方药既精，厥疾必瘳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160305_comment'></div>班固云：「经方者，本草石之寒温，原疾病之深浅」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160305_comment'></div>陶隐居云：「道经载扁鹊数法，其用药犹是本草家意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160305_comment'></div>张仲景最为众方之祖，悉依本草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160305_comment'></div>近世庸医鲜通本草，求其方药之验，固亦难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160305_comment'></div>余嘉龚医之方专用本草之意，因采仲景并《外台》、《千金》及诸家经验方共若干，辄加注，传于门内，以备处疗，谓之《药准》，以其依本草立方，则用之有准云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1160305_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　编《节要〈本草〉图》作品：《节要本草图序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷一一。）</span><div id='poem_1160306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>节要本草图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160306")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160306'>余尝以近世医工，虽处方有据，而用药不精，以至疗疾寡效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160306_comment'></div>盖古医用药，率多自采，故桐君著《采药录》，备其花叶形色，别其是非真假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160306_comment'></div>用之决无乖误，服之咸得痊愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160306_comment'></div>而又择郡国地产之良，及春秋秀实之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160306_comment'></div>今则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160306_comment'></div>药肆不能尽识，但凭采送之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160306_comment'></div>医工鲜通本草，莫辨良苦之杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160306_comment'></div>加之膺伪，遂以合和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160306_comment'></div>以兹疗治，宜其寡效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160306_comment'></div>唐室之盛，置《药园生本草图》，欲悉知其形色、气味，用药之精且慎如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160306_comment'></div>嘉祐初，余在政府，建言重定《本草图经》，凡数年而成，例蒙赐本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160306_comment'></div>然药品繁夥，尽形绘事，卷帙颇多，披阅匪易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160306_comment'></div>因录其常用要切者若干种，别为图策，以便披检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160306_comment'></div>简则易辨，人得有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160306_comment'></div>按图而验，辨误识真，用之于医，所益多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160306_comment'></div>潞国公宽夫记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1160306_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　诗赠窦舜卿，表达欲谢职归闲之意。作品：《诗赠提举窦侍郎舜卿》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诗赠提举窦侍郎<span class='inlineComment2'>（舜卿）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494988")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494988'>紫髯真将白云卿，总领琳宫道气清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494988'>蕲竹一林曾断买，青溪三弄得遗声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494988'>季伦自作思归曲，向秀方深感旧情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494988'>虽恨功名非谢傅，樽前更欲听君筝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　赠家园所酿酴醾与刘航。刘航各咏酴醾诗，文彦博有和诗。作品：《家园酴醾自京寄至奉送提举刘司封》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>家园酴醾自京寄至奉送提举刘司封</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494982")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494982'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494982'>小圃酴醾烂熳开，盈箱采得寄铜台。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494982'>当花对酒熏然意，似到清香洞里来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494982_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494982'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_494982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　为诗赠刘航。作品：《偶成小诗赠提举刘司封》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶成小诗赠提举刘司封</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494981")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494981'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494981'>向上应无快活人，斯言未敢便当仁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494981'>留君且住非他意，好作熙宁第八春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494981'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_494981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年</a>　请刘航来府园避暑，有诗纪之。作品：《招仲通司封府园避暑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招仲通司封府园避暑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494985")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494985'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494985'>骑山楼下水轩东，一室初开待白公<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494985'>虽是不如南涧上，都缘却有北窗风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494985'>衔杯避暑称河朔，飞盖延宾在邺中。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：白云，奇章欲于南溪上别葺一室，与白傅止宿，故诗云终恐不如南涧上，别开室待闲人。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494985_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_1160307_comment'></div>顷年尝游公藩，误蒙与进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160307_comment'></div>一日，延食于春明东阁，示予兰陵萧诚书，且曰：「名笔也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160307_comment'></div>乃知公之行笔类萧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160307_comment'></div>今观此小楷二轴，精劲有法，远出前辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160307_comment'></div>追惟东阁眷与之厚，不觉泫然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160307_comment'></div>熙宁九年六月二十四日，北都善养堂题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1160307_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　诏再判大名府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　谢陈知俭借新舟。作品：《谢假新舟》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢假新舟<span class='inlineComment2'>（赠运使陈金部知俭）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_494997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494997'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494997'>使舰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>新成泛碧澜，更陪李郭共登仙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494997'>深惭一<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>水如衣带，不称君家旧济川。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 原作槛，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_494997_0'>⑵ 自注：同计运李龙图、学省郭郎中共载。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_494997_0'>⑶ 原缺，据四库本补</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_494997_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年10月</a>　彦博生日，陈知俭惠绣寿仙香炉合。有诗为谢。作品：《谢运使陈金部生日惠绣寿仙香炉合依韵和二绝句》<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495009'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495009'>絺绣为章古法传，刺文肖象用功专。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495009'>他时携去伊川坞，欲并西方皤叟仙<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　言范子渊浚川杷无益于河事。作品：《不保明浚河3》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　奏开旧沙河入御河，以通江、淮之运事有害无利。作品：《言运河》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二三。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年11月28日</a>　于府署安正堂赏雪，有诗记之。作品：《熙宁丙辰十一月二十八日安正堂喜雪》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494994' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494994' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494994?labeling=true' target='_blank'>熙宁丙辰十一月二十八日安正堂喜雪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年11月28日）</span><span class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494994_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494994'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494994'>冻云浓厚朔风严，粉揉琼霙扑绮檐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494994_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494994'>斗变至和缘帝力，迎知上瑞协人占。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494994_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494994'>晚归渔市蓑衣重，晓上旗亭酒价添。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494994_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_494994'>更待三英同胜赏，翩翩赋笔紫毫铦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_494994_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_494994'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494994_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1076&endYear=1076')">1076年</a>　雪霁，登金宿楼赏雪，有诗记之。作品：《雪霁金宿楼闲望偶作》<span target='_blank'>雪霁金宿楼閒望偶作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1076年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", id='poem_sentence_0_494995'>盈尺初晴皓采鲜，长空极望势漫漫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494995_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494995'>铜台不惮三休上，冰井须添一倍寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494995_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_494995'>舟楫似从云外过，园林如在鉴中看。<div id='poem_sentence_2_494995_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
