id='poem_sentence_4_494995_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年5月</a>　范子渊言熊本、陈佑甫附会结托彦博。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　黄河水势甚急猛，彦博请固护堤防。作品：《奏黄河水势》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1160012' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160012' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏黄河水势</a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160012")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160012'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160012'>臣本司于七月九日据卫州申，管勾运河于良弼申，今月四日，沙河水涨，沫过上东水偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160012_comment'></div>寻下闸板栏截不住，沫过闸板，透入运河行流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160012_comment'></div>本司为今六月七日大名府御河连并添涨，日夕救护，仅免决溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160012_comment'></div>寻牒卫州火急闭塞闸口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160012_comment'></div>据卫州申，寻捲扫于上东水口闭塞了当，有些小津漏，见诸填次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160012_comment'></div>本司为穿府城水，大关梁下不通舟船，切虑运河闸口依前固护不定，透黄河水入御河，即为害不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160012_comment'></div>已奏乞指挥都水监速差官就运河闸口固护。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160012_comment'></div>今月十九日却据澶州申，据临河县申，十七日午时诣遥堤上巡睹，见水自西南来，波浪紧急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160012_comment'></div>问得人民，言说卫州樊店西黄河口决，一概水东北行流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160012_comment'></div>十六日夜二更以来到本县，冲注二十馀疃人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160012_comment'></div>观此水势及民间所说，为害不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160012_comment'></div>县司已逐急于沿河差船，令佐亲监辖救渡人命去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160012_comment'></div>又据卫州黎阳县申，今月十五日，御河水浑浓涨猛，水色与别日不同，认是黄河涨溢沫岸，通流入御河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160012_comment'></div>至三更，御河水一沫出两岸，见今此来相及南门，本县令、佐、都监即时救应盽口城门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160012_comment'></div>至十六日，南门、西门盽口节次破决，水头一并向城流注，遮塞不定，遂紧切一向固护城壁官物者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160012_comment'></div>本司即时火急再行文字，转指挥府城以上县镇官吏，严切固护盽防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1160012_comment'></div>如水势大，必不可防遏，即令本地分官吏究心详审，计较利害，相度踏行有自来分减水势旧河道处，即便火急开决，分减水势，无致奔冲，直向府城为害去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1160012_comment'></div>伏乞更赐指挥都水监，选委公心知河事官赴卫州，相度调集人兵物料固护盽防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1160012_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1160012_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1160012'>今据卫州十四日状申，水势沫过埽背，于运河上约，后行流，救护不定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1160012_comment'></div>及称河势危急处，系运河上约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1160012_comment'></div>卫州属河北西路，仍乞下西路转运司疾速应副人兵物料。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1160012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年7月</a>　言黄河澶州决溢原因。作品：《奏黄河曹村决溢利害乞择水官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1160014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160014?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏黄河曹村决溢利害乞择水官<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160014")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160014'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160014'>臣于今年正月六日奏，为据德州申，大河自去年秋夏至今冬，河底淤淀，通流不决，河势变移，不循故道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160014_comment'></div>见今四散漫流，两岸俱被水患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160014_comment'></div>臣详黄河下流淤淀，疏浚不行，泄水不快，即上流水势须至壅遏，若不预行经制，切虑将来河水泛涨，必于魏、博、恩、澶等州决溢为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160014_comment'></div>自后不闻水监别有擘画，只是固护东流北岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160014_comment'></div>今年五六七月间，大名金新堤一带诸埽非常危急，果致澶州决溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160014_comment'></div>臣又检会今年正月八日奏，为近年以来，河防官吏以减省物料，指望酬赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160014_comment'></div>只缘三四年来，黄河非常水小，埽岸偶无危急，是致减得物料，即非久远常制，必恐埽岸渐次有失添修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160014_comment'></div>若将来河水泛涨如旧，必致疏虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160014_comment'></div>伏乞检会旧条，不以减省物料，指望酬奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160014_comment'></div>今年夏秋水涨，诸埽危急，多称物料少数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160014_comment'></div>亦闻今来曹村埽决溢，自熙宁八年、九年、十年检计春料，合行接贴低怯之处，三年之中，并不曾应付接贴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160014_comment'></div>兼本埽兵士，多在别处占使，或驾舡装般水利司小麦外，见在只有兵士十七人实役，致今来以堤身低小怯薄，遂至决溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160014_comment'></div>臣前来因论列河事，并及水官乞行慎怿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1160014_comment'></div>今河朔、京东州县人民被水患者莫知其数，嗷嗷吁天，上轸圣念，而水官不能自讼，犹汲汲以希赏，于理安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1160014_comment'></div>臣前后所陈，出于至诚，本图补报，非敢激讦，轻有干冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1160014_comment'></div>伏望圣慈垂察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1160014_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　言开运河之患。作品：《再奏运河利害》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二三。）</span><div id='poem_1160013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再奏运河利害<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160013")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160013_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160013'>臣于去年冬奏：卫州王供埽下开堤，取黄河水作运河，置闸引水入御河，深为不便，以为大则决溢，小则淤淀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160013_comment'></div>寻闻差官定夺利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160013_comment'></div>今来果致黄河水入运河，防遏不住，沫过闸口，冲注下流州府县镇，为患甚大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160013_comment'></div>切虑定夺所未知得今来运河之害，乞指挥定夺所下卫州及大名路安抚司，取索自七月四日及十四日后来申报决溢一宗文字看详定夺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年8月6日</a>　请浚河案所涉人吏就地取勘，不赴京。作品：《奏定夺所勾人吏事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二四。）</span><div id='poem_1160015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏定夺所勾人吏事<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁十年八月六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1077年8月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160015")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160015'>臣本司准定夺取勘所牒，勾追安抚司全司人吏八人，留守司河盽一案人吏十人赴京照对浚河公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160015_comment'></div>伏为今来本路州府非常大雨，及黄、御河决溢，并德、棣、博等州贼盗常多，晓夕行遣文字救护水灾，修完城壁盽防，催促捕捉盗贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160015_comment'></div>凡百公事，比之常时数十倍多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160015_comment'></div>加以所行文移急于星火，今若尽勾却上件全司人吏，则所掌文案首尾并无人检会，承禀行遣必致违误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160015_comment'></div>本已具奏，乞将上件人吏如的合有何罪，即乞依条收坐，就邻近州差官取勘，敢不承伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160015_comment'></div>兼昨来保明熙宁八年浚川退出地土事，臣为见九年河水依旧复来，蒌浸却八年退出地土，人户并诉水灾，照会得事理子细分明，是以不敢雷同保明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160015_comment'></div>况事皆由臣，不由人吏，如显有不当，只今独坐臣罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160015_comment'></div>伏望圣慈详察，特赐指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160015_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160015_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1160015'>臣伏详元差官定夺疏浚黄河及开运河，如有理曲之人，便行取勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160015_comment'></div>今来定夺所勾追人吏不少，切恐定为理曲之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1160015_comment'></div>伏望圣慈将所定理曲之状付臣，容臣一一子细开析闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1160015_comment'></div>所贵不误朝廷赏罚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1160015_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1077&endYear=1077')">1077年</a>　大水后，黄莘贻书问念。作品：《运判秘丞黄以某自大水后，久无燕集声酒之乐，贻书问念……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_495008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_495008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/495008?labeling=true' -----title
孟州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7438bf8a733c4f3ca15acc87cb2d56c6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7438bf8a733c4f3ca15acc87cb2d56c6");'><span id='7438bf8a733c4f3ca15acc87cb2d56c6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>，68岁</div><div id='7438bf8a733c4f3ca15acc87cb2d56c6' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴河阳（今河南孟州）陛辞日面奏。作品：《赴河阳陛辞日面奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1159997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1159997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1159997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赴河阳陛辞日面奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1159997")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1159997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1159997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1159997'>陛下忧勤庶政，切于致治，乃尧舜用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1159997_comment'></div>更愿陛下广开言路，兼采博纳，使下情上达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1159997_comment'></div>收揽权纲，无使权臣卖弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1159997_comment'></div>爵人于朝，须协公议，与众共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1159997_comment'></div>任官令久于其任，候所职成败明著，而后赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1159997_comment'></div>用人当兼取群才，同济时务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1159997_comment'></div>若专任一才，即朋党胶固者希时而并进，孤忠自立者望风而銂退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1159997_comment'></div>更望法天地简易之道，守祖宗盈成之业，使上下安静，则不治而自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1159997_comment'></div>近时新进纤佞之人，多是妄有更张兴作，以为进身之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1159997_comment'></div>陛下今不采纳臣愚忠，异时必当自验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1159997_comment'></div>臣惟望圣明早悟，即天下之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1159997_comment'></div>臣今朝辞赴任，方瞻恋轩陛，更无劄子进呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1159997_comment'></div>伏恐有本任指挥事，乞赐圣旨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1159997'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1159997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1159997'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_12_1159997_0'>⑴ 《文潞公文集》卷二二。又见《历代名臣奏议》卷三九。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1159997_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>李柬之惠诗五首叙旧招隐，有诗记之。作品：《去春蒙西都致政李少师柬之惠诗五首，追叙旧游因而招隐。某尚羁枢务，请退未谐，深味来章，未知所答。迁延宿留，遂涉岁时。今蒙圣慈俯从人欲，听解重柄，均逸便藩，仰西河之上游，瞻仁宅之实迩。即当胥会，弥积欣怡，辄成小诗三章，代书见意，且答去春之赐》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_494942' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494942' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494942?labeling=true' target='_blank'>去春蒙西都致政李少师<span class='inlineComment2'>（东之）</span>惠诗五首追<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>叙旧游因而招隐某尚羁枢务请退未谐深味来章未知所答迁延宿留遂涉岁时今蒙圣慈俯从人欲听解重柄均逸便藩仰西河之上游瞻仁宅之实迩即当胥会弥积欣怡辄成小诗三章代书见意且答去春之赐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_494942_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494942_1'>① 原脱：据季校本、傅校本补</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494942'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494942'>新诗五首缘招隐，未得西归未敢酬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494942_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494942'>今许均劳解枢柄，期君同伴赤松游<span gray;'>▪</span>作诗三章，答李柬之去春之赐，且约以相访。作品：《去春蒙西都致政李少师柬之惠诗五首，叙旧游，因而招隐。某尚羁枢务，请退未谐……今蒙圣慈俯从人欲，听解重柄，均逸便藩，仰西河之上游，瞻仁宅之实迩，即当胥会，弥积欣怡，辄成小诗三章，代书见意，且答去春之赐3》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_1160214_comment'></div>伏望圣慈体察，早赐牵复知边要州军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160214_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1160214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　举陈州州学教授苏辙差充河阳州学教授。作品：《举苏辙》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此文见《文彦博集校注》卷三八。）</span><div id='poem_1160216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160216?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举苏辙劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁六年六月）</span></a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160216'>臣今复蒙圣慈从欲，均逸便藩，当求时才，助宣邦教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160216_comment'></div>切见权留守推官苏辙博通经术，深知治体，见任陈州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160216_comment'></div>今已岁满，欲望圣慈就差充河阳州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160216_comment'></div>如臣所举不如状，及犯正入己赃，甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_title_494733' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494733?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题史馆兵部傅君草堂<span class='inlineComment2'>（钦之）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_0_494957'>醽渌如渑味似饴<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：沁园之名酝也。）</span>，朝回何必典春衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494957_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_494957_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年11月</a>　被旨赴济源祈雪。作品：《乞免夫役一、二》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《文彦博集校注》卷二二。）</span><div id='poem_1160000' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1160000' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1160000?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免夫役奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（二）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_1160000")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1160000_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1160000'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1160000'>臣检会河阳累据诸县人户陈状：并值夏秋五料灾伤，乞免向去一料春夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1160000_comment'></div>州司体量得人户即日委是大段疲困，以三次奏乞朝廷体念，特免向去一料春夫，及先权住来年一年变修石岸一百步，所贵稍宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1160000_comment'></div>兼臣检会元初擘画改稍木岸作石岸一宗文字，所相度官亦无大段利害，癨且略依上言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1160000_comment'></div>臣僚施行，仍却于顺水不向著归岸，每年变作一百步石岸，显是不至紧急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1160000_comment'></div>所差夫采石，却甚劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1160000_comment'></div>若权住一年，极无妨碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1160000_comment'></div>兼臣于十一月十二日两次被旨赴济源祷雪祈云，所过河阳、济源两县界，以秋末至于冬中，久无雨雪，田畴乾旱，种麦全少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1160000_comment'></div>况此两县在本州稍为富庶，尚乃村落萧然，例有菜色，若不减重役，必不聊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1160000_comment'></div>以臣愚短，固无仁惠可以下苏疲瘵，上宽宵旰，惟是重砯力奏朝廷特赐体念矜恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1160000_comment'></div>伏乞检详本州前后三奏并臣今来劄子，早降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1160000_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1160000_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　游张靖、李章、傅尧俞济上郊园，有诗记之。作品：《游史馆张大卿致政李少卿史馆傅兵部济上郊园》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_494948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游史馆张大卿致政李少卿史馆傅兵部济上郊园<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_494948")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_494948_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_494948_0'>① 张靖、李章、傅尧俞，时判河阳祈雪济源庙作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_494948'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_494948'>畴昔常闻处士庄，林泉胜景甲山阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_494948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_494948'>一渠寒水流清济，千仞浓岚耸太行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_494948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年12月5日</a>　自济源回，得李师锡师，有诗记之。作品：《自济源回及中道得通守郎中诗跂羡山水之游以不得陪从为恨因以诗答之》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494969' id='poem_sentence_4_494969'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_494969_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年</a>　洛下有穷九老会，有诗记之，并寄示王拱辰。作品：前朔宪，孔嗣宗太傅过孟云，近于洛下结穷九老会，凡职事稍重生事稍丰者不得与焉。……》<span class='inlineComment2'>（此诗见《文彦博集校注》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_494960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_494960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/494960?labeling=true' target='_blank'>前朔宪孔嗣宗太博过孟云近于洛下结穷九老会凡职事稍重生事稍丰者不得与焉其宴集之式率称其名其事诚可嘉尚其语多资嗢噱因作小诗以纪之亦以见河南士人有名教之乐简贪薄之风辄录呈留守宣徽聊资解颐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(26200, "北宋", "文彦博", "poem_title_495031")'>文彦博</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_495031_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_495031'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_495031'>使指及门传惠赐，蕲春薤叶水纹寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_495031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_495031'>相君鼎意多兼济，欲使炎天老者安。<div id='poem_sentence_1_495031_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
